![Page cover](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FGV9Otvlt1woUBAYyh36y%252F79699.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfac5bc4c-ae55-445a-9d03-0dd897f8518f&width=1248&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ef458d9c&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool#from-token-launch-to-management-all-in-one-place)

🚀 From Token Launch to Management — All in One Place


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   CiaoTool integrates essential tools such as **one-click token launch**, **bulk transfers**, **cold distribution**, **sniping protection**, and **liquidity control**. From creation and deployment to distribution and permission management, users can execute complex on-chain operations **without writing any code**. Even Web3 newcomers can quickly master token issuance and operations through CiaoTool’s intuitive **visual interface**.
    
*   We care deeply about every user need. New features and integrations are continuously rolled out based on **community feedback**.
    

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool#user-eligibility-and-legal-notice)

🛡️ User Eligibility and Legal Notice


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  This platform strictly complies with local laws and is only accessible to users who meet their jurisdiction’s regulatory requirements.
    
2.  **Users located in mainland China are prohibited** from accessing and using this platform.
    
3.  All users must ensure they comply with their local laws while using the platform. CiaoTool is **not liable for any legal consequences** resulting from user violations.

# Wallet Security Guidelines | CiaoTool

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-security#web3-wallet-private-keys-are-crucial)

🔐 **Web3 Wallet Private Keys Are Crucial**

Once a private key falls into the wrong hands, your assets can be completely drained. However, executing batch operations often requires using the private key, as it is impossible to sign multiple wallets simultaneously without it.

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-security#to-address-such-needs-there-are-two-widely-used-types-of-tool-in-the-market)

To address such needs, there are two widely used types of tool in the market:

1.  **Telegram Bots (TG BOT):** TG BOTs inherently require access to private keys to sign transactions, making them a common choice for batch operations.
    
2.  Another approach involves using certain web-based tools that execute transactions on the backend after obtaining the user’s private key, but this method carries extremely high risk.
    
    *   **Trust:** The platform must be highly trustworthy.
        
    *   **Security:** The platform must have robust measures to protect private keys (e.g., the dexx server hack is a typical risk example).
        
    

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-security#how-does-ciaotool-keep-your-private-keys-safe)

✅ **How Does CiaoTool Keep Your Private Keys Safe?**

CiaoTool uses a **client-side signing mechanism**, meaning your private key is **never uploaded or stored on any server**. All transactions are signed locally within your browser, ensuring that the platform is **technically incapable of accessing or stealing your private key**. For users who perform frequent operations, we also offer an **optional local encrypted storage** feature — balancing convenience with maximum security.

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-security#how-to-ensure-private-keys-are-only-used-for-local-signing)

🛡️ **How to Ensure Private Keys Are Only Used for Local Signing**

Any frontend tool that wants to access a private key must make an HTTPS request to send the key to a backend server. To verify this, you can inspect the tool's network activity:

1.  Open **Chrome Browser**.
    
2.  Right-click and select **Inspect**.
    
3.  Navigate to **Network** -> **Fetch/XHR**.
    
4.  Check if any requests send your private key to the backend (excluding third-party RPC interfaces like Helius for on-chain data).
    

![](https://docs.dogtools.meme/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1231829018-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FbI9FOXIMOA6RLmAW6lRu%252Fuploads%252Fo4l39JAI7EGjKGuAlap0%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfe938640-f827-4d93-bdcd-ea9e50926773&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=67473b61&sv=2)

![](https://docs.dogtools.meme/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1231829018-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FbI9FOXIMOA6RLmAW6lRu%252Fuploads%252FAxjjRJUeSmBNcusHJeBX%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6d9694dd-48d9-436f-bfef-63752dba0b1e&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=125cb9c6&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-security#how-to-operate-private-keys-safely-and-conveniently)

🔐 **How to Operate Private Keys Safely and Conveniently**

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-security#ciaotool-offers-three-methods-for-managing-private-keys)

CiaoTool offers **three methods** for managing private keys:

![](https://docs.dogtools.meme/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1231829018-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FbI9FOXIMOA6RLmAW6lRu%252Fuploads%252F2oA9a8EoIJ2nWxSSqDAp%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df8165f14-1692-4832-8650-3561f5aaa132&width=300&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=bf95d4be&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-security#id-1.-manual-input)

**1\. Manual Input**

![](https://docs.dogtools.meme/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1231829018-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FbI9FOXIMOA6RLmAW6lRu%252Fuploads%252FuGb1vOoQwpMQlOfNFwRq%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D3f6f4fb8-d67a-4ebd-be10-a8a3aeb79ee1&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d6315174&sv=2)

This method requires you to manage your private keys yourself and paste them into an input field. CiaoTool will use your private key for local signing.

**⚠️ Security Precautions** :

*   Prevent malicious clipboard plugins on your computer from stealing your private key.
    
*   Ensure your private key isn’t stored in plain text on your device. Secure your device to prevent theft.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-security#id-2.-import-private-key-file)

**2\. Import Private Key File**

![](https://docs.dogtools.meme/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1231829018-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FbI9FOXIMOA6RLmAW6lRu%252Fuploads%252FkCjGk5RGWKgnxLSIl2um%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D71edfaad-5c27-4bc2-ac76-8b340b2b9c6b&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e1898dc6&sv=2)

CiaoTool supports importing private keys in **Excel**, **CSV**, **JSON**, or **TXT** formats. Compared to manual input, this method improves efficiency.

*   **Instructions**:
    
    *   **For existing wallets:** download the \[template file\] from the top left, paste your private keys into it, and import.
        
    *   **For new wallets:** use the **Multi Sender** feature to create new wallets, perform batch transfers, and export them in one go. Then, import the exported file.
        
    
*   **⚠️ Security Precautions** :
    
    *   Prevent malicious clipboard plugins from stealing your private key.
        
    *   Ensure your private key isn’t stored in plain text on your device. Secure your device to prevent theft.
        
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-security#id-3.-local-encrypted-storage-recommended)

**3\. Local Encrypted Storage (Recommended 👍)**

CiaoTool offers a **local encrypted storage** feature that uses AES encryption. Your private key is encrypted with a password you set (known only to you) and stored locally.

*   **Storage Location**: Chrome Browser -> Right-click -> Inspect -> Application.
    

![](https://docs.dogtools.meme/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1231829018-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FbI9FOXIMOA6RLmAW6lRu%252Fuploads%252FYTrC8jXxUIDjBChDBs8Q%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D213269a2-b35b-425b-822c-b15be6895d1d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=26bfa93d&sv=2)

*   **Advantages**:
    
    *   Compared to manual input or file upload, private keys are not stored in plain text on your device.
        
    *   It allows for easy wallet balance viewing and streamlined batch operations.
        
    
*   **Important Note**:
    
    *   Remember your encryption password. If lost, CiaoTool cannot recover your data. You’ll need to delete local data and start over.
        
    

**Instructions**:

*   **For existing wallets:** After enabling wallet management, click **\[Import Bulk Wallets\]** in the top left and import your private keys. You can then select them directly for batch operations.
    
*   **For new wallets:** After creating new wallets, import them into local wallet management with one click.
    

![](https://docs.dogtools.meme/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1231829018-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FbI9FOXIMOA6RLmAW6lRu%252Fuploads%252FwtVNr9ny6e3FQwdlS4D0%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1a669b22-e2fd-4587-be15-cf8e924fc987&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=713892d&sv=2)

**⚠️Security Precautions** :

*   Be cautious of malicious clipboard plugins when importing private keys into local management.
    
*   Ensure the security of your local device and encryption password.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-security#frequently-asked-questions-faq)

❓ Frequently Asked Questions（FAQ）

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-security#id-1.-how-can-i-keep-my-seed-phrase-secure)

1\. How can I keep my seed phrase secure?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Write it down with pen and paper and store it offline. Never save it as a screenshot, in cloud notes, or chat history.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-security#id-2.-why-shouldnt-i-save-my-wallet-using-screenshots)

2\. Why shouldn't I save my wallet using screenshots?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Screenshots can be accessed by malware or synced to the cloud, posing serious security risks.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-security#id-3.-will-clearing-my-browser-cache-affect-my-wallet)

3\. Will clearing my browser cache affect my wallet?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** No. Non-custodial wallet private keys are not stored in browser cache, but make sure you have backed up your seed phrase beforehand.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-security#id-4.-what-are-the-risks-of-using-browser-extension-wallets)

4\. What are the risks of using browser extension wallets?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Extension wallets can be exploited by fake websites or malicious approvals — always double-check every interaction and signature.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-security#id-5.-how-do-i-know-if-an-airdrop-or-link-is-safe)

5\. How do I know if an airdrop or link is safe?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Avoid clicking on unknown links or approving suspicious transactions — especially those claiming “free airdrops.”

# Before Token Launch: How Should Token Liquidity Be Allocated? | CiaoTool

circle-check

**Solana Create Token：**[https://ciaotool.io/zh-CN/token/createarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/zh-CN/token/create)

**Pump：**[https://ciaotool.io/zh-CN/pump/launch-and-buyarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/zh-CN/pump/launch-and-buy)

**Bonk：**[https://ciaotool.io/zh-CN/letsbonkZone/bundled-buyarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/zh-CN/letsbonkZone/bundled-buy)

circle-check

**BSC Create Token：**[https://bsc.ciaotool.io/token/create-tokenarrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/token/create-token)

**Fourmeme：**[https://bsc.ciaotool.io/fourmeme/bnb/create-and-buyarrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/fourmeme/bnb/create-and-buy)

**Flap：**[https://bsc.ciaotool.io/flap/usd1/create-and-buyarrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/flap/usd1/create-and-buy)

circle-check

**Base Create Token：**[https://base.ciaotool.io/token/create-tokenarrow-up-right](https://base.ciaotool.io/token/create-token)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/liquidity-configuration#why-is-liquidity-so-important)

🔑 Why Is Liquidity So Important?

*   **Trading Smoothness**: Liquidity directly affects slippage. The lower the liquidity, the greater the price impact of a single trade, resulting in a less smooth trading experience.
    
*   **Price Stability**: Higher liquidity can better absorb buy and sell pressure, improving price stability, but it also comes with higher capital lock-up costs.
    
*   **Manipulation Risk & Fit**: When liquidity is insufficient, pools become easier to manipulate. However, more liquidity is not always better—excessive liquidity can increase potential impermanent loss. The key is whether the liquidity configuration matches the project’s current stage.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/liquidity-configuration#first-define-your-liquidity-tier)

📊 First, Define Your Liquidity Tier

Regardless of which blockchain you launch on, you should first identify your project’s liquidity tier. This choice directly affects investor perception and price behavior.

*   **Very Low Liquidity**: Experimental projects or low-budget memes; high slippage and extremely vulnerable to bots.
    
*   **Low Liquidity**: Early-stage projects with a small community; price stability is still limited.
    
*   **Moderate Liquidity**: Projects with a growing user base and regular trading activity; prices are more controlled.
    
*   **High Liquidity**: Mature-stage projects; market confidence improves significantly.
    
*   **Very High Liquidity**: Well-funded or proven projects; manipulation becomes difficult.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/liquidity-configuration#liquidity-reference-ranges-by-blockchain)

🔗 Liquidity Reference Ranges by Blockchain

The table below summarizes commonly observed liquidity ranges based on real market conditions. These are **reference benchmarks**, not strict rules.

Liquidity Tier

SOL (Raydium)

SOL (PumpSwap)

BSC (BNB)

Base

Very Low

1 – 100 SOL

1 – 25 SOL

0.15 – 15 BNB

0.1 – 5 WETH

26 – 125 SOL

6 – 25 WETH

501 – 2,000 SOL

126 – 500 SOL

75 – 300 BNB

2,001 – 10,000 SOL

501 – 2,500 SOL

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252F6YLTtIJTDr0AhxOybYP3%252F79699.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D61ed9f51-35f1-4c7b-919e-c4d27a4bd4fd&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=bb25c37d&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/liquidity-configuration#what-problems-does-insufficient-liquidity-cause)

⚠️ What Problems Does Insufficient Liquidity Cause?

*   **Impact of Insufficient Liquidity**: When liquidity is low, slippage increases significantly, directly degrading the trading experience. At the same time, liquidity pools become more vulnerable to bot front-running and pump-and-dump attacks, raising overall market risk.
    
*   **The Need for Active Liquidity Management**: While increasing liquidity can help mitigate these issues to some extent, impermanent loss must still be considered—especially during periods of high price volatility. Therefore, liquidity should be managed dynamically rather than deployed as a one-time allocation.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/liquidity-configuration#should-you-allocate-100-of-tokens-to-the-liquidity-pool)

🔎 Should You Allocate 100% of Tokens to the Liquidity Pool?

*   Generally, no. A healthier approach is to allocate **40%–70%** of the total token supply to liquidity, while reserving the remainder for **staking incentives, ecosystem rewards, community growth, or future airdrops**.
    
*   This structure ensures sufficient market depth while preserving long-term flexibility for the project.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FWh9C92NlDq23PXzBgdxE%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D70abd2d1-f248-489a-9c89-32f4a5fb279f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ed83faef&sv=2)

*   Liquidity is core infrastructure for any token. Although specific ranges vary across blockchains, the underlying principle remains the same:
    

> **Adequate liquidity = more stable prices + stronger market confidence + lower manipulation risk**

Carefully planning your liquidity tier and token allocation is one of the most important steps to avoid failing at the very beginning.

# Solana Token Creation Tutorial | CiaoTool

circle-check

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/create#solana-create-token-https-ciaotool.io-en-us-token-create)

Solana Create Token：[https://ciaotool.io/en-US/token/createarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/en-US/token/create)



---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

circle-exclamation

If you prefer learning through videos, feel free to watch this tutorial.

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/create#how-to-create-a-token-on-solana)

🪙 **How to Create a Token on Solana**

1.  **Open the Solana One-Click Token Creation** interface: [https://ciaotool.io/en-US/token/createarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/en-US/token/create)
    
2.  **Fill in Basic Information：**The token **decimals** define how small the token can be divided. The maximum precision for SPL tokens is **9**, with common settings being **6** (for utility tokens) and **9** (for high-precision applications).
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FKTbHfxZDpph3EuDolsU8%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da4e1a1e1-5db6-4dce-bd65-9eca5b231249&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6c46b5ea&sv=2)

1.  **(Optional) Add Contact Information**
    

If you want users to join your community or learn more about your project, this is the most direct way to provide that information.

![](https://docs.dogtools.meme/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1231829018-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FbI9FOXIMOA6RLmAW6lRu%252Fuploads%252FDtDEcGy4wucGTAbUjw6O%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D886032f3-044c-4771-9e01-e0e3438306ca&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=61433598&sv=2)

1.  **Custom Contract Address:** Create a personalized token address and stand out from the start — **all for just 0.01 SOL.**
    

*   In the tool, select the “Import Private Key” option;
    
*   Paste your pre-generated private key (make sure to store it securely);
    
*   The system will deploy your token from this address, ensuring the contract address matches your expectations.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252F3JY3dfcRL4kNwKUn1Rxd%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4d9e7e32-3a8b-43d2-b838-81e2ab39d122&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=12767dd2&sv=2)

1.  **(Optional) Set Permissions**
    

*   Generally, for tokens that need to be added to **Raydium**, it is recommended to **revoke the freeze and mint permissions**.
    
*   The metadata update permission can be chosen at your discretion.
    
*   If the metadata update permission is revoked, the **token name and logo** can no longer be updated.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252F4yeE69wMipnjFeiWFiRb%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4e075cac-f841-491f-b9dc-36e2814f2324&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ceec98b8&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/create#token-creation-transaction-process)

🔁 **Token Creation Transaction Process**

*   When the process starts, a **log popup** will appear to update you on the progress in real time.
    
*   Once the transaction is successful, you will receive **transaction and token links**, which you can click to view directly.
    

![](https://docs.dogtools.meme/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1231829018-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FbI9FOXIMOA6RLmAW6lRu%252Fuploads%252FbX1Xk530gARy7TfZsV0w%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D35fa2967-8bc0-46c9-a17c-911effa622d3&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=fad18960&sv=2)

*   If anything goes wrong during the process, we will provide **clear feedback** on the issue, **No fees** will be charged for failed transactions.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/create#frequently-asked-questions-faq)

❓ Frequently Asked Questions（FAQ）

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/create#id-1.-what-wallet-do-i-need-to-create-a-token)

1\. What wallet do I need to create a token?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** We recommend using Solana-compatible browser extension wallets such as **Phantom** or **Backpack**, and ensuring the wallet is properly connected.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/create#id-2.-how-much-sol-is-required-for-one-click-token-creation)

2\. How much SOL is required for one-click token creation?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Typically around **0.1–0.3 SOL** is needed to create the token account and complete the initialization transaction (may vary slightly based on network congestion).
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/create#id-3.-why-is-nothing-happening-after-i-click-create)

3\. Why is nothing happening after I click "Create"?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Please check if your wallet is prompting for a signature. If not, try refreshing the page and reconnecting your wallet.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/create#id-4.-where-can-i-view-my-token-after-its-created)

4\. Where can I view my token after it's created?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** You can view the token details on a Solana block explorer such as **Solscan** by entering the token address, or import the token into your wallet to display it.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/create#id-5.-can-i-change-the-token-name-or-symbol-after-creation)

5\. Can I change the token name or symbol after creation?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Yes, **SPL tokens** allow you to modify the name and symbol even after the token has been created.

# The Beginner Guide to Token Creation | CiaoTool

*   The blockchain world can look complicated: tons of jargon, different chains, fee mechanisms, permission settings…
    
*   But in reality, creating a token isn’t mysterious at all. With smart one-click token-creation platforms like CiaoTool, you don’t need to write any code or stress about security and deployment. In just a few minutes, your token can be ready.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/basic-guide#part-1-preparations-and-basic-concepts-before-creating-a-token)

🧩 **Part 1: Preparations and Basic Concepts Before Creating a Token**

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/basic-guide#what-is-creating-a-token)

🔹 **What is “creating a token”?**

*   **Creating token** means deploying a token contract on an existing blockchain. You define its name, symbol, total supply, and functions — in short, you are its creator.
    

> **Example:** Bitcoin is an independent blockchain (produced through mining), whereas what you’re creating is a “token” deployed on an existing blockchain, such as generating your own token on BSC or Solana.

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/basic-guide#choosing-a-blockchain-where-to-launch-your-token)

🔹 **Choosing a Blockchain: Where to Launch Your Token?**

circle-info

Different blockchains have varying rules and costs, so this is something you should plan ahead. BSC and Solana are currently among the most popular choices.

*   The mainstream options are as follows:
    

Blockchain

Features

Suitable For

BSC (Binance Smart Chain)

Mature and stable, low transaction costs

Beginners / project teams

Solana

Fast, active ecosystem

Users creating Meme or light projects

Base / X Layer / IoTeX

Emerging chains, flexible operations

Developers exploring new ecosystems

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FZUxKuEHs2EGjWMsVLi5F%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D45cead28-7e14-4795-9073-a9d1d4f8b1b0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b5d78269&sv=2)

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/basic-guide#how-to-create-a-token)

🔹 **How to Create a Token?**

Normally, issuing a token requires a developer to write a smart contract and deploy it on the blockchain. But if you’re not technical, you can skip the coding step entirely by using a one-click token creation tool like **CiaoTool**. By paying a small service fee, you can have your own token ready in just a few minutes.

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/basic-guide#how-much-does-it-cost-to-create-a-token)

🔹 **How Much Does It Cost to Create a Token?**

The cost varies depending on the blockchain and is generally paid in the chain’s native token. You can check the official pages for real-time fees:

*   **Solana** ➜ Paid in SOL, fees: [https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/pricearrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/price)
    
*   **BSC** ➜ Paid in BNB, fees: [https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/bsc/pricearrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/bsc/price)
    
*   **Base** ➜ Paid in ETH，fees: [https://base.ciaotool.io/arrow-up-right](https://base.ciaotool.io/)
    
*   **IoTeX** ➜ Paid in IOTX，fees: [https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/iotex/pricearrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/iotex/price)
    
*   **OKX Chain**（X Layer) ➜ Paid in OKB，fees: [https://xlayer.ciaarrow-up-right](https://xlayer.ciaotool.io/)
    

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/basic-guide#what-can-you-do-after-creating-a-token)

🔹 **What Can You Do After Creating a Token?**

You can:

*   Transfer or airdrop it to others
    
*   Create a liquidity pool for trading
    
*   Track your token’s market data on DEX platforms
    

⚠️ **Note:** To enable **trading**, assign a **price**, and have your token appear on platforms like **GMGN** and **DexScreener**, you must create a **liquidity pool**.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/basic-guide#launch-vs.-one-click-token-creation)

🔹 **Launch vs. One-Click Token Creation**

Type

Features

Note

Launch

No liquidity pool, tokens must be purchased, limited control by the project team

Suitable for lightweight applications

One-Click Token Creation

Tokens are received directly, liquidity can be added independently, functions are configurable

The project team has full control over the token logic

> CiaoTool supports both modes: you can either use the **one-click token creation** feature or connect to internal platforms like PumpFun, BonkFun, Fourmeme, and Flap to create and purchase tokens within their ecosystems.

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/basic-guide#token-creation-prep-checklist)

⚙️ **Token Creation Prep Checklist**

Tools

Purpose

Computer / Phone

Using a computer is recommended for more stable and convenient operations

VPN or internet access tool

Access on-chain resources and tutorials

Wallet (MetaMask / Phantom / OKX)

Store blockchain assets

Assets Preparation

Have BNB, SOL, or other tokens ready to pay gas fees in your wallet

Telegram

Join the official CiaoTool Telegram group for support: [https://t.me/ciaotoolarrow-up-right](https://t.me/ciaotool)

circle-exclamation

*   Don’t know how to use a wallet ❌ Not recommended to create a token
    
*   Wallet has no funds ❌ Not recommended to create a token
    
*   Don’t understand basic concepts ❌ Not recommended to create a token
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/basic-guide#part-2-practical-guide-to-creating-a-token)

💥 **Part 2: Practical Guide to Creating a Token**

Ready? In this section, we dive into hands-on steps! Whether you’re making a community token, a Meme coin, or an experimental project, the process is largely the same.

1

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/basic-guide#fill-in-basic-information)

Fill in Basic Information

Parameters and recommendations:

*   **Name:** Full token name, can be in Chinese or English. Example: SolDog
    
*   **Symbol:** Short code, usually 3–5 letters. Example: DOG, MEOW
    
*   **Supply:** Maximum token amount, recommended as an integer (no decimals)
    
*   **Decimals:** Smallest divisible unit, default 6 or 9
    
*   **Logo:** Supported on Solana; for other chains, uploads may not display. (On Solana, you can replace freely; for other chains, contact official support)
    

2

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/basic-guide#optional-feature-configuration)

Optional Feature Configuration

Features and suitable users:

*   **Burn:** Destroy part of the tokens to increase scarcity. Suitable for deflationary projects
    
*   **Blacklist:** Freeze specific addresses to prevent malicious wallets
    
*   **Mint:** Dynamically increase supply, mainly for testing purposes
    
*   **Standard Token:** No special permissions, recommended for beginners, fully green in safety checks
    

> Beginners are recommended to create a **Standard Token** — simplest functionality, highest security, and most friendly for risk-control checks.

3

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/basic-guide#choose-a-blockchain)

Choose a Blockchain

*   **EVM-based chains (BSC / Base / X Layer):** Powerful features, high compatibility, slightly higher cost
    
*   **Solana:** Fast, logo displays nicely, simpler functionality
    

4

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/basic-guide#payment-and-creation)

**Payment and Creation**

After confirming all parameters, the system will prompt you to pay the token creation fee. Once paid, the token will be automatically generated and sent to your connected wallet.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/basic-guide#part-3-managing-and-maintaining-your-token)

💼 **Part 3: Managing and Maintaining Your Token**

Congratulations! You now officially own your token. But the next crucial step is how to operate and maintain your token ecosystem.

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/basic-guide#quick-faq-and-liquidity-pool-faq)

💡 **Quick FAQ and** Liquidity Pool FAQ

chevron-right**Q1：Where is my token? Why doesn’t it show in my wallet?**[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/basic-guide#q1-where-is-my-token-why-doesnt-it-show-in-my-wallet)

All tokens are in the wallet you connected. If it doesn’t appear, manually add the token address.

chevron-right**Q2：How can I trade it?**[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/basic-guide#q2-how-can-i-trade-it)

Create a liquidity pool, for example:

*   **BSC:** PancakeSwap → [https://pancakeswap.finance/liquidity/poolsarrow-up-right](https://pancakeswap.finance/liquidity/pools)
    ?
    
*   **Solana:** Raydium → [https://raydium.io/liquidity-pools/arrow-up-right](https://raydium.io/liquidity-pools/)
    
*   **Base:** PancakeSwap → [https://pancakeswap.finance/liquidity/poolsarrow-up-right](https://pancakeswap.finance/liquidity/pools)
    ?
    
*   **X Layer:** PotatoSwap → [https://potatoswap.finance/swaparrow-up-right](https://potatoswap.finance/swap)
    

chevron-right**Q3: How is the token price determined?**[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/basic-guide#q3-how-is-the-token-price-determined)

Price = ratio of the two assets in the liquidity pool. For example: 100 USDT + 100 TOKEN → initial price 1 USDT/TOKEN

chevron-rightQ4：Why does risk detection show red?[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/basic-guide#q4-why-does-risk-detection-show-red)

Adding features like “Mint” or “Blacklist” flags high risk in checks. It’s recommended to use a **Standard Token** to keep the green status.

chevron-rightQ5：If someone buys my token, where does the money go?[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/basic-guide#q5-if-someone-buys-my-token-where-does-the-money-go)

The purchase funds go into the liquidity pool. To withdraw earnings, use the “Remove Liquidity” function.

chevron-rightQ6: Who can create a liquidity pool?[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/basic-guide#q6-who-can-create-a-liquidity-pool)

Anyone with tokens and assets can create one.

chevron-right**Q7: How much should I invest in the pool?**[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/basic-guide#q7-how-much-should-i-invest-in-the-pool)

There’s no fixed minimum; even a few dozen USD can work.

chevron-right**Q8: Can the pool’s tokens be completely bought out?**[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/basic-guide#q8-can-the-pools-tokens-be-completely-bought-out)

In theory, no. The price will rise gradually as demand increases, approaching but never reaching zero.

chevron-right**Q9: How can I stabilize the token price?**[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/basic-guide#q9-how-can-i-stabilize-the-token-price)

Using CLMM (Concentrated Liquidity Market Maker) or adding single-token liquidity can help make the price more stable.

chevron-right**Q10: Does Solana require a Market ID?**[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/basic-guide#q10-does-solana-require-a-market-id)

Only in AMM mode is creating a Market ID necessary.

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/basic-guide#part-4-recommended-tools-after-creating-a-token)

✅ With CiaoTool, creating a token no longer requires coding or running a node. As long as you have your wallet and assets ready, you can complete the full cycle from **“Idea → Token → Market.”**

> 🚀 The barrier to creating a token is getting lower, but the barrier to managing it is getting higher. The real competition isn’t about “who launches first,” but “who can operate it best.” May your first token on-chain become your key to the Web3 world.

# Solana Mint Token Tutorial | CiaoTool

circle-check

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/mint#solana-mint-token-https-ciaotool.io-en-us-token-mint)

Solana Mint Token：[https://ciaotool.io/en-US/token/mintarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/en-US/token/mint)



---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/mint#how-to-mint-token-on-solana)

🔓 **How to Mint Token on Solana**


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  You can access the minting feature directly from the **Token Management** page. If you have the necessary minting permissions and have not renounced them, a **Mint** button will be displayed.
    
2.  You can go directly to the **Token Minting** page, select a token or enter the token address to search. If the **Mint Authority** is still active, you can proceed with minting. Simply enter the desired amount and click the **Mint** button.
    

![](https://docs.dogtools.meme/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1231829018-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FbI9FOXIMOA6RLmAW6lRu%252Fuploads%252FDWx0u0qq0ggslaHt0lLR%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2539c5f7-b2c0-4ffd-8e9a-00577824d410&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=d7170cce&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/mint#minting-transaction-process)

🔁 **Minting Transaction Process**


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Once the task begins, a log popup will appear to provide real-time updates on the transaction progress.
    

![](https://docs.dogtools.meme/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1231829018-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FbI9FOXIMOA6RLmAW6lRu%252Fuploads%252FOaO8BhCCuK12l6VROIpv%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7f1dcc1e-3374-404b-acf3-772b5ece5c20&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e7c6dfc0&sv=2)

*   If any issue arises during the process, we will clearly indicate the problem. **No fees will be charged for failed transactions.**
    

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/mint#frequently-asked-questions)

❓ Frequently Asked Questions

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/mint#id-1.-can-token-permissions-be-restored-after-revocation)

1\. Can token permissions be restored after revocation?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** No. Once permissions are revoked, the action is **permanent and cannot be undone**.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/mint#id-2.-why-should-i-revoke-token-permissions)

2\. Why should I revoke token permissions?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Revoking permissions **increases project transparency**, strengthens community trust, and attracts more investors.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/mint#id-3.-is-the-revocation-process-complicated)

3\. Is the revocation process complicated?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Not at all. With **CiaoTool**, it’s a **one-click operation** — no coding required.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/mint#id-4.-which-permissions-are-most-important-to-revoke)

4\. Which permissions are most important to revoke?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Typically, the **Mint** (minting) and **Freeze** (account freezing) permissions are key to ensuring supply integrity and operational safety.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/mint#id-5.-will-revoking-permissions-affect-token-trading)

5\. Will revoking permissions affect token trading?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** No. **Regular transfers and trading** of the token will remain unaffected.

# Solana Burn Token Tutorial | CiaoTool

circle-check

**Solana Burn Token：**[https://ciaotool.io/en-US/token/burnarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/en-US/token/burn)

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/burn#how-to-burn-token-on-solana)

🔥 **How to Burn Token on Solana**


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  You can navigate from the **Token Management** page (if you have a token balance, the **Burn** button will be displayed).
    
2.  Go directly to the **Burn Token** page, select the token you want to burn, enter the burn amount, and click the action button below.
    

![](https://docs.dogtools.meme/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1231829018-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FbI9FOXIMOA6RLmAW6lRu%252Fuploads%252FQlH3SUug1SuIf051znwU%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D904b04d9-3ba2-43c9-bcac-65026a822135&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=fae3ace7&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/burn#token-burn-transaction-process)

⛓️ **Token Burn Transaction Process**


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   When the task starts, a log popup will appear to update you on the transaction progress in real-time.
    
*   Once the task begins, a log popup will appear to provide real-time updates on the transaction progress. (A single transaction signature is required.)
    

![](https://docs.dogtools.meme/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1231829018-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FbI9FOXIMOA6RLmAW6lRu%252Fuploads%252FOaO8BhCCuK12l6VROIpv%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7f1dcc1e-3374-404b-acf3-772b5ece5c20&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e7c6dfc0&sv=2)

*   If any issue arises during the process, we will clearly indicate the problem. **No fees will be charged for failed transactions.**
    

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/burn#frequently-asked-questions)

❓ Frequently Asked Questions

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/burn#id-1.-what-is-token-burning)

1\. What is token burning?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Token burning refers to **permanently destroying** a certain amount of tokens to reduce the circulating supply.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/burn#id-2.-how-does-burning-tokens-impact-a-project)

2\. How does burning tokens impact a project?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Burning increases **token scarcity**, which can boost market confidence and perceived project value.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/burn#id-3.-can-a-burn-operation-be-reversed)

3\. Can a burn operation be reversed?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** **No**, once burned, tokens are **permanently removed** and cannot be recovered.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/burn#id-4.-how-do-i-burn-tokens-using-ciaotool)

4\. How do I burn tokens using CiaoTool?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Use the **Token Management** feature, enter the burn amount, and **sign the transaction** to complete the process.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/burn#id-5.-does-burning-tokens-incur-a-fee)

5\. Does burning tokens incur a fee?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Yes, burning tokens incurs a **standard on-chain transaction fee**.

# Solana Freeze Account Tutorial | CiaoTool

circle-check

**Solana Freeze Account：**[https://ciaotool.io/en-US/token/freeze-accountarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/en-US/token/freeze-account)

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/freeze#how-to-freeze-account-on-solana)

🧊 **How to Freeze Account on Solana**


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  You can navigate from the **Token Management** page (if you have freeze permissions and have not revoked them, the **Freeze** button will be displayed).
    
2.  Go directly to the **Freeze Account** page, select the token to operate on, enter the wallet address you want to freeze, and click the action button below.
    

![](https://docs.dogtools.meme/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1231829018-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FbI9FOXIMOA6RLmAW6lRu%252Fuploads%252Fat5iZ1eENyuVJoqzbkDV%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2513b46a-8bd0-4f1c-ac9d-ea8241b4eafa&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c4e1a410&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/freeze#freeze-account-transaction-process)

⛓️ **Freeze Account Transaction Process**


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   When the task starts, a log popup will appear to update you on the transaction progress in real-time.
    
*   Once the task begins, a log popup will appear to provide real-time updates on the transaction progress. (A single transaction signature is required.)
    

![](https://docs.dogtools.meme/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1231829018-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FbI9FOXIMOA6RLmAW6lRu%252Fuploads%252FOaO8BhCCuK12l6VROIpv%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7f1dcc1e-3374-404b-acf3-772b5ece5c20&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e7c6dfc0&sv=2)

*   If any issue arises during the process, we will clearly indicate the problem. **No fees will be charged for failed transactions.**
    

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/freeze#frequently-asked-questions)

❓ Frequently Asked Questions

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/freeze#id-1.-what-is-the-account-freezing-feature)

1\. What is the account freezing feature?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Freezing an account means temporarily restricting a wallet’s ability to **transfer or trade** specific tokens.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/freeze#id-2.-who-has-the-authority-to-freeze-an-account)

2\. Who has the authority to freeze an account?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Only accounts with the token's **Freeze authority** can perform freezing operations.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/freeze#id-3.-can-a-frozen-account-still-receive-tokens)

3\. Can a frozen account still receive tokens?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Yes, freezing only restricts **sending and trading**; receiving tokens is still allowed.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/freeze#id-4.-how-can-i-unfreeze-a-frozen-account)

4\. How can I unfreeze a frozen account?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** An account with **Freeze authority** can initiate the unfreeze operation at any time.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/freeze#id-5.-does-freezing-an-account-affect-overall-token-circulation)

5\. Does freezing an account affect overall token circulation?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** No, it only affects the **specific frozen wallet**, not the overall circulation of the token.

# Solana Token Management Tutorial | CiaoTool

circle-check

**Solana Token Management：**[https://ciaotool.io/en-US/token/managementarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/en-US/token/management)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/sol#tokens-are-categorized-into-the-following-four-types)

Tokens are categorized into the following **four types**:

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/sol#standard-tokens)

💰 **Standard Tokens：**

The most common type of SPL token, used for standard transfers and transactions.

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FFx4pMZnggIpCb9OaScI2%252F4.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De23b776d-435a-42ca-9888-3bc27760b4da&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fcb5e20f&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/sol#pump-tokens)

🎯 **Pump Tokens：**

Tokens created via Pump. You can perform token burning operations.

![](https://docs.dogtools.meme/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1231829018-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FbI9FOXIMOA6RLmAW6lRu%252Fuploads%252Fnl8J2OhK4BGlU5jldNrG%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D20a65685-dd94-453e-a706-b68370c4b556&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=9d11c578&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/sol#nft-tokens)

🖼️ **NFT Tokens：**

Displays the list of NFT tokens you own.

![](https://docs.dogtools.meme/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1231829018-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FbI9FOXIMOA6RLmAW6lRu%252Fuploads%252FAm0AerJnAHnQ5keeMfjt%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db2c4843b-1b31-4217-a835-5da14364070d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=541ff03e&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/sol#stable-tokens)

💵 **Stable Tokens：**

Displays the balance of USDT and USDC.

![](https://docs.dogtools.meme/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1231829018-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FbI9FOXIMOA6RLmAW6lRu%252Fuploads%252FjbDReAXof54KdV8qeVI3%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D0b70a9b7-6c78-4ec6-897e-af246eb11678&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e40a4ae9&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/sol#frequently-asked-questions)

❓ Frequently Asked Questions

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/sol#id-1.-can-i-change-the-total-supply-of-a-standard-token)

1\. Can I change the total supply of a standard token?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Yes, if you’ve retained the **Mint authority**, you can increase or reduce the supply through minting or burning; otherwise, the supply cannot be changed.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/sol#id-2.-do-i-have-to-revoke-permissions-for-pump-tokens)

2\. Do I have to revoke permissions for Pump tokens?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** It's strongly recommended to **revoke permissions early** to avoid concerns about potential minting or freezing, and to build community trust.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/sol#id-3.-whats-the-core-difference-between-nfts-and-regular-tokens)

3\. What’s the core difference between NFTs and regular tokens?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** **NFTs are unique, non-fungible assets** (usually based on the Metaplex standard), while standard tokens are **fungible and divisible**.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/sol#id-4.-how-do-stablecoins-maintain-price-stability)

4\. How do stablecoins maintain price stability?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Stablecoins typically rely on **reserves, pegging mechanisms,** or **algorithms** to maintain a 1:1 ratio with fiat currencies like USD.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/sol#id-5.-can-pump-tokens-or-nfts-be-managed-as-standard-tokens)

5\. Can Pump tokens or NFTs be managed as standard tokens?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Not recommended. NFTs and some Pump tokens have **different structures**, and their **permission controls and trading behavior** may not follow standard token rules.

# How to Create Liquidity on Raydium？ | CiaoTool

circle-check

**Create Raydium Liquidity:** [https://raydium.io/liquidity-pools/arrow-up-right](https://raydium.io/liquidity-pools/)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/create-liquidity#what-is-raydium)

🌊 What Is Raydium?

*   Raydium is an **Automated Market Maker (AMM)** built on the **Solana blockchain**. It leverages a **central limit order book** to enable lightning-fast trades, shared liquidity, and new yield-generating opportunities.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/create-liquidity#raydium-pool-types-explained-cpmm-clmm-ammv4)

🧩 Raydium Pool Types Explained: CPMM / CLMM / AMMv4

Below is a comparison of the three common pool types on Raydium and their typical use cases.

Type

Model & Features

Advantages

Best Use Case

⚙️ **CPMM (Constant Product AMM)**

Uses the (x \* y = k) model

Supports Token-2022, multiple fee tiers, stable capital efficiency

General trading pairs, first-time pool creation

🏛️ **AMMv4 (Legacy AMM)**

Raydium’s historical AMM version

Mature, stable, compatible with OpenBook

Legacy projects, users requiring backward compatibility

🎯 **CLMM (Concentrated Liquidity)**

LPs define price ranges for liquidity

Deeper liquidity, lower slippage, flexible yield

Advanced LPs, market makers, strategy-driven users

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/create-liquidity#how-to-add-liquidity-on-raydium-create-a-pool)

🛠️ How to Add Liquidity on Raydium (Create a Pool)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/create-liquidity#id-1-connect-your-wallet)

1️⃣ Connect Your Wallet

Open Raydium [(Liquidity page)arrow-up-right](https://raydium.io/liquidity-pools/)
 and click **Connect Wallet** to connect your Solana wallet (e.g. Phantom).

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FY7RRttarmU1HsPYoWjIB%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D817c15cd-f38c-4b7a-b787-71ce029fea28&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4ec870bc&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/create-liquidity#id-2-go-to-pool-creation)

2️⃣ Go to Pool Creation

Navigate to **Liquidity → Create**.

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252F82VFi1V05c0g3lW1Awx3%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D22cb4eff-0f51-4c16-9281-54c66f135777&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e4f6b5bb&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/create-liquidity#id-3-choose-pool-type)

3️⃣ Choose Pool Type

You can select one of the following:

*   **CPMM (Standard AMM)**
    
*   **CLMM (Concentrated Liquidity)**
    
*   **AMMv4 (Legacy AMM)**
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FgtNJkauJOGRKeqIc95ja%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De6859dcf-45db-4b19-b885-446abe13e5a2&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1b8e4c0f&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/create-liquidity#id-4-configure-pool-parameters-clmm-example)

4️⃣ Configure Pool Parameters (CLMM Example)

**1.Select Base & Quote Tokens**

*   The **base token** is the first token displayed in the trading pair.
    
*   The **quote token** is the token used to price the base token.
    

circle-info

For example, the quote token represents how much of it is required to buy **1 unit of the base token**. Common quote tokens include **SOL, USDC, or other stablecoins**.

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FPs2S0eXxgiU20VxeUgwJ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dabeeada0-68bf-408d-9751-7e696eca8c2e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8014ded5&sv=2)

**2.Select Fee Tier**

The selected fee is paid by traders. Liquidity providers receive:

*   **100% of token emission rewards**
    
*   **84% of trading fees**, while:
    
    *   **12%** goes to RAY buybacks
        
    *   **4%** goes to the project treasury
        
    

**Available fee tiers (selectable by pool creator):**

*   **0.01%** – Very stable assets
    
*   **0.05%** – Pegged assets and high-volume pairs
    
*   **0.25%** – Most token pairs
    
*   **1%** – Exotic or highly volatile pairs
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252Fmfusv80dY3NryBEV1koL%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd81fd204-568b-4aff-b091-7c4ddcec4b7e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=961341f6&sv=2)

**3.Set Initial Price**

The **initial price** defines how much quote token is required to purchase **1 base token** at pool creation.

The pool creator may view the price in either base token or quote token terms.

circle-exclamation

Once the pool is confirmed and initialized, the **initial price, fee tier, and initial liquidity cannot be edited**. However, the pool creator can add additional liquidity within any chosen price range at a later time.

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252Flc5orqAB7g7RhyovcM6f%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dd945b863-ddea-43e5-9fa3-e51d5516ad17&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ee2f7e88&sv=2)

**4.Choose Position Price Range**

When selecting the initial price range, you are only defining **your first liquidity position**.

After the pool is created:

*   Other users may add liquidity at **any price range**
    
*   You can withdraw or create new positions at any time
    

circle-info

By default, the system suggests a range of **±50% around the initial price**, but you may customize it.

**In CLMM:**

*   If the market price **falls below your lower bound**, your position becomes **100% base token** (accumulating at lower prices)
    
*   If the market price **exceeds your upper bound**, your position becomes **100% quote token** (selling at higher prices)
    

circle-info

This differs from **CPMM**, where liquidity is distributed automatically across the entire price range (from 0 to ∞).

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FlUhp9dHrLmGAJmlMhMFJ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8012d1b4-fb76-4494-9a4e-b912661b3683&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d8775dfc&sv=2)

**5.Deposit Amount**

*   The deposit amount represents the quantity of base and quote tokens used to initialize the pool.
    
*   Based on your previous settings, the system will automatically calculate the deposit ratio. The pool creator may manually adjust the amount of base and quote tokens.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FCDFL4urZmT9Wd16ZbEpK%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D86b77f96-d07d-482d-ad04-93e83f532868&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5fdb72ad&sv=2)

**6.Preview & Confirm**

*   After setting the deposit amount, preview the pool configuration.
    
*   Click **Confirm Deposit** and approve the transaction.
    
*   🎉 Congratulations! You have successfully created a **concentrated liquidity pool on Raydium**.
    

circle-exclamation

Due to pool initialization, **network gas fees will be higher than usual**

Once the transaction is approved and the pool is live:

1.  The initial price and initial liquidity **cannot be modified**
    
2.  The pool creator may still manage positions or add liquidity within any preferred price range
    

* * *

chevron-rightWhat Are the Benefits of Providing Liquidity in Raydium Traditional AMM Pools (CPMM)?[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/create-liquidity#what-are-the-benefits-of-providing-liquidity-in-raydium-traditional-amm-pools-cpmm)

**Earn Trading Fee Revenue：**A **0.25% trading fee** is charged on swaps within the pool, of which:

*   **0.22%** is distributed to the LP pool
    
*   **0.03%** is allocated to the **RAY single-sided staking pool**
    

**Earn OpenBook Market-Making Revenue：**

*   Raydium AMM automatically provides liquidity on the **OpenBook order book**.
    
*   Market-making revenue generated on OpenBook is distributed proportionally to liquidity providers.
    

**Receive LP Tokens as Proof of Liquidity：**After adding liquidity, you will receive **LP tokens** representing your share of the pool.

**Example:** Deposit **RAY + USDC** → receive **RAY-USDC LP**

As trading occurs, fees accumulate in the pool, and the **value of LP tokens increases accordingly**.

chevron-rightWhat Are LP Tokens?[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/create-liquidity#what-are-lp-tokens)

LP tokens represent your **proportional ownership** of assets in a liquidity pool.

**Example:** Add liquidity to the **SOL-RAY** pool → receive **SOL-RAY LP**

You may redeem LP tokens at any time to withdraw your corresponding share of the pool’s assets.

chevron-rightWhat Are Ecosystem Farms?[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/create-liquidity#what-are-ecosystem-farms)

*   **Ecosystem Farms** are a new type of **permissionless farming mechanism** designed for Raydium traditional AMM pools.
    
*   Any project team or user can create a farm to distribute rewards for a specific pool, further enhancing liquidity across the Solana ecosystem.
    

chevron-rightWhat Are the Benefits of Providing Liquidity in Raydium CLMM Pools?[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/create-liquidity#what-are-the-benefits-of-providing-liquidity-in-raydium-clmm-pools)

**CLMM (Concentrated Liquidity Market Maker)** is designed for more advanced liquidity providers.

**Concentrated Liquidity and Higher Capital Efficiency：**LPs can choose a **custom price range** in which their liquidity is active.

This results in:

*   More concentrated liquidity
    
*   Higher fee efficiency
    
*   Lower trading slippage
    

**More Flexible Risk Management：**By selecting different price ranges, LPs can express different market views, such as **bullish, bearish, or neutral** strategies.

circle-info

**Note:** Impermanent Loss (IL) risk is higher, especially when the market price moves outside the selected range.

circle-check

**Learn more about Raydium liquidity pools and rules：**[https://docs.raydium.io/raydiumarrow-up-right](https://docs.raydium.io/raydium)

circle-check

**Create a Standard AMM Pool:** [https://docs.raydium.io/raydium/zhong-wen/chuangjian-chi-zi/chuang-jian-biao-zhun-amm-chiarrow-up-right](https://docs.raydium.io/raydium/zhong-wen/chuangjian-chi-zi/chuang-jian-biao-zhun-amm-chi)

# Solana Update Token Tutorial | CiaoTool

circle-check

**Solana Update Token：**[https://ciaotool.io/zh-CN/token/updatearrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/zh-CN/token/update)

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/update#how-to-update-token-metadata-on-solana)

🖋️ **How to Update Token Metadata on Solana**


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  You can access the update feature directly from the **Token Management** page. If the token has update permissions, an **Update** button will be displayed.
    
2.  You can go directly to the **Token Update** page, select the token, and if the authority has not been renounced, you can proceed with the update.
    

![](https://docs.dogtools.meme/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1231829018-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FbI9FOXIMOA6RLmAW6lRu%252Fuploads%252FGkhXrOa85S5BJHypVVHP%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D04689105-1edc-4275-ab3f-64471ef46117&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=fbd96dd2&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/update#token-update-transaction-process)

🔄 **Token Update Transaction Process**


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Once the task begins, a log popup will appear to provide real-time updates on the transaction progress. (A single transaction signature is required.)
    

![](https://docs.dogtools.meme/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1231829018-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FbI9FOXIMOA6RLmAW6lRu%252Fuploads%252FOaO8BhCCuK12l6VROIpv%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7f1dcc1e-3374-404b-acf3-772b5ece5c20&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e7c6dfc0&sv=2)

If any issue arises during the process, we will clearly indicate the problem. **No fees will be charged for failed transactions**

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/update#frequently-asked-questions)

❓ Frequently Asked Questions

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/update#id-1.-what-token-information-can-be-updated-using-ciaotool)

1\. What token information can be updated using CiaoTool?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** You can update **token metadata**, as well as adjust **mint** and **freeze authorities**.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/update#id-2.-how-much-does-it-cost-to-update-token-info)

2\. How much does it cost to update token info?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** A fee is charged as marked by CiaoTool, currently **0.0375 SOL**.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/update#id-3.-do-permission-updates-take-effect-immediately)

3\. Do permission updates take effect immediately?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Yes, changes are **instantly synchronized on-chain**.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/update#id-4.-can-permissions-be-restored-after-revocation)

4\. Can permissions be restored after revocation?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** **No**, revoking permissions is an **irreversible action**, so proceed with caution.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/update#id-5.-is-it-safe-to-update-token-information)

5\. Is it safe to update token information?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Yes — as long as you're using a **secure wallet for signing**, the process is safe.

# Token Snapshot Tutorial | CiaoTool

circle-check

**Solana Token Snapshot:** [https://ciaotool.io/en-US/token/tokenTool/snapshot-token-holdersarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/en-US/token/tokenTool/snapshot-token-holders)

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/snapshot#common-use-cases)

✅ Common Use Cases


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Pre-airdrop targeting for active users
    
*   Analyze whales for market cap control
    
*   Identify loyal holders for community rewards
    
*   Support for data-driven marketing campaigns
    

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/snapshot#step-1-select-a-token)

🪙 Step 1: Select a Token


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Enter the target token address manually, or choose from tokens held in your connected wallet.

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FZWMnlSC6ZKFY1ZpUxSHw%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D90f1900e-1fb8-487b-9acb-fd51ff6403f1&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fea1e043&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/snapshot#step-2-set-filter-options)

📊 Step 2: Set Filter Options


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/snapshot#top-holder-filter-optional)

✅ Top Holder Filter (Optional)

Choose from preset ranges to fetch top holders:

*   Top 100 / 500 / 1000 / 2000 / 5000 / 10000 This will retrieve wallets with the highest token balances.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/snapshot#minimum-holding-amount-optional)

✅ Minimum Holding Amount (Optional)

Set a minimum token amount (e.g., 1000 tokens) to exclude low-balance or dust wallets from the snapshot.

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FUCLyIsKw4N1UGi4rIJss%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3De40d755e-91a9-4f18-918e-25782206d7b5&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b28b308f&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/snapshot#step-3-generate-and-export-snapshot)

🧾 Step 3: Generate & Export Snapshot


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Click **“Token Snapshot”** to fetch on-chain data. Once completed, export your results in one of the following formats:

*   **CSV** – ideal for airdrop distribution
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FcNYJ587qfhIS3vVOurjd%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8624b559-86e2-4bd2-888d-c73645346d91&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c2f24e93&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/snapshot#frequently-asked-questions)

❓Frequently Asked Questions

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/snapshot#id-1.-what-types-of-tokens-are-supported)

**1\. What types of tokens are supported?**

*   check
    
    **Answer:** All SPL-standard tokens are supported, including both standard tokens and Token2022 types.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/snapshot#id-2.-what-addresses-can-be-filtered-in-a-snapshot)

**2\. What addresses can be filtered in a snapshot?**

*   check
    
    **Answer:** You can filter Top 100 to Top 10,000 holders or set a custom minimum token balance to target specific users.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/snapshot#id-3.-can-i-export-the-snapshot-results)

**3\. Can I export the snapshot results?**

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Yes, results can be exported in CSV or JSON format for airdrop planning or market analysis.

# Solana Unfreeze Account Tutorial | CiaoTool

circle-check

**Solana Unfreeze Account：**[https://ciaotool.io/en-US/token/unfreeze-accountarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/en-US/token/unfreeze-account)

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/unfreeze#how-to-unfreeze-account-on-solana)

❄️ **How to Unfreeze Account on Solana**


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  You can navigate from the **Token Management** page (if you have unfreeze permissions and have not revoked them, the **Unfreeze** button will be displayed).
    
2.  Go directly to the **Unfreeze Account** page, select the token to operate on, enter the wallet address you want to unfreeze, and click the action button below.
    

![](https://docs.dogtools.meme/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1231829018-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FbI9FOXIMOA6RLmAW6lRu%252Fuploads%252FRTftXTzUbEQYGXimFTuV%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db0416a3f-cddd-4d3a-bac4-d41611fbac80&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=827a500b&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/unfreeze#unfreeze-account-transaction-process)

⛓️ **Unfreeze Account Transaction Process**


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Once the task begins, a log popup will appear to provide real-time updates on the transaction progress. (A single transaction signature is required.)
    

![](https://docs.dogtools.meme/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1231829018-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FbI9FOXIMOA6RLmAW6lRu%252Fuploads%252FOaO8BhCCuK12l6VROIpv%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7f1dcc1e-3374-404b-acf3-772b5ece5c20&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e7c6dfc0&sv=2)

*   If any issue arises during the process, we will clearly indicate the problem. **No fees will be charged for failed transactions.**
    

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/unfreeze#frequently-asked-questions)

❓ Frequently Asked Questions

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/unfreeze#id-1.-what-permission-is-required-to-unfreeze-an-account)

1\. What permission is required to unfreeze an account?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Only an account with **Freeze authority** can perform the unfreeze operation.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/unfreeze#id-2.-can-the-account-trade-immediately-after-being-unfrozen)

2\. Can the account trade immediately after being unfrozen?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Yes, once unfrozen, the account’s **transfer and trading rights** are instantly restored.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/unfreeze#id-3.-does-unfreezing-an-account-incur-a-transaction-fee)

3\. Does unfreezing an account incur a transaction fee?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Yes, the unfreeze action incurs a **standard on-chain transaction fee**.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/unfreeze#id-4.-can-the-unfreeze-action-be-reversed)

4\. Can the unfreeze action be reversed?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** No, once completed, the **account permissions are immediately restored** and cannot be undone.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/unfreeze#id-5.-how-do-i-unfreeze-an-account-using-ciaotool)

5\. How do I unfreeze an account using CiaoTool?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Go to the **Token Management** page, select the frozen account, click **Unfreeze**, and sign the transaction.
    

💬 **Need help? Join our community for real-time support:** [https://t.me/ciaotoolarrow-up-right](https://t.me/ciaotool)

# Solana Revoke Permission Tutorial | CiaoTool

circle-check

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/revoke#solana-revoke-permission-https-ciaotool.io-zh-cn-token-revoke-permission)

Solana Revoke Permission：[https://ciaotool.io/zh-CN/token/revoke-permissionarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/zh-CN/token/revoke-permission)



----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/revoke#how-to-renounce-token-authority-on-solana)

➕ **How to Renounce Token Authority on Solana**


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  You can access the renouncement feature directly from the **Token Management** page. If any authority has not been renounced, a **Renounce Authority** button will be displayed.
    
2.  You can go directly to the **Renounce Authority** page, select the token, and if any permissions are still active, you can toggle the renouncement switch and click the action button below to proceed.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252Fc0h3VEhXgep33vrVP6Ut%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da8402e73-e6f1-4011-af3f-81fbd40ad3ba&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=86e29790&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/revoke#renouncement-transaction-process)

🔄 **Renouncement Transaction Process**


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Once the task begins, a log popup will appear to provide real-time updates on the transaction progress. (A single transaction signature is required.)

![](https://docs.dogtools.meme/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1231829018-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FbI9FOXIMOA6RLmAW6lRu%252Fuploads%252FOaO8BhCCuK12l6VROIpv%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7f1dcc1e-3374-404b-acf3-772b5ece5c20&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e7c6dfc0&sv=2)

If any issue arises during the process, we will clearly indicate the problem. **No fees will be charged for failed transactions.**

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/revoke#frequently-asked-questions)

❓ Frequently Asked Questions

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/revoke#id-1.-what-permissions-are-required-to-mint-more-tokens)

1\. What permissions are required to mint more tokens?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** You must retain the **Mint authority** to perform any token minting operations.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/revoke#id-2.-will-the-total-supply-update-immediately-after-minting)

2\. Will the total supply update immediately after minting?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Yes, the change is reflected **instantly on-chain**, and updates will appear in your wallet and on block explorers.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/revoke#id-3.-will-minting-more-tokens-affect-the-token-price)

3\. Will minting more tokens affect the token price?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Minting increases the total supply, which may **impact market price and liquidity** — proceed with caution.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/revoke#id-4.-how-can-i-mint-tokens-using-ciaotool)

4\. How can I mint tokens using CiaoTool?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Go to the **Token Management** section in CiaoTool, select **Mint**, enter the amount, and confirm the signature.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/token-management/revoke#id-5.-is-token-minting-safe)

5\. Is token minting safe?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** As long as your **private key is secure** and permissions are properly managed, minting is a **safe and controlled** process.
