# Phantom Wallet Installation Guide Tutorial | CiaoTool

circle-info

Phantom is the most popular wallet for Solana users—install it first to use CiaoTool for token issuance.

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/solana-base/phantom-wallet-installation-guide-tutorial#browser-extension)

**Browser Extension**


---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  **Visit the Official Website**:
    

Navigate to [https://phantom.app/downloadarrow-up-right](https://phantom.app/download)
 and select your browser type.

1.  **Add Phantom to Your Browser**: Follow the steps in your browser's extension store to add Phantom. Once installed, you will see Phantom in your browser extensions.
    
2.  **Set Up Your Wallet**:
    
    *   If you're a new user, select **"Create New Wallet"** and set up a password.
        
    *   If you already have a Solana wallet, click **"I Already Have a Wallet"** and input your recovery phrase to restore the wallet.
        
    *   After entering your password, click **"Continue"**.
        
    

![](https://docs.dogtools.meme/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FbI9FOXIMOA6RLmAW6lRu%2Fblobs%2F9iqHQqbiXfCNBbAGmcE4%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=19c84caa&sv=2)

1.  **Secure Your Recovery Phrase**:
    

*   Store your recovery phrase in a secure location. It is the only way to recover your wallet.
    
*   **Important**: Never share your recovery phrase with anyone. Anyone with access to this phrase can access your funds.
    

![](https://docs.dogtools.meme/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FbI9FOXIMOA6RLmAW6lRu%2Fblobs%2F8grY8PuEQS6uiRtz6Qjy%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a9cae362&sv=2)

1.  **Complete Installation**:
    

*   Once the installation is complete, you can find your wallet via the browser extension icon in the top-right corner.
    

![](https://docs.dogtools.meme/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FbI9FOXIMOA6RLmAW6lRu%2Fblobs%2Fbrkq1nXEbwGr9kSHIu8q%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=8efe1d04&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/solana-base/phantom-wallet-installation-guide-tutorial#mobile-app)

**Mobile App**


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  **Visit the Official Website**: Navigate to [https://phantom.app/downloadarrow-up-right](https://phantom.app/download)
     and choose the appropriate app store for your device (iOS/Android).
    
2.  **Install the Phantom App**: You will be redirected to the app store. Follow the instructions to download and install the Phantom app on your device.
    
3.  **Set Up Your Wallet**:
    
    *   If you're a new user, select **"Create New Wallet"** and enable device verification (varies by device type) to protect your wallet from unauthorized access.
        
    *   If you already have a Solana wallet, select **"I Already Have a Wallet"** and input your recovery phrase to restore the wallet.
        
    

![](https://docs.dogtools.meme/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FbI9FOXIMOA6RLmAW6lRu%2Fblobs%2FRoGrwHczsml7g6aeIoAu%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=a1c04638&sv=2)

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/solana-base/phantom-wallet-installation-guide-tutorial#important-notes)

**Important Notes**


-----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

*   Phantom wallet supports Solana, Ethereum, and Polygon chains. After creating a wallet, you will have three separate addresses.
    
*   When withdrawing or transferring tokens, **always copy the Solana address**. Ensure you select the correct address to avoid errors.

# Pump Launch To Bundled Buy and Snipe Tutorial | CiaoTool

circle-check

**Pump Launch To Bundled Buy and Snipe**：[https://ciaotool.io/en-US/pump/snipe/launch-buy-snipearrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/en-US/pump/snipe/launch-buy-snipe)

circle-exclamation

If you prefer learning by video, check out this tutorial for a step-by-step guide on how to buy at launch and snipe on Solana.

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/launch-bundled-buy-snipe#how-to-pump-launch-to-bundled-buy-and-snipe)

🧩 **How to** Pump Launch To Bundled Buy and Snipe**？**


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/launch-bundled-buy-snipe#id-1.-connect-your-wallet-phantom-recommended)

**1\. Connect Your Wallet (Phantom Recommended)**

*   Open the **Pump Launch To Bundled Buy and Snipe** interface.
    
*   Click **“Select Wallet”** in the top-right corner, select your wallet, and approve authorization.
    
*   Once your wallet address appears in the top-right corner, the connection is successful.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252F5XYqYQG7Gvz6QYWzUWSj%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D6e39ebf0-39ba-47af-bab3-e699d9db5575&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=506db133&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/launch-bundled-buy-snipe#id-2.-fill-in-basic-token-information)

**2\. Fill in Basic Token Information**

*   You may manually enter token details or click **“Clone”** to copy information from another token.
    
*   Click **\[Show more options\]** to add website and other contact information.
    
*   You can set **auto-sell all tokens when price increases by X%**.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252F7xEeNH2e4AJKxAiKrNoy%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Debfafd62-afd4-4438-a2d7-d251dcc1dd16&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4884a46f&sv=2)

circle-info

If auto-sell is enabled, it is recommended **not to use the dev wallet for buying**, or provide the dev wallet’s private key below to participate. Otherwise, manual signature may be required during selling, which could cause delays.

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/launch-bundled-buy-snipe#id-3.-custom-contract-address)

**3\. Custom Contract Address**

**Two Methods for Setting Custom Contract Addresses：**

1.  Create a personalized token address and choose whether it ends with **“pump”**.
    
    *   Check ☑️ **pump** and confirm in your wallet
        
    
2.  Select **“Import Private Key”**
    
    *   Paste your pre-generated private key (**The address must be a new one that has never paid SOL rent**)**.**
        
    *   The system will deploy the token using this address, ensuring the contract matches your expectation.
        
    

circle-exclamation

**Note:** Selecting either option will immediately require wallet signature and payment of the platform fee (0.01 SOL).

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252Fmzpnj1NT3bmQGUqWFySH%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D19af14a6-55f6-4273-bf41-a7de593a2184&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4c70aee3&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/launch-bundled-buy-snipe#id-4.-dev-wallet-settings)

**4\. Dev Wallet Settings**

*   If the dev wallet does **not** set a buy amount, no service fee is charged.
    
*   If it participates in buying, the same service fee as other buy wallets applies.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FwKkF79cUF43v8JztdiRC%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D41db5a10-1c61-409f-88e9-c59ee787abd8&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fa1b2424&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/launch-bundled-buy-snipe#id-5.-bundled-buy-wallet-settings)

**5\. Bundled Buy Wallet Settings**

*   Bundled buy uses a **tiered pricing model**—the more wallets you add, the lower the service fee per wallet.
    
*   **Batch import wallets** (**Excel / CSV / TXT / JSON**) or manually paste private keys
    
*   **Set buy amount:** fixed amount / percentage / all (maximum purchasable amount per wallet)
    
*   In addition to service fees, each new address requires **0.00203928 SOL** as account rent.
    

circle-exclamation

For **Pump.fun Launch and Bundled Buy,** ensure buy wallets have sufficient funds and gas to avoid failure. Maximum **9 wallets** can participate simultaneously.

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FURyjUwIY2E21jJwzmYuS%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7fa11be0-886d-486f-9040-a108cb301f32&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=60780083&sv=2)

circle-info

**Note:** This might be detected by Pump as bot behavior.

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/launch-bundled-buy-snipe#id-6.-swap-buy-wallet)

**6\. Swap Buy Wallet：**

This wallet will be used for subsequent swap operations. Setup method:

*   Import the private key
    
*   Enter the estimated amount of SOL to be used by this wallet (_the actual buy amount depends on the selected purchase ratio_)
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252F9WdPvmzAQjf57dBp9fqC%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfd97630f-04b7-4c4b-9e6c-b40081ba08d9&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fc360b83&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/launch-bundled-buy-snipe#id-7.-pre-generate-token-contract)

**7\. Pre-Generate Token Contract**

Supports generating the contract address in advance—useful for pre-launch marketing or integrations.

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FPipqMSsubVBZQuH9xiM8%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D8f82e4b9-f5c0-418b-bda1-32350f1e1aef&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c4189f76&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/launch-bundled-buy-snipe#id-8.-jito-tip-settings)

**8\. Jito Tip Settings**

*   Configure the Jito MEV tip to accelerate transaction bundling and increase priority in block ordering.
    
*   After configuration, click **“Pump Launch and Buy Snipe.”**
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FzzfO5BjuWHuME9ae9oTu%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D5ab0affb-ec60-4f81-b84a-b29af852b774&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b9c7f11f&sv=2)

circle-exclamation

This feature relies on **Jito bundling**. Due to network conditions, Jito nodes, RPC nodes, and block engine factors, the failure rate may be relatively high.

If the operation fails:

*   The launch will not succeed
    
*   No fees will be charged
    

You may try switching RPC nodes or block engines, increasing the Jito tip (**recommended: 0.01 SOL**), or retrying during lower on-chain activity periods.

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/launch-bundled-buy-snipe#id-8.-process-display)

8\. Process Display

*   Once the task starts, a log pop-up will display real-time progress updates.
    
*   After a successful transaction, you will receive both the **transaction link** and **token link** for direct viewing.
    
*   If any issue occurs at any stage, clear feedback will be provided. No fees will be charged for failed operations.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252Fz3wWK61c5hIYKRqOunzD%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfc1576d6-68ea-42a4-b010-1b219b0f747e&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7ab158eb&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/launch-bundled-buy-snipe#frequently-asked-questions-faq)

❓ Frequently Asked Questions (FAQ)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/launch-bundled-buy-snipe#id-1.-what-is-a-bundled-buy-wallet)

1\. What is a Bundled Buy Wallet?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** This is a group of wallets used to simultaneously execute buy transactions at the moment a Pump project launches. You can set up to 12 wallets.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/launch-bundled-buy-snipe#id-2.-whats-the-difference-between-a-dev-wallet-and-a-swap-wallet)

2\. What’s the difference between a Dev Wallet and a Swap Wallet?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** The Dev Wallet is used to deploy the token contract; the Swap Wallet is used to buy tokens on the market after launch (typically for market-making or liquidity control).
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/launch-bundled-buy-snipe#id-3.-whats-the-advantage-of-pre-generating-the-token-contract)

3\. What’s the advantage of pre-generating the token contract?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** It saves deployment wait time and ensures a smoother sniping process without delays — especially useful for short-term opportunities.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/launch-bundled-buy-snipe#id-4.-is-paying-the-jito-tip-required)

4\. Is paying the Jito tip required?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** It’s not required, but enabling it greatly improves transaction priority and helps avoid being front-run or missing the launch.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/ecosystem/launch-bundled-buy-snipe#id-5.-will-the-system-store-my-private-key)

5\. Will the system store my private key?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** No. All signing processes are done locally in your browser. CiaoTool never uploads or stores private keys, ensuring your security.
    

💬 **Need help? Join our community for real-time support:** [https://t.me/ciaotoolarrow-up-right](https://t.me/ciaotool)

*   **Email:** [support@ciaotool.ioenvelope](mailto:support@ciaotool.io)
    
*   **Website:** [https://ciaotool.ioarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/)
    
*   **X (Twitter):** [https://x.com/CiaoToolarrow-up-right](https://x.com/CiaoTool)
    
*   **Blog**: [https://www.ciaoailiquidity.com/blogarrow-up-right](https://www.ciaoailiquidity.com/blog)
    
*   **Medium:** [https://medium.com/@ciaotoolarrow-up-right](https://medium.com/@ciaotool)
    
*   **YouTube:** [https://www.youtube.com/@CiaoToolarrow-up-right](https://www.youtube.com/@CiaoTool)

# Batch Create Wallets Tutorial | CiaoTool

circle-check

**Solana Batch Create Wallets：**[https://ciaotool.io/en-US/wallet/my-wallets/create-walletsarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/en-US/wallet/my-wallets/create-wallets)

circle-exclamation

If you prefer learning through video, feel free to watch this tutorial — it walks you through how to generate hundreds of wallets in just one click!

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-manage/batch-create-wallets-tutorial#steps-to-create-batch-wallets)

🔗 **Steps to Create Batch Wallets**


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

1.  **Enter the Quantity**: Input the number of wallets you want to create.
    
2.  **Click Create**: Click the **Create** button to generate the wallets.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F3238960597-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252F5o8CHZqXSViIIrTaxA5N%252Fuploads%252FUZvaUrR5r2dab5B2fcEn%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D1093d07b-dca7-4939-86ab-e23eef50a429&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8c8f82dc&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-manage/batch-create-wallets-tutorial#frequently-asked-questions)

❓Frequently Asked Questions

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-manage/batch-create-wallets-tutorial#id-1.-how-many-wallet-addresses-can-i-create-at-once)

1\. How many wallet addresses can I create at once?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** CiaoTool supports generating up to 500 wallet addresses in one click. You can customize the quantity as needed.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-manage/batch-create-wallets-tutorial#id-2.-do-the-created-wallets-include-private-keys-how-can-i-export-them)

2\. Do the created wallets include private keys? How can I export them?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Yes. Each wallet is generated with a corresponding private key, which can be exported as a CSV or JSON file after the operation for backup or later use.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/wallet-manage/batch-create-wallets-tutorial#id-3.-are-these-wallets-secure-will-my-private-keys-be-uploaded)

3\. Are these wallets secure? Will my private keys be uploaded?

*   check
    
    **Answer:** Yes, they are secure. All wallet generation and private key handling are performed locally in your browser. The platform does not upload, store, or access any private key data.

# EVM 多链通用操作说明（必读） | 「EVM」使用教程 | CiaoTool

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/start/evm-duo-lian-tong-yong-cao-zuo-shuo-ming-bi-du#wei-shen-me-jiao-cheng-shi-tong-yong-de)

💡 **为什么教程是通用的？**

*   教程截图可能以 **BSC (BNB** **Smart** **Chain)** 为示例，方便演示（交易速度快，Gas 费低）。
    

实际操作中：

*   **界面一致**：Base、IoTeX、X Layer 等链上的发币界面与 BSC 完全相同。
    
*   **功能一致**：发币、空投、归集等逻辑完全相同。
    
*   **唯一区别**：需要在钱包中切换网络，并准备对应链的 Gas 代币（如 BNB、IOTX、ETH）。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/start/evm-duo-lian-tong-yong-cao-zuo-shuo-ming-bi-du#he-xin-bu-zhou-qie-huan-wang-luo-guan-jian)

⚙️ **核心步骤：切换网络（关键）**

1.  **选择目标网络**：在页面 选择 BSC、IoTeX、Base 或 X Layer
    
2.  **连接钱包：**点击右上角 **Connect Wallet**
    
3.  **自动刷新与状态同步**：
    
    *   当前链标识自动更新
        
    *   Gas 代币符号自动更新（如 BNB → IOTX / ETH）
        
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/start/evm-duo-lian-tong-yong-cao-zuo-shuo-ming-bi-du#xuan-ze-nin-de-lian-yi-jian-jin-ru-zhuan-shu-ru-kou)

🌐 **选择您的链：一键进入专属入口**

链名称

状态

入口链接

🔶 BNB Chain (BSC)

✅ 稳定

[进入 BSC 中心页arrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/)

🟠 IoTeX

✅ 稳定

[进入 IoTeX 中心页arrow-up-right](https://iotex.ciaotool.io/)

🔵 Base Chain

✅ 稳定

[进入 Base 中心页arrow-up-right](https://base.ciaotool.io/)

⚫ X Layer

✅ 稳定

[进入 X Layer 中心页arrow-up-right](https://xlayer.ciaotool.io/)

> 新链上线后，CiaoTool 会自动添加工具中心页，无需等待教程更新。

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm#cong-fa-bi-dao-guan-li-ciaotool-yi-zhan-gao-ding)

🚀 从发币到管理，CiaoTool 一站搞定

*   平台集成了包括代币**一键发射、批量转账、冷分仓、狙击保护、流动性控制**等核心功能，涵盖从代币创建、部署、分发到管理的完整流程，用户无需编写任何代码，即可高效完成复杂的链上操作。
    
*   我们在乎用户的每一个需求和问题。未来平台也将根据社区反馈，持续拓展功能模块。
    

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm#yong-hu-zhun-ru-tiao-jian-yu-falze-ren-shuo-ming)

🛡️ 用户准入条件与法律责任说明

1.  本平台严格遵守所在地区法律规定，仅面向符合当地法律的用户开放服务。中国大陆地区用户不得访问和使用本平台。
    
2.  用户需保证使用本平台时遵守其所在国家和地区的法律法规，平台不承担因用户违规操作引发的法律责任。
    

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm#wei-shen-me-xuan-ze-ciaotool)

✅ 为什么选择 CiaoTool ？

1️⃣ **可视化无代码操作：**直观的合约创建与配置流程，零代码即可完成部署与关键设置，新手也能独立上币。

2️⃣ **PancakeSwap 深度整合：**支持一键创建、添加与撤销流动性，实时显示价格、滑点与池子状态，让流动性管理更清晰可控。

3️⃣ **批量与自动化工具：**提供中转转账、批量归集与发送、批量一转多等功能，大幅提升多地址操作效率。

4️⃣ **多链多场景支持：**覆盖 BSC（Four.meme、Flap、Binance Alpha）、IoTeX（Robot Pump）以及 Base、X Layer 等主流网络，满足多样化发币与运营需求。

circle-check

**⚠️温馨提醒：**平台收取的费用中不包括 Gas 费和 Jito 小费。Gas 费用的变化取决于您选择的优先级程度，Jito 小费也可以根据您的需求自行设置。

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/service-fee#dai-bi-guan-li)

    ：0.104 BNB

    : 0.112 BNB

🤖 Swap专区

*   **市值管理「v2 and v3」**：0.0008 BNB / 每个地址
    
*   **批量交易「v2 and v3」**：0.0008 BNB / 每个地址
    
*   **创建流动性「v2 and v3」**：0.024 BNB / 单次
    
*   **添加流动性「v2 and v3」**：0.024 BNB / 单次
    
*   **移除流动性「v2 and v3」**：0.024 BNB / 单次
    
*   **创建流动性并捆绑买入「v2 and v3」**：0.024 BNB / 单次，0.02 BNB / 每个地址
    
*   **多地址捆绑买入「v2 and v3」**: 0.008 BNB / 每个地址
    
*   **多地址捆绑卖出「v2 and v3」:** 0.008 BNB / 每个地址

    ：0.008 BNB / 每个地址

###

🔁 FourMeme专区工具（支持USD1和BNB模式）

# 「多转一」教程-通用版 | 「EVM」使用教程 | CiaoTool

circle-check

**BSC 多对一转账**：[https://bsc.ciaotool.io/transfer/many-to-onearrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/transfer/many-to-one)

**Base 多对一转账：**[https://base.ciaotool.io/transfer/many-to-onearrow-up-right](https://base.ciaotool.io/transfer/many-to-one)

**X Layer 多对一转账：**[https://xlayer.ciaotool.io/transfer/many-to-onearrow-up-right](https://xlayer.ciaotool.io/transfer/many-to-one)

**IoTeX 多对一转账：**[https://iotex.ciaotool.io/transfer/many-to-onearrow-up-right](https://iotex.ciaotool.io/transfer/many-to-one)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/transfer/many-to-one#cao-zuo-bu-zhou)

🔗 **操作步骤**

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/transfer/many-to-one#id-1.-da-kai-duo-zhuan-yi-ye-mian-shu-ru-jie-shou-di-zhi)

1\. 打开多转一页面，输入接收地址

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/transfer/many-to-one#id-2.-xuan-ze-dai-bi-di-zhi-qing-xuan-ze-huo-shu-ru-dai-bi-di-zhi)

2\. 选择代币地址：请选择或输入代币地址

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FDjW7CDxrqUVSyHdqgLYC%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=adf2253&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/transfer/many-to-one#id-3.-shang-chuan-fa-song-si-yao-shou-dong-nian-tie-huo-shang-chuan-wen-jian)

3\. 上传发送私钥：手动粘贴或上传文件

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FWn4RGIrYG5a1xtNMsTKw%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=630d24c0&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/transfer/many-to-one#id-4.-shu-ru-jie-shou-di-zhi-qing-wu-bi-zi-xi-que-ren-nin-de-jie-shou-di-zhi)

4\. 输入接收地址。请务必仔细确认您的接收地址

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2F3IyHxrSqTOfFOf3mT414%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=89fded7a&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/transfer/many-to-one#id-5.-she-zhi-zhuan-zhang-shu-liang-lei-xing)

5\. 设置转账数量类型

1.  全部数量
    
2.  固定数量
    
3.  固定留存
    
4.  自定义(点击输入)
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FemMYt00ZwPlkLhyPzPWo%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f79ad597&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/transfer/many-to-one#id-6.-que-ding-hou-zhi-xing-fa-song)

6.确定后执行发送

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FFuePxXpIHD3UxGcnxD9g%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=35e37db1&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/transfer/many-to-one#chang-jian-wen-ti-faq)

❓ 常见问题 FAQ

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/transfer/many-to-one#id-1.-shen-me-shi-duo-zhuan-yi)

**1\. 什么是 多转一？**

*   check
    
    答：指将多个钱包中的代币统一转账至一个主地址的操作。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/transfer/many-to-one#id-2.-xi-tong-shi-fou-zhi-chi-gui-ji-bu-tong-jine)

**2\. 系统是否支持归集不同金额？**

*   check
    
    答：支持。可设置全部转出或为每个地址自定义转账数额。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/transfer/many-to-one#id-3.-si-yao-shi-fou-an-quan)

**3\. 私钥是否安全？**

*   check
    
    答：安全。所有私钥仅用于本地签名，不上传任何服务器。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/transfer/many-to-one#id-4.-ke-yi-gui-ji-na-xie-dai-bi)

**4\. 可以归集哪些代币？**

*   check
    
    答：支持你选择链的所有代币，只需输入合约地址即可。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/transfer/many-to-one#id-5.-shi-fou-zhi-chi-dao-ru-da-liang-di-zhi)

**5\. 是否支持导入大量地址？**

*   check
    
    答：支持。可通过xls、xlsx格式文件导入地址。
    

**💬 如遇到问题？加入社群实时咨询**：[https://t.me/ciaotoolarrow-up-right](https://t.me/ciaotool)

*   **Email**：[support@ciaotool.ioenvelope](mailto:support@ciaotool.io)
    
*   **官网**：[https://ciaotool.ioarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/)
    
*   **X（Twitter）**：[https://x.com/CiaoToolarrow-up-right](https://x.com/CiaoTool)
    
*   **Medium**： [https://medium.com/@ciaotoolarrow-up-right](https://medium.com/@ciaotool)
    
*   **Blog**：[https://www.ciaoailiquidity.com/zh/blogarrow-up-right](https://www.ciaoailiquidity.com/zh/blog)
    
*   **YouTube**：[https://www.youtube.com/@CiaoToolarrow-up-right](https://www.youtube.com/@CiaoTool)
    
*   **WhatsApp**：[https://whatsapp.com/channel/0029VbAuLrVAojYxRNw95W1Jarrow-up-right](https://whatsapp.com/channel/0029VbAuLrVAojYxRNw95W1J)

# CiaoTool · EVM | 「EVM」Tutorial | CiaoTool

![Page cover](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F467813208-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcL6r1KVJmw4jLFWVpQbl%252Fuploads%252F68dq0AiOX5ixAY8KvvPq%252F423954199%2520%281%29.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc6334858-8c51-4149-ad5d-644dcbc0f039&width=1248&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f2ffd37a&sv=2)

*   CiaoTool integrates token creation, project management, liquidity deployment, airdrops, and market-making tools into one powerful platform.
    
*   It provides a complete one-stop solution to help users efficiently launch projects, optimize liquidity structures, and build successful tokens.
    

circle-check

Currently, CiaoTool supports major EVM networks including **BSC, IoTeX, Base, and X Layer**, with more chains and features continuously being added. Stay tuned.

[![Logo](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fbsc.ciaotool.io%2Ffavicon.ico&width=20&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=92b0cc9b&sv=2)https://bsc.ciaotool.io/bsc.ciaotool.iochevron-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/)

[![Logo](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fiotex.ciaotool.io%2Ffavicon.ico&width=20&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=571c5e7c&sv=2)https://iotex.ciaotool.io/iotex.ciaotool.iochevron-right](https://iotex.ciaotool.io/)

[![Logo](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fbase.ciaotool.io%2Ffavicon.ico&width=20&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=41cfabf4&sv=2)https://base.ciaotool.io/base.ciaotool.iochevron-right](https://base.ciaotool.io/)

[![Logo](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fxlayer.ciaotool.io%2Ffavicon.ico&width=20&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ce6a6be0&sv=2)https://xlayer.ciaotool.io/xlayer.ciaotool.iochevron-right](https://xlayer.ciaotool.io/)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en#from-token-launch-to-management-all-in-one-place)

🚀 From Token Launch to Management — All in One Place

*   CiaoTool integrates essential tools such as **one-click token launch**, **MultiSender**, **Asset Fragmentation**, **anti-MEV protection**, and **liquidity control**. From creation and deployment to distribution and permission management, users can execute complex on-chain operations **without writing any code**. Even Web3 newcomers can quickly master token issuance and operations through CiaoTool’s intuitive **visual interface**.
    
*   We value every user’s needs and feedback. The platform will continue expanding its feature modules based on community input.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en#user-eligibility-and-legal-notice)

🛡️ User Eligibility and Legal Notice

1.  This platform strictly complies with local laws and is only accessible to users who meet their jurisdiction’s regulatory requirements.
    
2.  **Users located in mainland China are prohibited** from accessing and using this platform.
    
3.  All users must ensure they comply with their local laws while using the platform. CiaoTool is **not liable for any legal consequences** resulting from user violations.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en#why-choose-ciaotool)

Why Choose CiaoTool ?

1️⃣ **Visual No-Code Operations：**Intuitive contract creation and configuration process. Deploy and set up critical parameters with zero code, empowering even beginners to launch tokens independently.

2️⃣ **Optimized for PancakeSwap：**Easily create, add, or remove liquidity with real-time price and slippage display.

3️⃣ **Batch Tools：**Handle multi-transfer, batch collection/sending, failed transaction retry, and gas budgeting with ease.

4️⃣ **Multi-chain, multi-scenario support:** Covering BSC (**Four.meme**, **Flap**, **Binance Alpha**), **IoTeX (Robot Pump**), as well as Base and X Layer, meeting diverse token issuance and operational needs across ecosystems.

# 「一转多」教程-通用版 | 「EVM」使用教程 | CiaoTool

circle-check

**BSC：**[https://bsc.ciaotool.io/transfer/one-to-manyarrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/transfer/one-to-many)

**Base：**[https://base.ciaotool.io/transfer/one-to-manyarrow-up-right](https://base.ciaotool.io/transfer/one-to-many)

**X Layer：**[https://xlayer.ciaotool.io/transfer/one-to-manyarrow-up-right](https://xlayer.ciaotool.io/transfer/one-to-many)

**IoTeX：**[https://iotex.ciaotool.io/transfer/one-to-manyarrow-up-right](https://iotex.ciaotool.io/transfer/one-to-many)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/transfer/one-to-many#shi-pin-jiao-cheng)

📹 视频教程

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/transfer/one-to-many#yi-dui-duo-zhuan-zhang-jiao-cheng-onetomany-transfer)

🧾 一对多转账教程（One-to-Many Transfer）

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/transfer/one-to-many#id-1.-bang-ding-qian-bao-bang-ding-zhi-chi-bsc-lian-de-qian-bao)

**1\. 绑定钱包：绑定支持BSC链的钱包**

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FNh1hoNxgVQrp3ioqC92a%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b0241f23&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/transfer/one-to-many#id-2.-xuan-ze-bang-ding-qian-bao-qian-bao)

**2\. 选择绑定钱包钱包**

*   可使用当前连接的钱包，或导入其他钱包私钥。
    

circle-info

**自用钱包**：接收钱包地址数量有 200 个限制

**其他钱包**：接收钱包地址数量无限制，可自由添加

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FPq0bsgnFDpjfX76aiNhX%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=18c43c44&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/transfer/one-to-many#id-3.-xuan-ze-jinemo-shi-zhi-chi-xiang-tong-shu-liang-zhuan-zhang-huo-wei-mei-ge-di-zhi-she-zhi-zi-ding)

**3\. 选择金额模式：**支持「相同数量转账」或为每个地址设置「自定义数量」，自定义数量如下图格式。

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FMqIfkNNzxhG44ol4ndR3%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f2aaa2dd&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/transfer/one-to-many#id-4.-shu-ru-dai-bi-di-zhi-xuan-ze-dai-bi-li-ru-busdusdt-huo-shou-dong-shu-ru-dai-bi-he-yue-di-zhi)

**4\. 输入代币地址：**选择代币（例如 BUSD、USDT），或手动输入代币合约地址。

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2Fl0ln02x60ycvSE9uBjol%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1bb67ec7&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/transfer/one-to-many#id-5.-tian-jia-jie-shou-di-zhi-ke-shou-dong-nian-tie-huo-shang-chuan-di-zhi-lie-biao-wen-jian-xlsxlsx-g)

**5\. 添加接收地址：**可手动粘贴或上传地址列表文件（xls、xlsx格式）。

1.  **选择相同数量转账，即需要设置相同转账金额** 输入每个接收地址的代币数量，或上传带金额的地址文件。
    
2.  **发送** 确认后签名，一键完成批量发送。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FEfUu9GN5YYKtjFd2ubG4%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=268fb47d&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/transfer/one-to-many#chang-jian-wen-ti-faq)

❓常见问题 FAQ

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/transfer/one-to-many#id-1.-shi-fou-zhi-chi-bu-tong-di-zhi-zhuan-bu-tong-shu-liang)

1\. 是否支持不同地址转不同数量？

*   check
    
    答：支持。可上传自定义金额的 xls、xlsx格式文件，精细控制每笔转账。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/transfer/one-to-many#id-2.-cao-zuo-shi-fou-an-quan)

2\. 操作是否安全？

*   check
    
    答：安全。私钥仅用于本地签名，系统不保存任何钱包数据。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/transfer/one-to-many#id-3.-zhuan-zhang-shi-bai-zen-me-ban)

3\. 转账失败怎么办？

*   check
    
    答：请检查地址是否有效、余额是否充足，并适当提高 Gas 限额重试。
    

**💬 如遇到问题？加入社群实时咨询**：[https://t.me/ciaotoolarrow-up-right](https://t.me/ciaotool)

*   **Email**：[support@ciaotool.ioenvelope](mailto:support@ciaotool.io)
    
*   **官网**：[https://ciaotool.ioarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/)

# 「多转多」教程-通用版 | 「EVM」使用教程 | CiaoTool

circle-check

**BSC多对多转账**：[https://bsc.ciaotool.io/transfer/many-to-manyarrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/transfer/many-to-many)

**Base多对多转账：**[https://base.ciaotool.io/transfer/many-to-manyarrow-up-right](https://base.ciaotool.io/transfer/many-to-many)

**X Layer多对多转账：**[https://xlayer.ciaotool.io/transfer/many-to-manyarrow-up-right](https://xlayer.ciaotool.io/transfer/many-to-many)

**IoTeX多对多转账：**[https://iotex.ciaotool.io/transfer/many-to-manyarrow-up-right](https://iotex.ciaotool.io/transfer/many-to-many)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/transfer/many-to-many#cao-zuo-bu-zhou)

🔗 **操作步骤**

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/transfer/many-to-many#id-1.-xuan-ze-dai-bi-di-zhi)

**1\. 选择代币地址**

*   输入或选择需要发送的代币合约地址。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FgD5FEZlKcauwwpyIKuFn%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=50da0a89&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/transfer/many-to-many#id-2.-shang-chuan-fa-song-si-yao)

**2\. 上传发送私钥**

*   上传包含多个私钥的钱包文件（xls、xlsx格式），系统将识别来源钱包。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FEF41y8aHvR2FeHCoTBXK%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5c601e0&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/transfer/many-to-many#id-3.-shang-chuan-jie-shou-di-zhi)

**3\. 上传接收地址**

*   上传接收地址列表，确保发送方和接收方数量一致（如10个地址发给10个接收地址）。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FHeK6LGgnDpFDh5LgIX2U%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=468a9ea6&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/transfer/many-to-many#id-4.-she-zhi-zhuan-zhang-can-shu)

**4\. 设置转账参数**

1.  全部数量
    
2.  固定数量
    
3.  固定留存
    
4.  自定义(点击输入)
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FIAdK1T4tsHPkiJ0bjGVB%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6ff51f52&sv=2)

*   自定义输入转账数量可上传文件或手动换行输入
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FW2qhRAwRxX26i9mAYugV%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d618ff8d&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/transfer/many-to-many#id-5.-zhi-xing-pi-liang-zhuan-zhang)

**5\. 执行批量转账**

*   一键确认操作并签名，系统将自动完成所有多对多交易。
    

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/transfer/many-to-many#chang-jian-wen-ti-faq)

❓ 常见问题 FAQ

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/transfer/many-to-many#id-1.-shen-me-shi-duo-dui-duo-zhuan-zhang)

**1\. 什么是多对多转账？**

*   check
    
    答：指多个发送地址向多个接收地址批量发送代币。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/transfer/many-to-many#id-2.-mei-ge-di-zhi-ke-yi-she-zhi-bu-tong-jinema)

**2\. 每个地址可以设置不同金额吗？**

*   check
    
    答：支持。可在上传文件中自定义每笔交易的金额。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/transfer/many-to-many#id-3.-xi-tong-shi-fou-bao-cun-wo-de-si-yao)

**3\. 系统是否保存我的私钥？**

*   check
    
    答：不会。所有签名操作仅在本地浏览器完成，保障私钥安全。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/transfer/many-to-many#id-4.-zhi-chi-duo-shao-zu-di-zhi-jin-xing-zhuan-zhang)

**4\. 支持多少组地址进行转账？**

*   check
    
    答：没有数量限制，适合中大型批量操作。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/transfer/many-to-many#id-5.-shi-fou-ke-yi-dao-ru-xlsxlsx-ge-shi-wen-jian)

**5\. 是否可以导入** xls、xlsx格式**文件？**

*   check
    
    答：可以。发送私钥和接收地址都支持xls、xlsx格式导入，提高效率。
    

**💬 如遇到问题？加入社群实时咨询**：[https://t.me/ciaotoolarrow-up-right](https://t.me/ciaotool)

*   **Email**：[support@ciaotool.ioenvelope](mailto:support@ciaotool.io)
    
*   **官网**：[https://ciaotool.ioarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/)
    
*   **X（Twitter）**：[https://x.com/CiaoToolarrow-up-right](https://x.com/CiaoTool)
    
*   **Medium**： [https://medium.com/@ciaotoolarrow-up-right](https://medium.com/@ciaotool)
    
*   **Blog**：[https://www.ciaoailiquidity.com/zh/blogarrow-up-right](https://www.ciaoailiquidity.com/zh/blog)
    
*   **YouTube**：[https://www.youtube.com/@CiaoToolarrow-up-right](https://www.youtube.com/@CiaoTool)
    
*   **WhatsApp**：[https://whatsapp.com/channel/0029VbAuLrVAojYxRNw95W1Jarrow-up-right](https://whatsapp.com/channel/0029VbAuLrVAojYxRNw95W1J)

# 市值管理教程「v2 and v3」 | 「EVM」使用教程 | CiaoTool

circle-check

**市值管理v2：**[https://bsc.ciaotool.io/swap/v2/market-making-manage-v2arrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/swap/v2/market-making-manage-v2)

**市值管理v3：**[https://bsc.ciaotool.io/swap/v3/market-making-manage-v3arrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/swap/v3/market-making-manage-v3)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/market-making-v2-v3#ru-he-shi-yong-shi-zhi-guan-li)

✅ 如何使用市值管理？

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/market-making-v2-v3#id-1.-she-zhi-dai-bi)

1\. 设置代币

*   在输入框中填写目标代币地址，或点击下拉菜单选择当前钱包持有的代币。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FeCTD2O8PWFE8g1saAeqr%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4c147172&sv=2)

*   快速切换交易买卖方向**（From**：支出的代币、**To**：获得的代币）
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FPRU1eLLTNlq3b5Yp1TQr%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5403c1d7&sv=2)

circle-exclamation

V3市值管理操作中，设置代币直接粘贴**币对**即可

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FWIiIDF1DCILNajNqDk8z%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=310c1a06&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/market-making-v2-v3#id-2.-she-zhi-jiao-yi-can-shu)

2\. 设置交易参数

*   **设置交易间隔（单位：秒 ⏱️）**
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FGpwzdbBRbgx0m03LTsug%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=27be84b8&sv=2)

*   **选择交易数量模式（固定数量/固定留存/全部数量）**
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2F6dFmbG36cFoLtZPJorTH%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9f189592&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/market-making-v2-v3#id-3.-dao-ru-qian-bao-si-yao)

**3\.** 导入钱包私钥

将用于支付市值操作手续费的钱包私钥导入。

circle-info

请务必确保私钥安全，不要随意外泄。

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/market-making-v2-v3#id-4.-she-zhi-ting-zhi-fang-shi-yu-xun-huan-zhi-xing-ci-shu)

**4.设置停止方式与循环执行次数**

*   check
    
    按执行次数停止：控制买卖力度与节奏
    
*   check
    
    按价格范围停止；避免超买或砸穿价格带
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2F2Rujsx7CRQyQQxE98k2S%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=aca88ec8&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/market-making-v2-v3#id-5.-dao-ru-pi-liang-jiao-yi-de-qian-bao)

5.导入批量交易的钱包

*   可上传私钥文件导入和手动输入
    

circle-info

每个交易的钱包中，需要有一些（0.0008BNB） BNB 用于支付交易 Gas.

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2Flt34cQY1WIIwy1U3jwL6%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f960b72&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/market-making-v2-v3#id-6.-zui-zhong-que-ren-bing-kai-shi-jiao-yi)

6\. 最终确认并开始交易

*   执行前请检查，仔细确认后点击 → **开始交易**
    

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/market-making-v2-v3#chang-jian-wen-ti-faq)

❓常见问题 FAQ

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/market-making-v2-v3#id-1.-yun-xing-zhong-neng-zan-ting-ma)

**1\.** 运行中能暂停吗？

*   check
    
    答：可以，随时可暂停或立即终止，不影响资产储备。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/market-making-v2-v3#id-2.-wei-shen-me-shi-zhi-guan-li-jian-yi-shi-yong-duo-qian-bao)

**2\.** 为什么市值管理建议使用多钱包？

*   check
    
    答：分散持仓、做盘痕迹更自然、盘口深度更真实、避免“一眼控盘”。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/market-making-v2-v3#id-3.-gu-ding-liu-cun-mo-shi-de-yong-tu)

**3\.** 固定留存模式的用途？

*   check
    
    答：保持每个钱包持仓结构不变，对外看更自然，减少恐慌性抛压。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/market-making-v2-v3#id-4.-chang-jian-zhi-xing-shi-bai-yuan-yin)

**4\.** 常见执行失败原因？

*   check
    
    答：滑点太低、余额不足、RPC 拥堵、Gas费用不足。
    

**💬 如遇到问题？加入社群实时咨询**：[https://t.me/ciaotoolarrow-up-right](https://t.me/ciaotool)

*   **Email**：[support@ciaotool.ioenvelope](mailto:support@ciaotool.io)
    
*   **官网**：[https://ciaotool.ioarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/)

# 移除流动性「v3」教程 | 「EVM」使用教程 | CiaoTool

circle-check

**移除流动性 v3：**[https://bsc.ciaotool.io/swap/v3/remove-liquidity-v3arrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/swap/v3/remove-liquidity-v3)

circle-exclamation

必须确保余额充足**（钱包内至少有 0.03 BNB）**

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/remove-liquidity-v3#yi-chu-liu-dong-xing-xiang-xi-liu-cheng)

**🛠️ 移除流动性详细流程**

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/remove-liquidity-v3#id-1-lian-jie-qian-bao)

**1️⃣ 连接钱包**

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FNdlNqKeYrPleFWqlKF40%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2eccfc14&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/remove-liquidity-v3#id-2-shu-ru-yong-yu-yi-chu-liu-dong-xing-de-si-yao)

**2️⃣** 输入用于移除流动性的私钥

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2Fp6nIIrKtBcHbEb8o9ze8%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=aeb41112&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/remove-liquidity-v3#id-3-she-zhi-yi-chu-bi-li)

**3️⃣ 设置移除比例**

*   输入移除的流动性比例：自定义，最大为100%，点击Max即可。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FGLudfjoVp0YLIM2kwWZ9%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f43d49cc&sv=2)

circle-info

**关于比例：**假设池子都是您一个人加的， 那么这个百分比=池子的百分比。如果池子是多个人加的，就需要另外算的。比如，您本身占有池子份额的20%。那么您即便选择100%，整个池子也只是锁了20%的流动性而已。如果您选择20%，那么整个池子也就是锁了4%的流动性。

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/remove-liquidity-v3#id-4-gou-xuan-xu-yao-yi-chu-de-liu-dong-xing)

**4️⃣ 勾选需要移除的流动性**

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/remove-liquidity-v3#id-5-yi-chu-liu-dong-xing)

**5️⃣ 移除流动性**

*   确认信息无误后，点击开始交易。
    

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/remove-liquidity-v3#faq)

**FAQ**

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/remove-liquidity-v3#id-1.-wei-shen-me-che-chi-hui-shi-bai)

**1\. 为什么撤池会失败？**

*   check
    
    钱包内 BNB / WBNB 是否足够。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/remove-liquidity-v3#id-2.-che-chi-hou-dai-bi-hai-neng-jiao-yi-ma)

**2\. 撤池后代币还能交易吗？**

*   check
    
    如果全部移除是不能交易的，只是移除添加一部分是还能交易的。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/remove-liquidity-v3#id-3.-yi-chu-hui-shou-qu-fei-yong-ma)

**3\. 移除会收取费用吗？**

*   check
    
    会的，移除流动性是按次收费，每次0.024BNB

# Token 流动性该如何配置？ | 「EVM」使用教程 | CiaoTool

circle-check

**Solana 发币：**[https://ciaotool.io/zh-CN/token/createarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/zh-CN/token/create)

**Pump：**[https://ciaotool.io/zh-CN/pump/launch-and-buyarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/zh-CN/pump/launch-and-buy)

**Bonk：**[https://ciaotool.io/zh-CN/letsbonkZone/bundled-buyarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/zh-CN/letsbonkZone/bundled-buy)

circle-check

**BSC 发币：**[https://bsc.ciaotool.io/token/create-tokenarrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/token/create-token)

**Fourmeme：**[https://bsc.ciaotool.io/fourmeme/bnb/create-and-buyarrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/fourmeme/bnb/create-and-buy)

**Flap：**[https://bsc.ciaotool.io/flap/usd1/create-and-buyarrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/flap/usd1/create-and-buy)

circle-check

**Base 发币：**[https://base.ciaotool.io/token/create-tokenarrow-up-right](https://base.ciaotool.io/token/create-token)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/start/liquidity-configuration#wei-shen-me-liu-dong-xing-hen-guan-jian)

📈 为什么流动性很关键？

*   **交易顺畅度：**流动性直接影响滑点大小。流动性越低，单笔交易对价格的冲击越大，交易越不顺畅。
    
*   **价格稳定性：**更高的流动性能有效吸收买卖波动，提升价格稳定性，但同时也会带来更高的资金占用成本。
    
*   **操纵风险与匹配度**：流动性不足时，池子更容易被操纵；但流动性并非越多越好，过高的流动性还会放大潜在的无常损失。关键在于流动性配置是否与项目所处阶段相匹配。
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/start/liquidity-configuration#xian-que-ding-ni-de-liu-dong-xing-deng-ji)

📊 先确定你的流动性等级

无论在哪条链上发币，你都需要先判断项目所处的流动性等级，这会直接影响投资者预期和价格行为。

*   **极低流动性：**实验性项目或低成本 Meme，滑点高，极易被 bot 操纵。
    
*   **低流动性：**初期项目，有少量社区，但价格仍不稳定。
    
*   **中等流动性：**已有一定用户和交易频率，价格相对可控。
    
*   **高流动性**：成熟项目阶段，市场信任度明显提升。
    
*   **极高流动性：**资金雄厚或已验证成功的项目，几乎不易被操纵。
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/start/liquidity-configuration#bu-tong-qu-kuai-lian-de-liu-dong-xing-can-kao-qu-jian)

🔗 不同区块链的流动性参考区间

*   下表基于实际市场情况整理，用于帮助你快速定位合理区间（非硬性标准）：
    

流动性等级

Solana (Raydium)

Solana (PumpSwap)

BSC (BNB)

Base

极低

1 – 100 SOL

1 – 25 SOL

0.15 – 15 BNB

0.1 – 5 WETH

低

101 – 500 SOL

26 – 125 SOL

15 – 75 BNB

6 – 25 WETH

中等

501 – 2,000 SOL

126 – 500 SOL

75 – 300 BNB

26 – 100 WETH

高

2,001 – 10,000 SOL

501 – 2,500 SOL

300 – 1,500 BNB

101 – 500 WETH

极高

\>10,000 SOL

\>2,500 SOL

\>1,500 BNB

\>500 WETH

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FtLGXpKtBfoP1NuxWA1bj%2Fimage&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=261b0d5d&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/start/liquidity-configuration#liu-dong-xing-bu-zu-hui-dai-lai-na-xie-zhi-jie-wen-ti)

⚠️ 流动性不足会带来哪些直接问题？

*   **流动性不足的影响：**当流动性不足时，滑点会被显著放大，直接影响交易体验；同时，池子也更容易成为 bot 抢跑和拉砸的目标，增加市场风险。
    
*   **流动性管理的必要性：**即便通过提高流动性可以在一定程度上缓解上述问题，仍需关注无常损失，尤其是在价格波动剧烈的阶段。因此，流动性需要进行动态管理，而不是一次性投入。
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/start/liquidity-configuration#shi-fou-ying-gai-ba-quan-bu-token-dou-fang-jin-chi-zi)

🔎 是否应该把全部 Token 都放进池子？

*   通常不建议。更合理的做法是将 **40%–70%** 的 Token 用于流动性，其余部分留作**质押激励、生态奖励、社区运营或未来空投。**
    
*   这种结构既能保证交易深度，也能为项目后续发展保留空间。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2Fu4ZWnh1DG4rsIgk00oDW%2Fimage&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=66854c8d&sv=2)

Token Allocation 示例

* * *

流动性是 Token 的基础设施。在不同公链上，区间虽有差异，但核心逻辑一致：

> 足够的流动性 = 更稳定的价格 + 更高的市场信任 + 更低的操纵风险

提前规划流动性等级与 Token 分配，是避免项目在早期阶段“死在起跑线”的关键一步。

* * *

*   **Email**：[support@ciaotool.ioenvelope](mailto:support@ciaotool.io)
    
*   **官网**：[https://ciaotool.ioarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/)
    
*   **X（Twitter）**：[https://x.com/CiaoToolarrow-up-right](https://x.com/CiaoTool)
    
*   **Medium**： [https://medium.com/@ciaotoolarrow-up-right](https://medium.com/@ciaotool)

# 持币暴利分红创建教程 - BSC | 「EVM」使用教程 | CiaoTool

circle-check

**持币暴利分红**：[https://bsc.ciaotool.io/token/hold-ref-othersarrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/token/hold-ref-others)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/token/hold-ref-others#shen-me-shi-chi-bi-bao-li-fen-hong)

🛠 什么是持币暴利分红？

*   持有发行的代币即可分红其他代币，如 USDT、Doge、ETH 等。
    
*   分红比例按持币量计算，持币越多，分红越高。
    

**检测风险：**

*   该类型的代币创建后安全检测可能**存在风险**，如果您特别在意检测结果，可以选择创建标准代币，标准币没有任何风险。
    
*   如果您最终决定创建此类型的代币，则说明您**可以接受代币检测风险。**
    

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/token/hold-ref-others#ru-he-chuang-jian-chi-bi-bao-li-fen-hong-dai-bi)

🎯 **如何创建**持币暴利分红**代币？**

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/token/hold-ref-others#yi-lian-jie-qian-bao)

一、连接钱包

1.  **打开发币页面**：[https://bsc.ciaotool.io/token/hold-ref-othersarrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/token/hold-ref-others)
    
2.  点击右上角**【连接钱包】**，在弹窗中确认钱包地址
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2Fqi5y1ACYR5j7KFkJrdrN%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=cd88c116&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/token/hold-ref-others#er-shu-ru-dai-bi-ji-chu-xin-xi)

二、输入代币基础**信息**

*   **代币全称**：如 CiaoTool，支持中文、英文及中英混合
    
*   **代币符号**：如 C，在钱包和交易所显示
    
*   **发行总量**：固定总供应量，创建后不可增发
    
*   **精度**：代币最小单位，如 0.000001 精度为 6，默认一般为 18
    
*   **收币地址**：代币创建完成后接收代币的钱包地址 (可设置当前钱包地址）
    
*   **分红代币**：填写分红币合约地址（必须与BNB有交易对且流动性充足，即流动性较好的主流币，如果流动性过低，则可能**无法分红**）
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2Fdo9nny5YJzTo0WypGtUr%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=35e2ec4&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/token/hold-ref-others#san-mai-ru-shuil0x25)

三、买入税率**（0**≤x<**25%）**

*   **营销税率**：交易中指定额度的代币将会自动转入营销钱包中,用于项目方做其他营销
    
*   **分红税率**：交易中指定额度的代币会按持币比例分配给所有持币者,实现持币分红
    
*   **销毁税率**：交易中指定额度的代币将会被打入黑洞地址,变相实现通缩机制
    
*   **回流税率**：交易中指定额度的代币将会自动添加到流动池内,保证交易始终存在流动性
    
    ![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2086467048-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%252Fuploads%252F8kFEUjRTUd5G7YurxDAT%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D94afcde0-a85b-4036-8b3e-9eb56c09a123&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=54529eb3&sv=2)
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/token/hold-ref-others#si-mai-chu-shuil0x25)

四、卖出税率**（0**≤x<**25%）**

*   包括营销、分红、销毁、回流，与买入税率逻辑相同，只在卖出交易时生效
    
    ![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2086467048-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%252Fuploads%252FKlIfuQ2JrgwzCftGaPV1%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dfa8d8c22-63a5-458b-bfa7-4a46cb9acd56&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=cd782c6c&sv=2)
    

circle-exclamation

买入和卖出税率不能超过25%,交易总税率不能超过50%

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/token/hold-ref-others#wu-qi-ta-can-shu)

五、其他参数

*   **营销钱包**：接收营销税率对应的本币（可设置当前钱包）
    
*   **分红最小持币量**：设置最小持币量，低于门槛的地址无法获得分红。
    
*   **选择交易所**：PancakeSwap
    
*   **选择底池代币**：WBNB / USDT 等，后续添加流动性需使用同样代币
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FmsUjvkv9SMRi7dDPaoAM%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c26d89ff&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/token/hold-ref-others#liu-xiang-guan-gong-neng-kai-guan-can-shu)

六、相关功能开关参数

**1\. 手动开启交易**

*   check
    
    打开：添加池子后的首次交易需要在控制台手动开启
    
*   关闭：则添加流动性后立即可以进行交易
    

**2\. 税率开关**

*   check
    
    打开：创建后可手动调整买卖税率，但是买卖税率都需要为0≤25%
    
*   关闭：无法修改滑点，后期也不能再次开启
    

**3\. 黑名单功能**

*   check
    
    打开：可添加/解除黑名单，被拉黑地址无法转账或卖币
    
*   关闭：无法使用
    

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/token/hold-ref-others#chang-jian-wen-ti-faq)

❓常见问题 FAQ

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/token/hold-ref-others#id-1.-he-yue-quan-xian-neng-fou-diu)

**1\.** 合约权限能否丢？

*   check
    
    交易开盘后确认税率无误再丢权限，避免损失。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/token/hold-ref-others#id-2.-hei-dong-di-zhi-he-yue-di-zhi-hui-fen-hong-ma)

**2\.** 黑洞地址、合约地址会分红吗？

*   check
    
    不会，黑洞、代币合约、流动性池地址默认排除。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/token/hold-ref-others#id-3.-wei-shen-me-qian-bao-duo-chu-tracker-dai-bi)

**3\.** 为什么钱包多出 Tracker 代币？

*   check
    
    Tracker 用于记录分红权重，不可转账，否则分红会混乱。
    

**💬 如遇到问题？加入社群实时咨询**：[https://t.me/ciaotoolarrow-up-right](https://t.me/ciaotool)

*   **Email**：[support@ciaotool.ioenvelope](mailto:support@ciaotool.io)
    
*   **官网**：[https://ciaotool.ioarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/)
    
*   **X（Twitter）**：[https://x.com/CiaoToolarrow-up-right](https://x.com/CiaoTool)

*   **YouTube**：[https://www.youtube.com/@CiaoToolarrow-up-right](https://www.youtube.com/@CiaoTool)

# 多地址捆绑买入教程「v2 and v3」 | 「EVM」使用教程 | CiaoTool

circle-check

**多地址捆绑买入v2：**[https://bsc.ciaotool.io/swap/v2/multi-address-buy-v2arrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/swap/v2/multi-address-buy-v2)

**多地址捆绑买入v3：**[https://bsc.ciaotool.io/swap/v3/multi-address-buy-v3arrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/swap/v3/multi-address-buy-v3)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/v2-v3-multi-address-buy#duo-di-zhi-kun-bang-mai-ru-jiao-cheng)

🪜 多地址捆绑买入教程

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/v2-v3-multi-address-buy#id-1.-dao-ru-si-yao)

1\. 导入私钥

*   将用于支付市值操作手续费的钱包私钥导入。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FvVtAMFWuGgoNnCvYfjQj%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=74f8652&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/v2-v3-multi-address-buy#id-2.-dao-ru-bi-dui-di-zhi-huo-xuan-ze-bi-dui)

2\. 导入币对地址或选择币对

*   **v2-**在输入框中填写目标代币地址，或点击下拉菜单选择当前钱包持有的代币。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2Fgjluf7csT7zet2lhBxMc%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=385d8099&sv=2)

*   **v3-**在币对输入框中 **粘贴目标币对**。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2F2GyM9wN3dNywtprGN3hu%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=573b97e5&sv=2)

circle-exclamation

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/v2-v3-multi-address-buy#di-er-bu-cao-zuo-zhong-v2-he-v3-de-qu-bie-zai-yu-v2-shou-dong-xuan-ze-liang-zhong-dai-bi-v3-shu-ru-b)

第二步操作中v2和v3的区别在于：v2手动选择两种代币，v3输入币对地址。

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/v2-v3-multi-address-buy#id-3.-dao-ru-mai-ru-qian-bao-si-yao)

3\. 导入买入钱包私钥

*   选择批量导入方式，可以 **手动粘贴多个私钥**，也可以 **上传包含私钥的表格文件（**xls、xlsx格式**）**。
    
*   系统将自动识别每个钱包的 BNB 余额、TokenA余额、TokenB余额。
    

circle-info

注意：单次最多支持导入 **20 个地址**。

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/v2-v3-multi-address-buy#id-4.-she-zhi-mai-ru-can-shu)

4\. 设置买入参数

**配置方式：**

1.  为每个地址设置「买入金额」 ，单个地址无上限买入金额，刷新余额查看即可
    
2.  可选择刷新余额或调整买入比例
    
3.  系统将展示每个地址的状态 + 操作按钮
    

triangle-exclamation

💡 注意：买入地址的BNB余额必须大于 0.0008！

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FA0vQi2nE1C5RnB0jCbZO%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b7042b87&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/v2-v3-multi-address-buy#id-5.-kai-shi-jiao-yi)

5\. 开始交易

*   检查无误后，点击 **“开始交易”** 按钮。
    
*   系统会自动为每个钱包生成交易并执行捆绑买入操作。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2Fa4AbPzlrGYNhEhe3VOXX%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6ebc8f5a&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/v2-v3-multi-address-buy#chang-jian-wen-ti-faq)

❓ 常见问题 FAQ

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/v2-v3-multi-address-buy#id-1.-shen-me-shi-duo-di-zhi-kun-bang-mai-ru)

1\. 什么是多地址捆绑买入？

*   check
    
    答：指多个钱包同时买入同一代币，以批量执行交易，提高交易成功率与速度。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/v2-v3-multi-address-buy#id-2.-yi-ci-zui-duo-zhi-chi-ji-ge-qian-bao)

2\. 一次最多支持几个钱包？

*   check
    
    答：单次操作最多可导入 **20 个钱包地址** 进行同步买入。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/v2-v3-multi-address-buy#id-3.-wei-shen-me-mai-ru-di-zhi-de-bnb-yuebi-xu-da-yu-0.0008)

**3\.** 为什么买入地址的BNB余额必须大于 0.0008？

*   check
    
    答：每个钱包至少保留 0.0008 BNB 以上余额，以确保足够支付交易 Gas 费用。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/v2-v3-multi-address-buy#id-4.-dai-bi-di-zhi-shu-ru-cuo-wu-zen-me-ban)

4\. 代币地址输入错误怎么办？

*   check
    
    答：请在执行前确认代币合约地址正确无误。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/v2-v3-multi-address-buy#id-5.-shi-fou-zhi-chi-zi-ding-yi-mai-ru-jine)

5\. 是否支持自定义买入金额？

*   check
    
    答：支持。你可以为不同钱包单独设定买入金额，也可以统一设定同样的买入数额。
    

**💬 如遇到问题？加入社群实时咨询**：[https://t.me/ciaotoolarrow-up-right](https://t.me/ciaotool)

*   **Email**：[support@ciaotool.ioenvelope](mailto:support@ciaotool.io)
    
*   **官网**：[https://ciaotool.ioarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/)
    
*   **X（Twitter）**：[https://x.com/CiaoToolarrow-up-right](https://x.com/CiaoTool)
    
*   **Medium**： [https://medium.com/@ciaotoolarrow-up-right](https://medium.com/@ciaotool)
    
*   **Blog**：[https://www.ciaoailiquidity.com/zh/blogarrow-up-right](https://www.ciaoailiquidity.com/zh/blog)
    
*   **YouTube**：[https://www.youtube.com/@CiaoToolarrow-up-right](https://www.youtube.com/@CiaoTool)
    
*   **WhatsApp**：[https://whatsapp.com/channel/0029VbAuLrVAojYxRNw95W1Jarrow-up-right](https://whatsapp.com/channel/0029VbAuLrVAojYxRNw95W1J)

# 创建/添加流动性「v2」教程 | 「EVM」使用教程 | CiaoTool

circle-check

**创建流动性 v2：**[https://bsc.ciaotool.io/swap/v2/create-liquidity-v2arrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/swap/v2/create-liquidity-v2)

**添加流动性 v2：**[https://bsc.ciaotool.io/swap/v2/add-liquidity-v2arrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/swap/v2/add-liquidity-v2)

circle-info

如果你更偏好视频形式的学习，欢迎观看本教程

circle-exclamation

创建前必须确保余额充足**（钱包内至少有 0.03 BNB**）

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/create-add-liquidity-v2#chuang-jian-tian-jia-liu-dong-xing-xiang-xi-liu-cheng)

**🛠️ 创建/添加流动性详细流程**

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/create-add-liquidity-v2#id-1-lian-jie-qian-bao)

**1️⃣ 连接钱包**

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2F8AhGayayJ4AHNtEmNeFz%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7c71d944&sv=2)

*   输入用于创建/添加流动性的私钥
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2Fp6nIIrKtBcHbEb8o9ze8%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=aeb41112&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/create-add-liquidity-v2#id-2-xuan-ze-jia-chi-de-liang-zhong-dai-bi)

**2️⃣ 选择加池的两种代币**

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FW7W59pBfNoSt8Uw6eOR4%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e408dd41&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/create-add-liquidity-v2#id-3-tian-xie-jia-chi-shu-liang)

**3️⃣ 填写加池数量**

*   输入两种代币的数量。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FH7IlbzsmUqJZYYVZMFX5%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2568d044&sv=2)

circle-info

提示：请自行计算合适的比例后再创建流动性。

*   添加流动性时：会出现已经有的流动池详细，且价格固定，只需要输入TokanA的数量即可。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2F4sWWKGzF5KAuJ4ekH62p%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c17ff827&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/create-add-liquidity-v2#id-4-shou-quan-dai-bi)

**4️⃣ 授权代币**

*   第一次操作时，需要授权合约使用你的代币。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/create-add-liquidity-v2#id-5-chuang-jian-liu-dong-xing)

**5️⃣ 创建流动性**

*   检查无误后，点击“**开始交易”**按钮。
    

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/create-add-liquidity-v2#chang-jian-wen-ti-faq)

❓ 常见问题**FAQ**

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/create-add-liquidity-v2#id-1.-wei-shen-me-jia-chi-hui-shi-bai)

**1\. 为什么加池会失败？**

*   check
    
    钱包内 BNB /WBNB是否足够。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/create-add-liquidity-v2#id-2.-wo-chuang-jian-de-shi-wbnb-jiao-yi-dui-yong-hu-ke-yi-yong-usdt-mai-bi-ma)

**2\. 我创建的是 WBNB 交易对，用户可以用 USDT 买币吗？**

*   check
    
    可以的，即使你创建的是 WBNB 池：仍可用 USDT → BNB → 你的代币 链上交易是自动路由的，结果是相通的。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/create-add-liquidity-v2#id-3.-jia-chi-de-dai-bi-shu-liang-you-yao-qiu-ma)

**3\. 加池的代币数量有要求吗？**

*   check
    
    没有强制要求,你可以根据代币经济模型、想要的初始价格、市值目标、来灵活决定加池比例。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/create-add-liquidity-v2#id-4.-yu-gu-jia-ge-hou-mian-hui-bian-ma)

**4\. 预估价格后面会变吗？**

*   check
    
    会的，预估价格 = 上线初始价格，随着用户不断买卖，价格会实时变化，交易越多，价格波动越真实。
    

**💬 如遇到问题？加入社群实时咨询**：[https://t.me/ciaotoolarrow-up-right](https://t.me/ciaotool)

*   **Email**：[support@ciaotool.ioenvelope](mailto:support@ciaotool.io)
    
*   **官网**：[https://ciaotool.ioarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/)
    
*   **X（Twitter）**：[https://x.com/CiaoToolarrow-up-right](https://x.com/CiaoTool)
    
*   **Medium**： [https://medium.com/@ciaotoolarrow-up-right](https://medium.com/@ciaotool)
    
*   **Blog**：[https://www.ciaoailiquidity.com/zh/blogarrow-up-right](https://www.ciaoailiquidity.com/zh/blog)
    
*   **YouTube**：[https://www.youtube.com/@CiaoToolarrow-up-right](https://www.youtube.com/@CiaoTool)
    
*   **WhatsApp**：[https://whatsapp.com/channel/0029VbAuLrVAojYxRNw95W1Jarrow-up-right](https://whatsapp.com/channel/0029VbAuLrVAojYxRNw95W1J)

# 批量交易教程「v2 and v3」 | 「EVM」使用教程 | CiaoTool

circle-check

**批量交易 v2：**[https://bsc.ciaotool.io/swap/batch-swap-v2arrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/swap/batch-swap-v2)

**批量交易 v3：**[https://bsc.ciaotool.io/swap/v3/batch-swap-v3arrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/swap/v3/batch-swap-v3)

circle-exclamation

如果你更偏好视频形式的学习，欢迎观看本教程

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/batch-swap-v2-v3#ru-he-shi-yong-swap-pi-liang-jiao-yi)

✅ 如何使用Swap批量交易?

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/batch-swap-v2-v3#id-1.-dao-ru-qian-bao-si-yao)

1.导入钱包私钥

*   将用于支付操作手续费的钱包私钥导入（私钥需要与交易私钥不同）
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2Fxu5msyAHOnz1sPK6wO1X%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8b0e12db&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/batch-swap-v2-v3#id-1.-xuan-ze-dai-bi)

1\. 选择代币

*   在输入框中填写目标代币地址，或点击下拉菜单选择当前钱包持有的代币。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FeCTD2O8PWFE8g1saAeqr%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4c147172&sv=2)

*   快速切换交易买卖方向**（From**：支出的代币、**To**：获得的代币）
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FPRU1eLLTNlq3b5Yp1TQr%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5403c1d7&sv=2)

circle-info

注：v3的批量交易选择代币页面只需要导入币对地址即可

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FysDsibCeU4bd0NGpk81d%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b1902676&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/batch-swap-v2-v3#id-3.-she-zhi-jiao-yi-can-shu)

3\. 设置交易参数

*   选择交易数量模式（固定数量/固定留存/全部数量）
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FmQwuK9vpus7sbkN2c9Dh%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2bd62943&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/batch-swap-v2-v3#id-4.-dao-ru-qian-bao-si-yao)

4.导入钱包私钥

*   将用于支付市值操作手续费的钱包私钥导入。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FLU7TFMWuoT1dU49gjrOb%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9d38d2f9&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/batch-swap-v2-v3#id-5.-she-zhi-hua-dian-jiao-yi-su-du-yu-chao-shi-shi-jian-v3-de-pi-liang-jiao-yi-tiao-guo-gai-bu-zhou)

5\. 设置滑点、交易速度、与超时时间。（v3的批量交易跳过该步骤）

circle-info

**超时时间**指交易的最长等待时间，若在此时间内未完成，则可能导致交易失败。

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2F20ILBGYoKkt8imiouMBq%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d7170df1&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/batch-swap-v2-v3#id-6.-dao-ru-pi-liang-jiao-yi-de-qian-bao)

6\. 导入批量交易的钱包

*   可上传私钥文件导入
    

circle-info

每个交易的钱包中，需要有一些 BNB（至少0.0008 BNB） 用于支付交易 Gas.

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FmoeXNX0XG5tuNfs0jsJp%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8c6413a6&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/batch-swap-v2-v3#id-7.-kai-shi-jiao-yi)

7\. 开始交易

*   重新检查参数设置，无误后点击开始交易。
    
*   交易速度会受到链上拥堵情况影响，链上拥堵时可能交易速度较慢，还请您耐心等待。
    

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/batch-swap-v2-v3#chang-jian-wen-ti-faq)

❓常见问题 FAQ

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/batch-swap-v2-v3#id-1.-shen-me-shi-pi-liang-jiao-yi)

**1\. 什么是批量**交易**？**

*   check
    
    答：批量交易允许用户通过多个钱包地址同时发起代币交换交易，适用于刷量、控盘等多地址操作需求。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/batch-swap-v2-v3#id-2.-zhi-chi-na-xie-lei-xing-de-qian-bao)

**2\. 支持哪些类型的钱包？**

*   check
    
    答：支持导入私钥的钱包，也支持使用当前连接的钱包进行操作，可手动粘贴或上传 xls、xlsx格式文件。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/batch-swap-v2-v3#id-3.-shi-fou-zhi-chi-zi-ding-yi-swap-can-shu)

**3\. 是否支持自定义 Swap 参数？**

*   check
    
    答：支持。你可以设置每笔交易的 Swap 金额、超时时间、滑点等，灵活配置策略。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/batch-swap-v2-v3#id-4.-cao-zuo-shi-fou-an-quan-si-yao-hui-bei-shang-chuan-ma)

**4\. 操作是否安全？私钥会被上传吗？**

*   check
    
    答：安全。所有操作均在本地浏览器完成签名，私钥不会上传或存储至服务器，确保资产安全。
    

**💬 如遇到问题？加入社群实时咨询**：[https://t.me/ciaotoolarrow-up-right](https://t.me/ciaotool)

*   **Email**：[support@ciaotool.ioenvelope](mailto:support@ciaotool.io)
    
*   **官网**：[https://ciaotool.ioarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/)
    
*   **X（Twitter）**：[https://x.com/CiaoToolarrow-up-right](https://x.com/CiaoTool)
    
*   **Medium**： [https://medium.com/@ciaotoolarrow-up-right](https://medium.com/@ciaotool)
    
*   **Blog**：[https://www.ciaoailiquidity.com/zh/blogarrow-up-right](https://www.ciaoailiquidity.com/zh/blog)
    
*   **YouTube**：[https://www.youtube.com/@CiaoToolarrow-up-right](https://www.youtube.com/@CiaoTool)
    
*   **WhatsApp**：[https://whatsapp.com/channel/0029VbAuLrVAojYxRNw95W1Jarrow-up-right](https://whatsapp.com/channel/0029VbAuLrVAojYxRNw95W1J)
    

triangle-exclamation

# 创建/添加流动性「v3」教程 | 「EVM」使用教程 | CiaoTool

circle-check

**创建流动性 v2：**[https://bsc.ciaotool.io/swap/v3/create-liquidity-v3arrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/swap/v3/create-liquidity-v3)

**添加流动性 v2：**[https://bsc.ciaotool.io/swap/v3/add-liquidity-v3arrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/swap/v3/add-liquidity-v3)

circle-exclamation

创建前必须确保余额充足**（钱包内至少有 0.03 BNB）**

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/create-add-liquidity-v2-1#chuang-jian-tian-jia-liu-dong-xing-v3-xiang-xi-liu-cheng)

**🛠️ 创建/添加流动性v3详细流程**

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/create-add-liquidity-v2-1#id-1-lian-jie-qian-bao)

**1️⃣ 连接钱包**

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2F8AhGayayJ4AHNtEmNeFz%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7c71d944&sv=2)

*   输入用于创建/添加流动性的私钥
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2Fp6nIIrKtBcHbEb8o9ze8%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=aeb41112&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/create-add-liquidity-v2-1#id-2-xuan-ze-jia-chi-de-liang-zhong-dai-bi)

**2️⃣ 选择加池的两种代币**

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FFcslP8CSH9YAcMnLGWH2%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=dfbe1cf&sv=2)

circle-exclamation

添加流动性时：输入币对地址即可

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2F6liyVtfSkXWNzxboeJnH%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7747f57d&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/create-add-liquidity-v2-1#id-3-xuan-ze-shou-xu-fei-ji-bie)

**3️⃣ 选择手续费级别**

*   V3 的 LP 手续费不同于V2，不再是复利。
    
*   交易费用不同：V3有四种不同的交易费等级，最多可降低25倍交易费用；V2每一笔交易将支付0.25%手续费。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2Ftz5TOEaoz0lzKBQ28oPb%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c7365aa6&sv=2)

circle-info

Swap v3创建流动性滑点设置默认为1%

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/create-add-liquidity-v2-1#id-4-she-zhi-chu-shi-jia-ge-yu-jia-ge-qu-jian)

**4️⃣ 设置初始价格与价格区间**

1.区间大小決定收益高低 (LP 手续费收益、CAKE 收益皆适用)

*   越窄收益越高，无常损失越大
    
*   越宽收益越低，无常损失越小
    
*   全区间设置则类似于 V2 运作，收益将非常少
    

2.超出区间时

*   无收益
    
*   流动性仓位将变为单币
    
*   可以移除流动性并重新添加，或是等待价格重新回到区间内
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FKCiVPNtRpqyauuZgXEGX%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c4e7a943&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/create-add-liquidity-v2-1#id-5-tian-xie-jia-chi-shu-liang)

**5️⃣ 填写加池数量**

*   输入代币的数量。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2F8Zlmc9TNOTG6lH0PxPBv%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=36fa8fc7&sv=2)

circle-info

提示：请自行计算合适的比例后再创建流动性。

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/create-add-liquidity-v2-1#id-6-shou-quan-dai-bi)

6️⃣ **授权代币**

*   第一次操作时，需要授权合约使用你的代币。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/create-add-liquidity-v2-1#id-7-kai-shi-jiao-yi)

7️⃣ **开始交易**

*   检查无误后，点击 **“开始交易”** 按钮。
    

**💬 如遇到问题？加入社群实时咨询**：[https://t.me/ciaotoolarrow-up-right](https://t.me/ciaotool)

*   **Email**：[support@ciaotool.ioenvelope](mailto:support@ciaotool.io)
    
*   **官网**：[https://ciaotool.ioarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/)
    
*   **X（Twitter）**：[https://x.com/CiaoToolarrow-up-right](https://x.com/CiaoTool)
    
*   **Medium**： [https://medium.com/@ciaotoolarrow-up-right](https://medium.com/@ciaotool)
    
*   **Blog**：[https://www.ciaoailiquidity.com/zh/blogarrow-up-right](https://www.ciaoailiquidity.com/zh/blog)
    
*   **YouTube**：[https://www.youtube.com/@CiaoToolarrow-up-right](https://www.youtube.com/@CiaoTool)
    
*   **WhatsApp**：[https://whatsapp.com/channel/0029VbAuLrVAojYxRNw95W1Jarrow-up-right](https://whatsapp.com/channel/0029VbAuLrVAojYxRNw95W1J)
    

triangle-exclamation

CiaoTool 致力于提供便捷的工具服务，但不构成任何投资建议。平台内容可能根据产品迭代进行调整，敬请用户自行判断并留意更新。

[上一页创建流动性并捆绑买入「v2」教程chevron-left](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/create-liquidity-and-buy-v2)
[下一页移除流动性「v3」教程chevron-right](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/remove-liquidity-v3)

# BSC 中转转账教程 | 「EVM」使用教程 | CiaoTool

circle-check

**BSC 中转转账**：[https://bsc.ciaotool.io/transfer/relay-transferarrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/transfer/relay-transfer)

circle-exclamation

如果你更偏好视频形式的学习，欢迎观看本教程

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/transfer/relay-transfer#cao-zuo-bu-zhou)

🔗 **操作步骤**

triangle-exclamation

**转出钱包数量需要和目标钱包数量一致！**

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/transfer/relay-transfer#id-1.-xuan-ze-dai-bi-di-zhi)

**1\. 选择代币地址**

*   输入或选择需要发送的 BSC 代币合约地址。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FgD5FEZlKcauwwpyIKuFn%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=50da0a89&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/transfer/relay-transfer#id-2.-shang-chuan-fa-song-si-yao)

**2\. 上传发送私钥**

*   上传包含多个私钥的钱包文件（xls、xlsx格式），系统将识别来源钱包。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FEF41y8aHvR2FeHCoTBXK%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5c601e0&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/transfer/relay-transfer#id-3.-shang-chuan-jie-shou-di-zhi)

**3\. 上传接收地址**

*   上传接收地址列表，确保发送方和接收方数量一致（如10个地址发给10个接收地址）。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FHeK6LGgnDpFDh5LgIX2U%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=468a9ea6&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/transfer/relay-transfer#id-4.-she-zhi-zhuan-zhang-can-shu)

**4\. 设置转账参数**

1.  **全部数量**：把地址中持有的**全部代币数量**一次性转出。
    
2.  **固定数量**：为每个目标地址**分配相同数量**的代币。
    
3.  **固定留存：**在操作时**保留钱包中一定数量**的代币，不全部转出。
    
4.  **自定义数量(点击输入)：**手动输入每个地址应获得的具体数量，可**灵活设置不同分配比例**。
    
5.  **中转次数：**在一次完整转账过程中，**资金经过多少次中间地址转移**后，才到达最终接收地址。
    

triangle-exclamation

中转次数越多，代表资金路径越复杂

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FaTokpxrjiSH2rxhyMEe4%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5cad0719&sv=2)

*   自定义输入转账数量可上传文件或手动换行输入
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FW2qhRAwRxX26i9mAYugV%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d618ff8d&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/transfer/relay-transfer#id-5.-sheng-cheng-zhong-zhuan-qian-bao)

**5\. 生成中转钱包**

*   系统自动生成中间跳转地址，用于中转操作（隐藏转账路径）。
    
*   查看钱包资金状态
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2F2yacbeUozHwk8WVzqPAP%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d96c115f&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/transfer/relay-transfer#id-6.-zhi-xing-fa-song)

**6\. 执行发送**

*   一键确认操作并签名，系统将自动完成中转转账交易。
    

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/transfer/relay-transfer#chang-jian-wen-ti-faq)

❓ 常见问题 FAQ

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/transfer/relay-transfer#id-1.-shen-me-shi-bsc-zhong-zhuan-zhuan-zhang)

**1\. 什么是 BSC** 中转转账**？**

*   check
    
    答：为用户提供一种更隐蔽和安全的转账方式。用户可以有效隐藏转账路径，从而提高资金转账的隐私性和安全性。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/transfer/relay-transfer#id-2.-mei-ge-di-zhi-ke-yi-she-zhi-bu-tong-jinema)

**2\. 每个地址可以设置不同金额吗？**

*   check
    
    答：支持。可在上传文件中自定义每笔交易的金额。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/transfer/relay-transfer#id-3.-xi-tong-shi-fou-bao-cun-wo-de-si-yao)

**3\. 系统是否保存我的私钥？**

*   check
    
    答：不会。所有签名操作仅在本地浏览器完成，保障私钥安全。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/transfer/relay-transfer#id-4.-zhi-chi-duo-shao-ge-di-zhi-jin-xing-zhong-zhuan-zhuan-zhang)

**4\. 支持多少个地址进行**中转**转账？**

*   check
    
    答：地址越多，中转消耗的时间就越久，但是隐私和安全性久越高，理论上没有数量限制，取决于网络以及服务器，适合中大型批量操作。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/transfer/relay-transfer#id-5.-shi-fou-ke-yi-dao-ru-xlsxlsx-ge-shi-wen-jian)

**5\. 是否可以导入**xls、xlsx格式**文件？**

*   check
    
    答：可以。发送私钥和接收地址都支持 xls、xlsx格式导入，提高效率。
    

**💬 如遇到问题？加入社群实时咨询**：[https://t.me/ciaotoolarrow-up-right](https://t.me/ciaotool)

*   **Email**：[support@ciaotool.ioenvelope](mailto:support@ciaotool.io)
    
*   **官网**：[https://ciaotool.ioarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/)
    
*   **X（Twitter）**：[https://x.com/CiaoToolarrow-up-right](https://x.com/CiaoTool)
    
*   **Medium**： [https://medium.com/@ciaotoolarrow-up-right](https://medium.com/@ciaotool)
    
*   **Blog**：[https://www.ciaoailiquidity.com/zh/blogarrow-up-right](https://www.ciaoailiquidity.com/zh/blog)
    
*   **YouTube**：[https://www.youtube.com/@CiaoToolarrow-up-right](https://www.youtube.com/@CiaoTool)
    
*   **WhatsApp**：[https://whatsapp.com/channel/0029VbAuLrVAojYxRNw95W1Jarrow-up-right](https://whatsapp.com/channel/0029VbAuLrVAojYxRNw95W1J)
    

triangle-exclamation

CiaoTool 致力于提供便捷的工具服务，但不构成任何投资建议。平台内容可能根据产品迭代进行调整，敬请用户自行判断并留意更新。
