# Fourmeme 市值管理教程 | 「EVM」使用教程 | CiaoTool

circle-check

**Fourmeme市值管理：**[https://bsc.ciaotool.io/fourmeme/market-making-managearrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/fourmeme/market-making-manage)

circle-exclamation

如果你更偏好视频形式的学习，欢迎观看本教程

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/fourmeme/market-making-manage#ru-he-shi-yong-fourmeme-shi-zhi-guan-li-gong-ju)

✅ 如何使用Fourmeme 市值管理工具：


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/fourmeme/market-making-manage#id-1.-dao-ru-qian-bao-si-yao)

1\. 导入钱包私钥

将用于支付市值操作手续费的钱包私钥导入工具中

circle-info

请务必确保私钥安全，不要随意外泄。

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/fourmeme/market-making-manage#id-2.-she-zhi-dai-bi)

2\. 设置代币

*   在输入框中填写目标代币地址，或点击下拉菜单选择当前钱包持有的代币。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FeCTD2O8PWFE8g1saAeqr%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4c147172&sv=2)

*   快速切换交易买卖方向**（From**：支出的代币、**To**：获得的代币）
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FPRU1eLLTNlq3b5Yp1TQr%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5403c1d7&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/fourmeme/market-making-manage#id-3.-she-zhi-jiao-yi-can-shu)

3\. 设置交易参数

*   **设置交易间隔（单位：秒 ⏱️）**
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FGpwzdbBRbgx0m03LTsug%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=27be84b8&sv=2)

*   **选择交易数量模式（固定数量/固定留存/全部数量）**
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2F6dFmbG36cFoLtZPJorTH%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9f189592&sv=2)

*   **设置滑点**
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FIDWiB101Ryw7YlgkC1Rt%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6f77a9df&sv=2)

*   **设置停止方式与循环执行次数**
    

*   check
    
    按执行次数停止：控制买卖力度与节奏
    
*   check
    
    按价格区间停止；避免超买或砸穿价格带
    

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/fourmeme/market-making-manage#id-4.-dao-ru-pi-liang-jiao-yi-de-qian-bao)

4.导入批量交易的钱包

*   可上传私钥文件导入和手动输入
    

circle-info

每个交易的钱包中，需要有一些（0.0008） BNB 用于支付交易 GAS

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FshCZsfKxtWOcLD4OU47p%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9a32e854&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/fourmeme/market-making-manage#id-5.-zui-zhong-que-ren-bing-zhi-xing)

5\. 最终确认并执行

*   执行前请检查： ✅ 买卖方向 ✅ 代币是否正确 ✅ 滑点是否合理 ✅ 停止条件是否设好
    
    确认后点击 → **开始执行**
    

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/fourmeme/market-making-manage#chang-jian-wen-ti-faq)

❓常见问题 FAQ

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/fourmeme/market-making-manage#id-1.-yun-xing-zhong-neng-zan-ting-ma)

**1\.** 运行中能暂停吗？

*   check
    
    答：可以，随时可暂停或立即终止，不影响资产储备。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/fourmeme/market-making-manage#id-2.-hua-dian-tai-di-hui-dao-zhi-shen-me)

**2\.** 滑点太低会导致什么？

*   check
    
    答：成交失败/无法完成买卖/交易频繁报错，尤其是低池深代币必须提高滑点。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/fourmeme/market-making-manage#id-3.-wei-shen-me-shi-zhi-guan-li-jian-yi-shi-yong-duo-qian-bao)

**3\.** 为什么市值管理建议使用多钱包？

*   check
    
    答：分散持仓、做盘痕迹更自然、盘口深度更真实、避免“一眼控盘”。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/fourmeme/market-making-manage#id-4.-gu-ding-liu-cun-mo-shi-de-yong-tu)

**4\.** 固定留存模式的用途？

*   check
    
    答：保持每个钱包持仓结构不变，对外看更自然，减少恐慌性抛压。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/fourmeme/market-making-manage#id-5.-chang-jian-zhi-xing-shi-bai-yuan-yin)

**5\.** 常见执行失败原因？

*   check
    
    答：滑点太低、余额不足、RPC 拥堵、Gas费用不足。
    

**💬 如遇到问题？加入社群实时咨询**：[https://t.me/ciaotoolarrow-up-right](https://t.me/ciaotool)

*   **Email**：[support@ciaotool.ioenvelope](mailto:support@ciaotool.io)
    
*   **官网**：[https://ciaotool.ioarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/)

*   **YouTube**：[https://www.youtube.com/@CiaoToolarrow-up-right](https://www.youtube.com/@CiaoTool)
    
*   **WhatsApp**：[https://whatsapp.com/channel/0029VbAuLrVAojYxRNw95W1Jarrow-up-right](https://whatsapp.com/channel/0029VbAuLrVAojYxRNw95W1J)

# Batch One-to-Multi - Universal Tutorial | 「EVM」Tutorial | CiaoTool

circle-check

**BSC** **Batch One-to-Multi:** [https://bsc.ciaotool.io/transfer/one-to-many-multiarrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/transfer/one-to-many-multi)

**Base Batch One-to-Multi:** [https://base.ciaotool.io/transfer/one-to-many-multiarrow-up-right](https://base.ciaotool.io/transfer/one-to-many-multi)

**X Layer Batch One-to-Multi:** [https://xlayer.ciaotool.io/transfer/one-to-many-multiarrow-up-right](https://xlayer.ciaotool.io/transfer/one-to-many-multi)

**IoTeX Batch One-to-Multi:** [https://iotex.ciaotool.io/transfer/one-to-many-multarrow-up-right](https://iotex.ciaotool.io/transfer/one-to-many-multi)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/multisender/one-to-many-multi#batch-one-to-multi-transfer-tutorial)

📘 **Batch One-to-Multi** Transfer Tutorial

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/multisender/one-to-many-multi#id-1.-connect-wallet)

**1\.** Connect Wallet

*   Connect a wallet that supports the EVM chain.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FcL6r1KVJmw4jLFWVpQbl%2Fblobs%2FKmguytDSQtWizWu9p8EU%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fd544895&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/multisender/one-to-many-multi#id-2.-click-add-page)

**2\. Click "Add Page"**

*   Create a page for each Batch One-to-Multi transfer task (customize transfer addresses and amounts).
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F467813208-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcL6r1KVJmw4jLFWVpQbl%252Fuploads%252F2ExfVVOHYeujJJui3hwv%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da0d2393b-696a-41d1-b2e2-e842411085aa&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=49b56c1d&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/multisender/one-to-many-multi#id-3.-fill-in-parameters-for-each-page)

**3\. Fill in Parameters for Each Page**

*   Select token address, input recipient addresses and amounts.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FcL6r1KVJmw4jLFWVpQbl%2Fblobs%2F83b1jEEMZJpj74Xv28KD%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f7f64264&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/multisender/one-to-many-multi#id-4.-click-refresh-balance)

**4\.** Click "Refresh Balance"

*   View the current wallet balance required for each page.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FcL6r1KVJmw4jLFWVpQbl%2Fblobs%2FmrqjFY4JKCOan2YpHtir%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7c38076&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/multisender/one-to-many-multi#id-5.-click-one-click-execute)

**5\. Click "One-Click Execute"**

*   The system will automatically process batch transfer operations page by page, improving execution efficiency.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F467813208-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcL6r1KVJmw4jLFWVpQbl%252Fuploads%252FsQZ3lr2loRZDr2KiW1B9%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D36a34910-8fbd-4e1a-a102-5cd0005d50ad&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d714ade5&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/multisender/one-to-many-multi#frequently-asked-questions-faq)

❓Frequently Asked Questions (FAQ)

**1\. What is Batch One-to-Multi Transfer?**

*   check
    
    **Answer**：Batch One-to-Multi Transfer is a method of combining multiple One-to-Multi transfer tasks and executing them together, suitable for complex fund distribution scenarios.
    

**2\. How many pages can I add at once?**

*   check
    
    **Answer**：The system defaults to support adding multiple transfer pages. The specific number depends on device performance and page complexity.
    

**3\. Can each page use different tokens?**

*   check
    
    **Answer**：Yes. Each page can set independent tokens and recipient addresses.
    

**4\. Can I pause or cancel after clicking "One-Click Execute"?**

*   check
    
    **Answer**：The operation cannot be interrupted during execution. Please ensure parameters are correct before proceeding.
    

**5\. Does it support importing recipient address files?**

*   check
    
    **Answer**：Yes. Each page can upload a recipient address xls, xlsx file for quick import of large batches of addresses.

❓常见问题（FAQ）

**1\. 什么是批量一转多？**

*   check
    
    **答**：批量一转多是将多个一对多转账任务组合在一起统一执行的方式，适合复杂资金分发场景。
    

**2\. 一次最多能添加几个页面？**

*   check
    
    **答**：系统默认支持添加多个转账页面，具体数量取决于设备性能与页面复杂度。
    

**3\. 每个页面是否可以使用不同的代币？**

*   check
    
    **答**：可以。每个页面可设置独立的代币和接收地址。
    

**4\. 点击「一键执行」后可以暂停或取消吗？**

*   check
    
    **答**：执行过程中不可中断，请在确认参数无误后再操作。
    

**5\. 是否支持导入接收地址文件？**

*   check
    
    **答**：支持。每个页面都可上传接收地址xls、xlsx格式文件，便于快速导入大批量地址。

# How Should Token Liquidity Be Allocated? | 「EVM」Tutorial | CiaoTool

circle-check

**Solana 发币：**[https://ciaotool.io/zh-CN/token/createarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/zh-CN/token/create)

**Pump：**[https://ciaotool.io/zh-CN/pump/launch-and-buyarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/zh-CN/pump/launch-and-buy)

**Bonk：**[https://ciaotool.io/zh-CN/letsbonkZone/bundled-buyarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/zh-CN/letsbonkZone/bundled-buy)

circle-check

**BSC 发币：**[https://bsc.ciaotool.io/token/create-tokenarrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/token/create-token)

**Fourmeme：**[https://bsc.ciaotool.io/fourmeme/bnb/create-and-buyarrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/fourmeme/bnb/create-and-buy)

**Flap：**[https://bsc.ciaotool.io/flap/usd1/create-and-buyarrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/flap/usd1/create-and-buy)

circle-check

**Base 发币：**[https://base.ciaotool.io/token/create-tokenarrow-up-right](https://base.ciaotool.io/token/create-token)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/quick-start/liquidity-configuration#why-is-liquidity-so-important)

🔑 Why Is Liquidity So Important?

*   **Trading Smoothness**: Liquidity directly affects slippage. The lower the liquidity, the greater the price impact of a single trade, resulting in a less smooth trading experience.
    
*   **Price Stability**: Higher liquidity can better absorb buy and sell pressure, improving price stability, but it also comes with higher capital lock-up costs.
    
*   **Manipulation Risk & Fit**: When liquidity is insufficient, pools become easier to manipulate. However, more liquidity is not always better—excessive liquidity can increase potential impermanent loss. The key is whether the liquidity configuration matches the project’s current stage.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/quick-start/liquidity-configuration#first-define-your-liquidity-tier)

📊 First, Define Your Liquidity Tier

Regardless of which blockchain you launch on, you should first identify your project’s liquidity tier. This choice directly affects investor perception and price behavior.

*   **Very Low Liquidity:** Experimental projects or low-budget memes; high slippage and extremely vulnerable to bots.
    
*   **Low Liquidity:** Early-stage projects with a small community; price stability is still limited.
    
*   **Moderate Liquidity:** Projects with a growing user base and regular trading activity; prices are more controlled.
    
*   **High Liquidity:** Mature-stage projects; market confidence improves significantly.
    
*   **Very High Liquidity:** Well-funded or proven projects; manipulation becomes difficult.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/quick-start/liquidity-configuration#liquidity-reference-ranges-by-blockchain)

🔗 Liquidity Reference Ranges by Blockchain

The table below summarizes commonly observed liquidity ranges based on real market conditions. These are **reference benchmarks**, not strict rules.

Liquidity Tier

SOL (Raydium)

SOL (PumpSwap)

BSC (BNB)

Base

Very Low

1 – 100 SOL

1 – 25 SOL

0.15 – 15 BNB

0.1 – 5 WETH

Low

101 – 500 SOL

26 – 125 SOL

15 – 75 BNB

6 – 25 WETH

Moderate

501 – 2,000 SOL

126 – 500 SOL

75 – 300 BNB

26 – 100 WETH

High

2,001 – 10,000 SOL

501 – 2,500 SOL

300 – 1,500 BNB

101 – 500 WETH

Very High

\>10,000 SOL

\>2,500 SOL

\>1,500 BNB

\>500 WETH

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FcL6r1KVJmw4jLFWVpQbl%2Fblobs%2FtpRgS9nlqSNCwqFLpUPS%2Fimage&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ff3cd902&sv=2)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/quick-start/liquidity-configuration#what-problems-does-insufficient-liquidity-cause)

⚠️ What Problems Does Insufficient Liquidity Cause?

*   **Impact of Insufficient Liquidity**: When liquidity is low, slippage increases significantly, directly degrading the trading experience. At the same time, liquidity pools become more vulnerable to bot front-running and pump-and-dump attacks, raising overall market risk.
    
*   **The Need for Active Liquidity Management**: While increasing liquidity can help mitigate these issues to some extent, impermanent loss must still be considered—especially during periods of high price volatility. Therefore, liquidity should be managed dynamically rather than deployed as a one-time allocation.
    

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/quick-start/liquidity-configuration#should-you-allocate-100-of-tokens-to-the-liquidity-pool)

🔎 Should You Allocate 100% of Tokens to the Liquidity Pool?

*   Generally, no. A healthier approach is to allocate **40%–70%** of the total token supply to liquidity, while reserving the remainder for **staking incentives, ecosystem rewards, community growth, or future airdrops**.
    
*   This structure ensures sufficient market depth while preserving long-term flexibility for the project.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FcL6r1KVJmw4jLFWVpQbl%2Fblobs%2FN79FUb8CBkaNaXfqFKYj%2Fimage&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c31e08fa&sv=2)

*   Liquidity is core infrastructure for any token. Although specific ranges vary across blockchains, the underlying principle remains the same:
    

> **Adequate liquidity** = more stable prices + stronger market confidence + lower manipulation risk

Carefully planning your liquidity tier and token allocation is one of the most important steps to avoid failing at the very beginning.

* * *

![Page cover](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252FwsnXY0ZWLI3UUnNLSjyH%252F1234.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D79554360-9207-4350-a0d3-77c165af8323&width=1248&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ff37598a&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol#cong-fa-bi-dao-guan-li-ciaotool-yi-zhan-gao-ding)

🚀 从发币到管理，CiaoTool 一站搞定

*   平台集成了包括代币一键发射、批量转账、冷分仓、狙击保护、流动性控制等核心功能，涵盖从代币创建、部署、分发到管理的完整流程，用户无需编写任何代码，即可高效完成复杂的链上操作。即使是 Web3 新手，也能通过 CiaoTool 的可视化界面，快速掌握加密资产的发行与运营。
    
*   我们在乎用户的每一个需求和问题。未来平台也将根据社区反馈，持续拓展功能模块。

**🔗 深度适配 Solana，生态模块强力协同**

# 多功能代币创建教程 - BSC | 「EVM」使用教程 | CiaoTool

circle-check

**多功能代币**：[https://bsc.ciaotool.io/token/simple-controlarrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/token/simple-control)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/token/simple-control#shen-me-shi-duo-gong-neng-dai-bi)

🛠 什么是多功能代币？

多功能代币是指包含多种可选功能的智能合约集合体，例如增发代币、交易暂停、黑名单管理、最大持币量限制等。这类代币可以让用户根据需求灵活测试和使用不同功能。

**检测风险提醒**：

*   创建多功能代币后可能存在安全检测风险。如果你对检测结果非常在意，可以选择创建标准代币，标准币不存在风险。
    
*   创建此类型代币意味着你接受高风险检测结果。部分检测平台可以在权限丢弃后复查，从而去掉风险提示。
    

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/token/simple-control#ru-he-chuang-jian-duo-gong-neng-dai-bi)

🪙 如何创建多功能代币？

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/token/simple-control#yi-lian-jie-qian-bao)

一、连接钱包

1.  打开发币页面：[https://bsc.ciaotool.io/token/simple-controlarrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/token/simple-control)
    
2.  点击右上角【连接钱包】，在弹窗中确认钱包授权即可。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FCCBTK81ESCVaaITuTTi4%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=64cb8462&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/token/simple-control#er-shu-ru-dai-bi-ji-chu-xin-xi)

二、输入代币基础**信息**

*   **代币全称**：如 CiaoTool，支持中文、英文及中英混合
    
*   **代币符号**：如 C，在钱包和交易所显示
    
*   **发行总量**：固定总供应量，创建后不可增发
    
*   **精度（Decimals）**：代币最小单位，如 0.000001 精度为 6，默认一般为 18
    
*   **收币地址**：代币创建完成后接收代币的钱包地址 (可设置当前钱包地址）
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2Ff3h0HjJC7QsZwlcQL5LB%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=c5210af&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/token/simple-control#san-xiang-guan-can-shu)

三、相关参数

**1\. 增发代币：**

*   选中可通过**控制台**增发/铸造代币，不选则无法使用增发功能
    

circle-info

增发可发送到指定地址

**2\. 暂停交易**

*   选中可以**暂停或开启**全部的转账和交易，不选则无法使用该功能
    

**3\. 黑名单功能**

*   选中可可拉黑部分钱包地址令其无法交易，不选则无法使用该功能
    

circle-info

注：此开关关闭后无法再次开启

**4\. 最大持币量限制**

*   选中：可设置单个钱包最大持有代币数量，不选则无法使用此功能
    

circle-info

注：此开关关闭后无法再次开启

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FU5ZlkiHCFHnjBEKzpJQy%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=66b21561&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/token/simple-control#si-wan-cheng-chuang-jian)

四、完成创建

1\. 确认相关参数是否填写正确

2.确认无误后点击**创建合约**

circle-info

注：如果创建过程中未成功请及时截图联系我们，如果创建成功未显示请自行添加到钱包**（参考如何添加代币到钱包）**

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/token/simple-control#wu-kong-zhi-tai-shi-yong-shuo-ming)

五、控制台使用说明

*   成功创建代币后，可在控制台管理各项功能：
    

**1\. 权限控制**

*   **转让所有权**：将合约权限转移给其他地址（需通过控制台链接操作）
    
*   **放弃所有权**：权限丢至黑洞，永远无法恢复
    

**2\. 交易控制**

*   **暂停交易**：开启后，非白名单地址无法转账或买卖代币
    
*   **修改持币限制**：调整单个钱包最大持有量
    
*   **关闭持币限制**：放弃限制，钱包持币无限制
    
*   **设置黑名单**：批量添加或移除黑名单
    
*   **设置全局白名单**：该地址不受持币上限或暂停交易影响
    

**3\. 代币控制**

*   **增发代币**：手动增发代币
    
*   **提取合约内代币**：提取合约内存留的 WBNB 和本币
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/token/simple-control#zhu-yi-shi-xiang)

⚠️ 注意事项

1.  **无法创建流动性：**如果钱包持币限制为 100 枚，而创建池子时添加了 101 枚，则会失败。 解决方法：先创建 99 枚代币池，将池子地址加入白名单，再增加池子数量。
    
2.  **暂停交易期间白名单无法买币：**因为暂停交易时，池子地址无法转账。需将池子地址加入白名单，才能继续买卖。
    
3.  **正常交易期间用户无法卖币：**如果池子地址内代币数量达到持仓上限，需提高持仓上限或加入白名单，用户才能继续卖币。
    

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/token/simple-control#chang-jian-wen-ti-faq)

❓ 常见问题 FAQ

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/token/simple-control#id-1.-duo-gong-neng-dai-bi-an-quan-ma)

**1\. 多功能代币安全吗？**

*   check
    
    多功能代币功能丰富，但安全检测可能存在风险。标准代币不会存在风险。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/token/simple-control#id-2.-chuang-jian-hou-neng-xiu-gai-gong-neng-ma)

**2\. 创建后能修改功能吗？**

*   check
    
    部分功能如权限丢弃后无法修改，需谨慎操作。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/token/simple-control#id-3.-hei-ming-dan-shi-fou-ying-xiang-fen-hong-huo-jiao-yi)

**3\. 黑名单是否影响分红或交易？**

*   check
    
    被拉入黑名单的地址无法转账或卖币，但其他正常地址不受影响。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/token/simple-control#id-4.-ru-he-guan-li-dai-bi-gong-neng)

**4\. 如何管理代币功能？**

*   check
    
    可进入控制台进行权限、交易、代币控制的管理操作。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/token/simple-control#id-5.-liu-dong-xing-tian-jia-shi-bai-zen-me-ban)

**5\. 流动性添加失败怎么办？**

*   check
    
    检查钱包持币上限，确保池子地址在白名单内，并符合持币限制。

# EVM Multi-Chain Universal Operation Guide (Must Read) | 「EVM」Tutorial | CiaoTool

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/quick-start/evm-multi-chain-universal-operation-guide-must-read#why-is-the-tutorial-universal)

💡 **Why is the tutorial universal?**

*   Most screenshots may use **BSC (BNB Smart Chain)** for demonstration purposes (faster transactions and lower gas fees).
    

In actual usage:

*   **Same Interface:** The token creation interface on Base, IoTeX, and X Layer is identical to BSC.
    
*   **Same Functions:** Token launch, airdrops, fund collection, and other operations follow the same logic.
    
*   **Only Difference:** You need to switch networks in your wallet and prepare the corresponding gas token (such as BNB, IOTX, or ETH).
    

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/quick-start/evm-multi-chain-universal-operation-guide-must-read#core-step-switching-networks-important)

⚙️ **Core Step: Switching Networks (Important)**

*   **Select Target Network:** Choose BSC, IoTeX, Base, or X Layer on the platform.
    
*   **Connect Wallet:** Click **Connect Wallet** in the top-right corner.
    
*   **Automatic Refresh & Sync:**
    
    *   The current chain indicator updates automatically.
        
    *   The gas token symbol updates accordingly (e.g., BNB → IOTX / ETH).
        
    

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/quick-start/evm-multi-chain-universal-operation-guide-must-read#choose-your-chain-enter-the-dedicated-portal)

🌐 **Choose Your Chain: Enter the Dedicated Portal**

Access

🔶 BNB Chain (BSC)

Enter BSC Hub

🟠 IoTeX

✅ Stable

Enter IoTeX Hub

🔵 Base Chain

Enter Base Hub

# 多地址捆绑卖出-BNB/USD1教程 | 「EVM」使用教程 | CiaoTool

circle-check

**FourMeme多地址捆绑卖出-BNB：**[https://bsc.ciaotool.io/fourmeme/bnb/multi-address-sellarrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/fourmeme/bnb/multi-address-sell)

circle-check

**FourMeme多地址捆绑卖出-USD1:** [https://bsc.ciaotool.io/fourmeme/usd1/multi-address-sellarrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/fourmeme/usd1/multi-address-sell)

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/fourmeme/multi-address-sell#duo-di-zhi-kun-bang-mai-chu-jiao-cheng)

🪜 多地址捆绑卖出教程


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/fourmeme/multi-address-sell#di-yi-bu-dao-ru-si-yao)

🧩 第一步：导入私钥

*   手动粘贴私钥，粘贴完成后会显示当前钱包的余额，可刷新余额。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2F6V9nhvX1IejVTKNhhv3d%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6a7f6cf2&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/fourmeme/multi-address-sell#di-er-bu-dao-ru-dai-bi-he-yue-di-zhi)

🌐 第二步：导入代币合约地址

*   在代币输入框中 **粘贴目标代币的合约地址**。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FsFsc7Pp1ZfvAtvcTcmEZ%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5fd6f5c4&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/fourmeme/multi-address-sell#di-san-bu-dao-ru-mai-chu-qian-bao-si-yao)

🏷 第三步：导入卖出钱包私钥

*   选择批量导入方式，可以 **手动粘贴多个私钥**，也可以 **上传包含私钥的表格文件（**xls、xlsx格式**）**。
    
*   系统将自动识别每个钱包的 BNB 余额与授权状态。
    

circle-info

注意：单次最多支持导入 **20 个钱包地址**。

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/fourmeme/multi-address-sell#di-si-bu-she-zhi-mai-chu-can-shu)

💰 第四步：设置卖出参数

**配置方式：**

1.  为每个地址设置「卖出金额」 ，单个地址无上限卖出金额，刷新余额查看即可
    
2.  可选择刷新余额
    
3.  系统将展示每个地址的状态 + 操作按钮
    

triangle-exclamation

💡 注意：卖出地址的BNB余额必须大于 0.0008！

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FzIHs70zkmBK1u9QUSyTH%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5475a095&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/fourmeme/multi-address-sell#di-wu-bu-zhi-xing-mai-chu-cao-zuo)

🛠 第五步：执行卖出操作

*   点击 **“执行（代币**卖出**）”** 按钮。
    
*   系统会自动为每个钱包生成交易并执行捆绑卖出操作。
    
*   执行完成后，可实时查看各钱包的卖出状态
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2Fa4AbPzlrGYNhEhe3VOXX%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6ebc8f5a&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/fourmeme/multi-address-sell#chang-jian-wen-ti-faq)

❓ 常见问题 FAQ

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/fourmeme/multi-address-sell#id-1.-shen-me-shi-duo-di-zhi-kun-bang-mai-chu)

1\. 什么是多地址捆绑卖出？

*   check
    
    答：指多个钱包同时卖出同一代币，以批量执行交易，提高交易成功率与速度。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/fourmeme/multi-address-sell#id-2.-yi-ci-zui-duo-zhi-chi-ji-ge-qian-bao)

2\. 一次最多支持几个钱包？

*   check
    
    答：单次操作最多可导入 **20 个钱包地址** 进行同步卖出。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/fourmeme/multi-address-sell#id-3.-wei-shen-me-mai-chu-di-zhi-de-bnb-yuebi-xu-da-yu-0.0008)

**3\.** 为什么卖出地址的BNB余额必须大于 0.0008？

*   check
    
    答：每个钱包至少保留 0.0008 BNB 以上余额，以确保足够支付交易 Gas 费用。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/fourmeme/multi-address-sell#id-4.-dai-bi-di-zhi-shu-ru-cuo-wu-zen-me-ban)

4\. 代币地址输入错误怎么办？

*   check
    
    答：请在执行前确认代币合约地址正确无误。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/fourmeme/multi-address-sell#id-5.-shi-fou-zhi-chi-zi-ding-yi-mai-chu-jine)

5\. 是否支持自定义卖出金额？

*   check
    
    答：支持。你可以为不同钱包单独设定卖出金额，也可以统一设定同样的卖出数额。
    

**💬 如遇到问题？加入社群实时咨询**：[https://t.me/ciaotoolarrow-up-right](https://t.me/ciaotool)

*   **Email**：[support@ciaotool.ioenvelope](mailto:support@ciaotool.io)
    
*   **官网**：[https://ciaotool.ioarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/)

# 创建流动性并捆绑买入「v2」教程 | 「EVM」使用教程 | CiaoTool

circle-check

**创建流动性并捆绑买入 v2：**[https://bsc.ciaotool.io/swap/v2/create-liquidity-and-buy-v2arrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/swap/v2/create-liquidity-and-buy-v2)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/create-liquidity-and-buy-v2#ru-he-shi-yong-chuang-jian-liu-dong-xing-bing-kun-bang-mai-ru)

✅ 如何使用**创建流动性并捆绑买入**？

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/create-liquidity-and-buy-v2#id-1.-lian-jie-qian-bao)

1\. **连接钱包**

circle-info

创建前必须确保余额充足**（钱包内至少有 0.03 BNB）**

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FIVf4IOZk63OZDweTKe3R%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=559b5673&sv=2)

*   输入用于创建/添加流动性的私钥。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FhhD5AaWP8Y7YT8jwiWOO%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e47026b4&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/create-liquidity-and-buy-v2#id-2.-xuan-ze-jia-chi-de-liang-zhong-dai-bi)

2\. 选择加池的两种代币

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FNbjzC96pyAMUXmkhDzO0%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a8a0bba5&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/create-liquidity-and-buy-v2#id-3.-tian-xie-jia-chi-shu-liang)

3.**填写加池数量**

*   输入两种代币的数量。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FikIxiIOzzvrI5QKRnLxd%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=85cc50a&sv=2)

circle-info

提示：请自行计算合适的比例后再创建流动性。

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/create-liquidity-and-buy-v2#id-4.-dao-ru-mai-ru-qian-bao-si-yao)

4\. 导入买入钱包私钥

*   选择批量导入方式，可以手动粘贴多个私钥，也可以 上传包含私钥的表格文件（xlsx / xls）。
    
*   系统将自动识别每个钱包的 BNB 余额、From余额、To余额。
    

circle-exclamation

注意：单次最多支持导入 **20 个地址**。

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/create-liquidity-and-buy-v2#id-5.-she-zhi-mai-ru-can-shu)

5\. 设置买入参数

**配置方式：**

*   为每个地址设置「买入金额」 ，单个地址无上限买入金额，刷新余额查看即可
    
*   可选择刷新余额或调整买入比例
    
*   系统将展示每个地址的状态 + 操作按钮
    

circle-info

注意：买入地址的BNB余额必须大于 0.0008！

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FylaxJvYLIARyXhf9k0Pp%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d05af914&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/create-liquidity-and-buy-v2#id-6.-kai-shi-jiao-yi)

6\. 开始交易

*   检查无误后，点击 **“开始交易”** 按钮。
    
*   交易速度会受到链上拥堵情况影响，链上拥堵时可能交易速度较慢，还请您耐心等待。
    

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/create-liquidity-and-buy-v2#chang-jian-wen-ti-faq)

❓常见问题 FAQ

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/create-liquidity-and-buy-v2#id-1.-wei-shen-me-chuang-jian-liu-dong-xing-bing-kun-bang-mai-ru-hui-shi-bai)

**1\.** 为什么创建流动性并捆绑买入会失败？

*   check
    
    答：请确认钱包内 BNB / WBNB 余额是否充足，以覆盖加池，捆绑买入所需资金及 Gas 费用。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/create-liquidity-and-buy-v2#id-2.-jia-chi-de-dai-bi-shu-liang-he-bi-li-you-yao-qiu-ma)

**2\.** 加池的代币数量和比例有要求吗？

*   check
    
    答：没有强制限制。你可以根据 代币经济模型、预期初始价格及市值目标 灵活调整加池数量与比例。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/create-liquidity-and-buy-v2#id-3.-yu-gu-jia-ge-hui-yi-zhi-gu-ding-ma)

**3\.** 预估价格会一直固定吗？

*   check
    
    答：不会。预估价格仅代表 上线初始价格，随着用户持续买卖，价格会实时变化，交易越活跃，价格越真实。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/create-liquidity-and-buy-v2#id-4.-shen-me-shi-duo-di-zhi-kun-bang-mai-ru-you-na-xie-xian-zhi)

**4\.** 什么是多地址捆绑买入？有哪些限制？

*   check
    
    答：多地址捆绑买入是指 多个钱包同时执行买入操作，实现更合理的筹码分布。

# BSC Relay Transfer Tutorial | 「EVM」Tutorial | CiaoTool

circle-check

**BSC Relay Transfer:** [https://bsc.ciaotool.io/transfer/relay-transferarrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/transfer/relay-transfer)

circle-exclamation

If you prefer learning through videos, feel free to watch this tutorial.

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/multisender/relay-transfer#operation-steps)

🔗 Operation Steps

triangle-exclamation

The number of sending wallets must match the number of receiving wallets!

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/multisender/relay-transfer#id-1.-select-token-address)

**1\.** Select Token Address

*   Input or select the BSC token contract address you wish to send.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FcL6r1KVJmw4jLFWVpQbl%2Fblobs%2FDi5wl7RDCKtIBYWdB881%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e499b021&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/multisender/relay-transfer#id-2.-enter-upload-send-private-key)

**2\. Enter** / Upload Send Private Key

*   Upload a wallet file containing multiple private keys (xls, xlsx); the system will recognize the source wallets.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FcL6r1KVJmw4jLFWVpQbl%2Fblobs%2FyMnBIRW3UM6qEuYenURL%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3678f7ae&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/multisender/relay-transfer#id-3.-upload-recipient-addresses)

**3\.** Upload Recipient Addresses

*   Upload a list of recipient addresses, ensuring the number of sender and recipient addresses match (e.g: 10 sender addresses to 10 recipient addresses).
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FcL6r1KVJmw4jLFWVpQbl%2Fblobs%2FPgS8UV3ogFTMdfdCtel9%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=171eea3d&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/multisender/relay-transfer#id-4.-set-transfer-parameters)

**4\.** Set Transfer Parameters

1.  **All Amount：**transfers the entire token balance held in the address in a single transaction.
    
2.  **Fixed Amount：**allocates the same token amount to each recipient address.
    
3.  **Fixed Retain：**keeps a specified amount of tokens in the wallet during the operation instead of transferring everything.
    
4.  **Custom (Click to Input)：**manually enter the specific amount each address should receive; allows flexible, per-recipient allocations.
    
5.  **Transfer Count Per Address**：the number of intermediate transfers the funds pass through before reaching the final recipient in a single end-to-end transfer.
    

triangle-exclamation

The more intermediary transfers there are, the more complex the fund path becomes.

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FcL6r1KVJmw4jLFWVpQbl%2Fblobs%2FAokxpjpBDPhXLIOBJKFH%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=be671727&sv=2)

*   For custom amounts, you can upload a file or manually input each amount on a new line.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FcL6r1KVJmw4jLFWVpQbl%2Fblobs%2Fhl7MbMkLAuJ9OUcmKnSM%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4cc6ba7&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/multisender/relay-transfer#id-5.-generate-relay-wallets)

**5\.** Generate relay wallets

*   The system automatically creates intermediate hop addresses for relay operations (to obscure the transfer path).
    
*   View wallet funds status / Check wallet balance status.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FcL6r1KVJmw4jLFWVpQbl%2Fblobs%2FnFQSk5QkwlxRxGhcNwJ9%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6fb21c36&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/multisender/relay-transfer#id-6.-execute-transfer)

**6\.** Execute Transfer

*   Click to confirm and sign the operation; the system will automatically complete all relay transfer transactions.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/multisender/relay-transfer#frequently-asked-questions-faq)

❓ Frequently Asked Questions (FAQ)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/multisender/relay-transfer#id-1.-what-is-bsc-relay-transfer)

**1\.** What is **BSC Relay Transfer** ?

*   check
    
    **Answer**：Relay transfers route funds through multiple hops to obscure the path and boost transaction privacy and security.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/multisender/relay-transfer#id-2.-can-each-address-be-set-with-a-different-amount)

**2\.** Can each address be set with a different amount?

*   check
    
    **Answer**：Yes. You can customize each transaction amount in the uploaded file.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/multisender/relay-transfer#id-3.-does-the-system-save-my-private-keys)

**3\.** Does the system save my private keys?

*   check
    
    **Answer**：No. All signing operations are completed locally in your browser, ensuring private key security.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/multisender/relay-transfer#id-4.-how-many-address-pairs-can-i-transfer-at-once)

**4\.** How many address pairs can I transfer at once?

*   check
    
    **Answer**：More relay addresses increase transfer time but improve privacy and security. There's no strict limit—depends on network and servers—suitable for medium‑to‑large batch operations.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/multisender/relay-transfer#id-5.-can-i-import-xls-xlsx-files)

**5\.** Can I import xls, xlsx files?

*   check
    
    **Answer**：Yes. Both sender private keys and recipient addresses support xls, xlsx format import, improving efficiency.

# 分红本币创建教程 - BSC | 「EVM」使用教程 | CiaoTool

circle-check

**分红本币：**[https://bsc.ciaotool.io/token/holders-dividendarrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/token/holders-dividend)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/token/holders-dividend#shen-me-shi-fen-hong-ben-bi)

🛠 什么是分红本币？

*   分红本币代币是一种内置**持币分红机制**的代币类型，每笔买入或卖出交易会按设定比例扣除本币，并按持币比例自动分配给所有持币地址。持有数量越多，获得的分红越多。
    

**检测风险提醒**：

*   创建分红代币后可能存在安全检测风险。如果你对检测结果非常在意，可以选择创建标准代币，标准币不存在风险。
    
*   创建此类型代币意味着你接受高风险检测结果。部分检测平台可以在权限丢弃后复查，从而去掉风险提示。
    

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/token/holders-dividend#ru-he-chuang-jian-fen-hong-ben-bi-dai-bi)

🪙 如何创建分红本币代币？

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/token/holders-dividend#yi-lian-jie-qian-bao)

一、连接钱包

1.  安装支持BSC链的钱包插件（如 MetaMask / 小狐狸 或 OKX Web3 钱包）
    
2.  打开发币页面： [https://bsc.ciaotool.io/token/holders-dividendarrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/token/holders-dividend)
    
3.  点击右上角【连接钱包】，选择钱包地址并确认授权
    
4.  页面右上角显示钱包地址，表示连接成功
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FA7haNlZZEA3GWyBn4yua%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=53948010&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/token/holders-dividend#er-shu-ru-dai-bi-ji-chu-xin-xi)

二、输入代币基础**信息**

*   **代币全称**：如 CiaoTool，支持中文、英文及中英混合
    
*   **代币符号**：如 C，在钱包和交易所显示
    
*   **发行总量**：固定总供应量，创建后不可增发
    
*   **精度（Decimals）**：代币最小拆分单位，常用 18
    
*   **收币地址**：代币创建完成后接收代币的钱包地址 (可设置当前钱包地址）
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FSS446jBvjWnmfFqwGuIh%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1306332f&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/token/holders-dividend#san-mai-ru-shuil-0x25)

**三、买入税率（ 0**≤x<**25%）**

*   **营销税率**：交易中指定额度的代币将会自动转入营销钱包中,用于项目方做其他营销。
    
*   **分红税率**：交易中指定额度的代币会按持币比例分配给所有持币者,实现持币分红。
    
*   **销毁税率**：交易中指定额度的代币将会被打入黑洞地址,变相实现通缩机制。
    
*   **回流税率**：交易中指定额度的代币将会自动添加到流动池内,保证交易始终存在流动性
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2086467048-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%252Fuploads%252Fi9PjYUhkL9YJOVCTLHzl%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D713c5682-4ff6-432e-970b-2fe2814b7319&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=fbf2c6f8&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/token/holders-dividend#si-mai-chu-shuil-0x25)

**四、卖出税率（ 0**≤x<**25%）**

*   包括营销、分红、销毁、回流，与买入税率逻辑相同，只在卖出交易时生效
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FFwfWg89GGmRtLT9qjkiv%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2ef130dd&sv=2)

circle-exclamation

买入总税率不能超过25%,交易总税率不能超过50%

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/token/holders-dividend#wu-qi-ta-can-shu)

**五、其他参数**

*   **营销钱包**：接收营销税率对应的本币（可设置当前钱包）
    
*   **选择交易所**：PancakeSwap
    
*   **选择底池代币**：WBNB / USDT 等，后续添加流动性需使用同样代币
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FexuOKF1Vsi7h7r67yNDn%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=78271269&sv=2)

triangle-exclamation

代币创建完成后，需要创建流动性池才能交易：

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/token/holders-dividend#liu-tian-jia-liu-dong-xing)

六、添加流动性

*   [**V2 流动性池**arrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/swap/v2/create-liquidity-v2)
    ：首次添加必须使用，支持分红机制，
    
*   **V3 流动性池**：不支持分红机制，不可直接使用
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/token/holders-dividend#qi-zhu-yi-shi-xiang)

七、注意事项

*   黑洞地址持有代币也会参与分红
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/token/holders-dividend#ba-ru-guo-xu-yao-fang-qi-quan-xian-qing-can-kao-yi-xia-bu-zhou)

八、如果需要放弃权限，请参考以下步骤

1.  进入[https://bscscan.com/arrow-up-right](https://bscscan.com/)
     官网
    
2.  输入你的合约地址，找到 **Contract /** **Write Contract as Proxy**
    
3.  找到这个选项：**transferOwnership，** 在 **newOwner** 中输入新的地址**（放弃权限则输入死亡地址或黑洞地址）**
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FAjflDbj6OH6YgWaosops%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=48b6c650&sv=2)

1.  地址：0x000000000000000000000000000000000000dEaD 0x0000000000000000000000000000000000000000
    

triangle-exclamation

**注：放弃权限之后，无法再修改参数，也无法管理合约，谨慎操作**

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/token/holders-dividend#chang-jian-wen-ti-faq)

❓常见问题 FAQ

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/token/holders-dividend#id-1.-he-yue-shi-fou-ke-xiu-gai)

**1\. 合约是否可修改？**

*   check
    
    创建完成后默认丢弃权限，无法修改代币参数，也没有后台控制功能。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/token/holders-dividend#id-2.-chuang-jian-dai-bi-xu-yao-duo-jiu)

**2\. 创建代币需要多久？**

*   check
    
    通常 2-5 分钟，部署完成后可立即在链上查看。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/token/holders-dividend#id-3.-chuang-jian-dai-bi-xu-yao-duo-shao-fei-yong)

**3\. 创建代币需要多少费用？**

*   check
    
    服务费 0.048 BNB + 链上 Gas 费（根据网络浮动）。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/token/holders-dividend#id-4.-ru-he-she-zhi-fa-xing-liang-he-jing-du)

**4\. 如何设置发行量和精度？**

*   check
    
    在发币页面填写总量和精度，精度常用 18 位。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/token/holders-dividend#id-5.-v2-v3-liu-dong-xing-chi-ru-he-xuan-ze)

**5\. V2 / V3 流动性池如何选择？**

*   check
    
    首次加池必须使用 V2，V3 不支持分红机制。

*   **Email**：[support@ciaotool.ioenvelope](mailto:support@ciaotool.io)
    
*   **官网**：[https://ciaotool.ioarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/)

# 314协议代币创建教程 - BSC | 「EVM」使用教程 | CiaoTool

circle-check

**314协议代币**：[https://bsc.ciaotool.io/token/314-protocolarrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/token/314-protocol)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/token/314-protocol#shen-me-shi-314-xie-yi)

🛠 什么是314协议？

314协议是一种新的实验性代币标准，该协议旨在降低用户交易时高昂的交易费用与繁琐的授权流程。和传统的Swap不同，314协议实现了“转账即交易”的新型功效。

*   **买币**：用户将 BNB 转入合约地址，即可获得代币
    
*   **卖币**：用户将代币转入合约地址，即可获得 BNB
    
*   **交易冷却**：设定时间内，全市场仅允许一笔买单，每个地址仅允许一笔卖单
    

**检测风险：**

*   该类型代币可能存在安全检测风险。如果你在意检测结果，可以选择创建标准代币，标准币没有风险。 创建燃烧代币即表示你接受可能的检测风险。
    

circle-exclamation

314 协议尚处于实验阶段，可能存在未知风险。权限功能重要，请确认无误后再丢弃。

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/token/314-protocol#ru-he-chuang-jian-314-xie-yi-dai-bi)

🎯 **如何创建**314协议代币**？**

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/token/314-protocol#yi-lian-jie-qian-bao)

一、连接钱包

1.  **打开发币页面**：[https://bsc.ciaotool.io/token/314-protocolarrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/token/314-protocol)
    
2.  点击右上角**【连接钱包】**，在弹窗中确认钱包地址
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2Fqi5y1ACYR5j7KFkJrdrN%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=cd88c116&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/token/314-protocol#er-shu-ru-dai-bi-ji-chu-xin-xi)

二、输入代币基础**信息**

*   **代币全称**：如 CiaoTool，支持中文、英文及中英混合
    
*   **代币符号**：如 C，在钱包和交易所显示
    
*   **发行总量**：固定总供应量，创建后不可增发
    
*   **精度**：代币最小单位，如 0.000001 精度为 6，默认一般为 18
    
*   **收币地址**：代币创建完成后接收代币的钱包地址 (可设置当前钱包地址，默认白名单）
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FdiLXkCcET6B8o7RHQfcb%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7e9902a9&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/token/314-protocol#san-314-she-zhi)

三、314设置

*   流动性占比:发币时,自动转入合约地址的代币比例,用以提供流动性
    
*   冷却时间(秒):每次买入之间的间隔时间,单个每次卖出的间隔时间
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FCr6J8epGqFceVCKpwB9v%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f0bcee26&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/token/314-protocol#si-mai-ru-shuil-bi-li-0x25)

四、买入税率**（比例 0**≤x<**25%）**

*   **营销税率**：买入扣除后，合约触发阈值自动卖出换成分红币发到营销钱包
    
*   **销毁税率**：发送到黑洞地址销毁
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2F7lmU16ELdwQhNT8wtofy%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6efe3b24&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/token/314-protocol#wu-mai-chu-shuil-bi-li-0x25)

五、卖出税率**（比例 0**≤x<**25%）**

*   包括营销、销毁，与买入税率逻辑相同，只在卖出交易时生效
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2F47DubuloS6SFJ5gmbWOq%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8b3dba4c&sv=2)

circle-exclamation

买入和卖出税率不能超过25%,交易总税率不能超过50%

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/token/314-protocol#liu-qi-ta-can-shu)

六、其他参数

*   **营销钱包**：仅营销钱包有权添加流动性、撤出流动性、延长锁池时间，建议用**当前发币钱包**作为营销钱包
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2Fl3G8WnyvjIK0DXqlMKIF%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2dbe0970&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/token/314-protocol#qi-xiang-guan-gong-neng-kai-guan-can-shu)

七、相关功能开关参数

**最大持币量**

*   check
    
    打开：可设置单个钱包持有的最大代币数量
    
*   关闭：无法使用，此开关关闭后无法再次开启
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/token/314-protocol#zhu-yi-shi-xiang)

⚠️注意事项

circle-info

不推荐在薄饼做池子交易，因为存在多限制且没有税率，可能导致转账交易受影响。同时，一个代币会形成两个池子（薄饼池与转账池）、两个价格，容易被搬砖套利。

**交易区别**：

*   薄饼交易代币变成标准币，没有税率和滑点。
    
*   冷却时间仍有效，薄饼交易会影响转账交易，需等待冷却结束。
    
*   Ave显示的价格K线仅反映薄饼池价格，不等于转账价格。
    

**常见失败原因**：

*   加了V3池子，只支持V2池子。
    
*   持币限制低于加池数量，加池失败。解决方法：加池后将池子地址加入持币白名单。
    
*   卖出失败：池子地址未加持币白名单或冷却时间内有人转账。解决方法：同时将池子地址和路由地址加入冷却白名单与持币白名单。
    

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/token/314-protocol#chang-jian-wen-ti-faq)

❓常见问题 FAQ

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/token/314-protocol#id-1.-jiao-yi-leng-que-ru-he-sheng-xiao)

**1\.** 交易冷却如何生效？

*   check
    
    交易冷却在设置的时间内限制全网买单和每个地址卖单数量。冷却时间内，其他用户无法买入，单个地址也只能卖一次。冷却时间结束后，交易才会恢复。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/token/314-protocol#id-2.-quan-xian-diu-qi-hou-hai-neng-jia-chi-huo-che-chi-ma)

**2\.** 权限丢弃后还能加池或撤池吗？

*   check
    
    如果营销钱包与权限钱包为同一地址，即使丢弃权限，营销钱包仍可操作加池和撤池，流动性功能不受影响。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/token/314-protocol#id-3.-ru-he-bao-zheng-pi-liang-zhuan-zhang-huo-cao-zuo-bu-shou-leng-que-xian-zhi)

**3\.** 如何保证批量转账或操作不受冷却限制？

*   check
    
    批量转账前需将转账合约地址加入交易冷却白名单，同时如果有持币上限，也需加入持币白名单，否则操作会失败。
    

**💬 如遇到问题？加入社群实时咨询**：[https://t.me/ciaotoolarrow-up-right](https://t.me/ciaotool)

*   **Email**：[support@ciaotool.ioenvelope](mailto:support@ciaotool.io)
    
*   **官网**：[https://ciaotool.ioarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/)
    
*   **X（Twitter）**：[https://x.com/CiaoToolarrow-up-right](https://x.com/CiaoTool)
    
*   **Medium**： [https://medium.com/@ciaotoolarrow-up-right](https://medium.com/@ciaotool)
    
*   **Blog**：[https://www.ciaoailiquidity.com/zh/blogarrow-up-right](https://www.ciaoailiquidity.com/zh/blog)
    
*   **YouTube**：[https://www.youtube.com/@CiaoToolarrow-up-right](https://www.youtube.com/@CiaoTool)
    
*   **WhatsApp**：[https://whatsapp.com/channel/0029VbAuLrVAojYxRNw95W1Jarrow-up-right](https://whatsapp.com/channel/0029VbAuLrVAojYxRNw95W1J)
    

triangle-exclamation

# 多地址捆绑卖出教程「v2 and v3」 | 「EVM」使用教程 | CiaoTool

circle-check

**多地址捆绑卖出v2：**[https://bsc.ciaotool.io/swap/v2/multi-address-sell-v2arrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/swap/v2/multi-address-sell-v2)

**多地址捆绑卖出v3：**[https://bsc.ciaotool.io/swap/v3/multi-address-sell-v3arrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/swap/v3/multi-address-sell-v3)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/v2-v3-multi-address-sell#duo-di-zhi-kun-bang-mai-chu-jiao-cheng)

🪜 多地址捆绑卖出教程

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/v2-v3-multi-address-sell#id-1.-dao-ru-si-yao)

1\. 导入私钥

*   将用于支付市值操作手续费的钱包私钥导入。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FvVtAMFWuGgoNnCvYfjQj%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=74f8652&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/v2-v3-multi-address-sell#id-2.-dao-ru-bi-dui-di-zhi-huo-xuan-ze-bi-dui)

2\. 导入币对地址或选择币对

*   **v2-**在输入框中填写目标代币地址，或点击下拉菜单选择当前钱包持有的代币。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2Fgjluf7csT7zet2lhBxMc%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=385d8099&sv=2)

*   **v3-**在币对输入框中 **粘贴目标币对**。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2F2GyM9wN3dNywtprGN3hu%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=573b97e5&sv=2)

circle-exclamation

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/v2-v3-multi-address-sell#di-er-bu-cao-zuo-zhong-v2-he-v3-de-qu-bie-zai-yu-v2-shou-dong-xuan-ze-dai-bi-v3-shu-ru-bi-dui-di-zhi)

第二步操作中v2和v3的区别在于：v2手动选择代币，v3输入币对地址。

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/v2-v3-multi-address-sell#id-3.-dao-ru-mai-chu-qian-bao-si-yao)

3\. 导入卖出钱包私钥

*   选择批量导入方式，可以 **手动粘贴多个私钥**，也可以 **上传包含私钥的表格文件（**xls、xlsx格式**）**。
    
*   系统将自动识别每个钱包的 BNB 余额、TokenA余额、TokenB余额。
    

circle-info

注意：单次最多支持导入 **20 个地址**。

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/v2-v3-multi-address-sell#id-4.-she-zhi-mai-chu-can-shu)

4\. 设置卖出参数

**配置方式：**

1.  为每个地址设置「卖出金额」 ，单个地址无上限卖出金额，刷新余额查看即可
    
2.  可选择刷新余额或调整卖出比例
    
3.  系统将展示每个地址的状态 + 操作按钮
    

triangle-exclamation

💡 注意：卖出地址的BNB余额必须大于 0.0008！

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FlI8TtkoqdX1MEsJAxJ26%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=146ea671&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/v2-v3-multi-address-sell#id-5.-zhi-xing-mai-chu-cao-zuo)

5\. 执行卖出操作

*   检查无误后，点击 **“开始交易”** 按钮。
    
*   系统会自动为每个钱包生成交易并执行捆绑卖出操作。
    

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/v2-v3-multi-address-sell#chang-jian-wen-ti-faq)

❓ 常见问题 FAQ

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/v2-v3-multi-address-sell#id-1.-shen-me-shi-duo-di-zhi-kun-bang-mai-chu)

1\. 什么是多地址捆绑卖出？

*   check
    
    答：指多个钱包同时卖出同一代币，以批量执行交易，提高交易成功率与速度。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/v2-v3-multi-address-sell#id-2.-yi-ci-zui-duo-zhi-chi-ji-ge-qian-bao)

2\. 一次最多支持几个钱包？

*   check
    
    答：单次操作最多可导入 **20 个钱包地址** 进行同步卖出。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/v2-v3-multi-address-sell#id-3.-wei-shen-me-mai-chu-di-zhi-de-bnb-yuebi-xu-da-yu-0.0008)

**3\.** 为什么卖出地址的BNB余额必须大于 0.0008？

*   check
    
    答：每个钱包至少保留 0.0008 BNB 以上余额，以确保足够支付交易 Gas 费用。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/v2-v3-multi-address-sell#id-4.-dai-bi-di-zhi-shu-ru-cuo-wu-zen-me-ban)

4\. 代币地址输入错误怎么办？

*   check
    
    答：请在执行前确认代币合约地址正确无误。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/v2-v3-multi-address-sell#id-5.-shi-fou-zhi-chi-zi-ding-yi-mai-chu-jine)

5\. 是否支持自定义卖出金额？

*   check
    
    答：支持。你可以为不同钱包单独设定卖出金额，也可以统一设定同样的卖出数额。

# Multi-to-one - Universal Tutorial | 「EVM」Tutorial | CiaoTool

circle-check

**BSC** **Multi-to-one Transfer**：[https://bsc.ciaotool.io/transfer/many-to-onearrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/transfer/many-to-one)

**Base Multi-to-one Transfer:** [https://base.ciaotool.io/transfer/many-to-onearrow-up-right](https://base.ciaotool.io/transfer/many-to-one)

**X Layer Multi-to-one Transfer:** [https://xlayer.ciaotool.io/transfer/many-to-onearrow-up-right](https://xlayer.ciaotool.io/transfer/many-to-one)

**IoTeX Multi-to-one Transfer:** [https://iotex.ciaotool.io/transfer/many-to-onearrow-up-right](https://iotex.ciaotool.io/transfer/many-to-one)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/multisender/many-to-one#operation-steps)

🔗 Operation Steps

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/multisender/many-to-one#id-1.-open-the-multi-to-one-page-and-input-the-receiving-address)

1\. Open the Multi-to-one Page and Input the Receiving Address

*   Navigate to the Multi-to-one Transfer page and enter the main address where tokens will be aggregated.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/multisender/many-to-one#id-2.-select-token-address)

2\. Select Token Address

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FcL6r1KVJmw4jLFWVpQbl%2Fblobs%2F83QQ9UWvSswFf8UTgVo4%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1f73037d&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/multisender/many-to-one#id-3.-enter-upload-sender-private-key)

3\. Enter / Upload Sender Private Key

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FcL6r1KVJmw4jLFWVpQbl%2Fblobs%2FTlVDKLukYkxQyMYt0MDI%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=edfdf354&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/multisender/many-to-one#id-4.-enter-receiving-address)

4\. Enter Receiving Address

*   Please ensure you have carefully confirmed the receiving address.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FcL6r1KVJmw4jLFWVpQbl%2Fblobs%2FfRE2ejPcaB2jJaloK472%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ef8948d7&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/multisender/many-to-one#id-5.-set-transfer-amount-type)

5\. Set Transfer Amount Type

1.  **All Amount:** Transfer the entire balance.
    
2.  **Fixed Amount:** Specify a fixed amount to transfer.
    
3.  **Fixed Retain:** Specify an amount to retain in each sender wallet.
    
4.  **Custom (Click to Input):** Manually input custom amounts for each sender.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FcL6r1KVJmw4jLFWVpQbl%2Fblobs%2FIpQFZFaRxfT59MsQ6nBX%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7fce20c3&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/multisender/many-to-one#id-6.confirm-and-execute-transfer)

6.Confirm and Execute Transfer

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FcL6r1KVJmw4jLFWVpQbl%2Fblobs%2FfzPEcv2O6Kc0V0CuJGej%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=304a3f02&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/multisender/many-to-one#frequently-asked-questions-faq)

❓ Frequently Asked Questions (FAQ)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/multisender/many-to-one#id-1.-what-is-multi-to-one-transfer)

**1\. What is** Multi-to-one **Transfer?**

*   check
    
    **Answer**：It refers to transferring tokens from multiple wallets to a single main address.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/multisender/many-to-one#id-2.-does-the-system-support-consolidating-different-amounts)

**2\.** Does the system support consolidating different amounts?

*   check
    
    **Answer**：Yes. You can set to transfer all amounts or customize the transfer amount for each address.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/multisender/many-to-one#id-3.-are-my-private-keys-secure)

**3\.** Are my private keys secure?

*   check
    
    **Answer**：Yes. All private keys are used for local signing and are not uploaded to any server.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/multisender/many-to-one#id-4.-which-tokens-can-i-consolidate)

**4\.** Which tokens can I consolidate?

*   check
    
    **Answer**：The system supports all tokens on the selected network; simply input the contract address.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/multisender/many-to-one#id-5.-does-it-support-importing-a-large-number-of-addresses)

**5\.** Does it support importing a large number of addresses?

*   check
    
    **Answer**：Yes. You can import an unlimited number of source addresses via xls, xlsx file.

# Multi-to-Multi - Universal Tutorial | 「EVM」Tutorial | CiaoTool

circle-check

**BSC** **Multi-to-Multi Transfer:** [https://bsc.ciaotool.io/transfer/many-to-manyarrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/transfer/many-to-many)

**Base Multi-to-Multi Transfer:** [https://base.ciaotool.io/transfer/many-to-manyarrow-up-right](https://base.ciaotool.io/transfer/many-to-many)

**X Layer Multi-to-Multi Transfer:** [https://xlayer.ciaotool.io/transfer/many-to-manyarrow-up-right](https://xlayer.ciaotool.io/transfer/many-to-many)

**IoTeX Multi-to-Multi Transfer:** [https://iotex.ciaotool.io/transfer/many-to-manyarrow-up-right](https://iotex.ciaotool.io/transfer/many-to-many)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/multisender/many-to-many#operation-steps)

🔗 Operation Steps

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/multisender/many-to-many#id-1.-select-token-address)

**1\.** Select Token Address

*   Enter or select the token contract address you wish to send.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FcL6r1KVJmw4jLFWVpQbl%2Fblobs%2FDi5wl7RDCKtIBYWdB881%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e499b021&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/multisender/many-to-many#id-2.-enter-upload-sender-private-key)

**2\.** Enter / Upload Sender Private Key

*   Upload a wallet file containing multiple private keys (xls, xlsx); the system will recognize the source wallets.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FcL6r1KVJmw4jLFWVpQbl%2Fblobs%2FyMnBIRW3UM6qEuYenURL%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3678f7ae&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/multisender/many-to-many#id-3.-upload-recipient-addresses)

**3\.** Upload Recipient Addresses

*   Upload a list of recipient addresses, ensuring the number of sender and recipient addresses match (e.g., 10 sender addresses to 10 recipient addresses).
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FcL6r1KVJmw4jLFWVpQbl%2Fblobs%2FPgS8UV3ogFTMdfdCtel9%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=171eea3d&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/multisender/many-to-many#id-4.-set-transfer-parameters)

**4\.** Set Transfer Parameters

1.  **All Amount**
    
2.  **Fixed Amount**
    
3.  **Fixed Retain**
    
4.  **Custom (Click to Input)**
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FcL6r1KVJmw4jLFWVpQbl%2Fblobs%2FB7C9XdGvn8aBnv3GSVOR%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=cdfa7fb0&sv=2)

*   For custom amounts, you can upload a file or manually input each amount on a new line.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FcL6r1KVJmw4jLFWVpQbl%2Fblobs%2Fhl7MbMkLAuJ9OUcmKnSM%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4cc6ba7&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/multisender/many-to-many#id-5.-execute-transfer)

**5\.** Execute Transfer

*   Click to confirm and sign the operation; the system will automatically complete all Multi-to-Multi transactions.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/multisender/many-to-many#frequently-asked-questions-faq)

❓ Frequently Asked Questions (FAQ)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/multisender/many-to-many#id-1.-what-is-multi-to-multi-transfer)

**1\.** What is Multi-to-Multi Transfer?

*   check
    
    **Answer**：It refers to batch sending tokens from multiple sender addresses to multiple recipient addresses.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/multisender/many-to-many#id-2.-can-each-address-be-set-with-a-different-amount)

**2\.** Can each address be set with a different amount?

*   check
    
    **Answer**：Yes. You can customize each transaction amount in the uploaded file.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/multisender/many-to-many#id-3.-does-the-system-save-my-private-keys)

**3\.** Does the system save my private keys?

*   check
    
    **Answer**：No. All signing operations are completed locally in your browser, ensuring private key security.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/multisender/many-to-many#id-4.-how-many-address-pairs-can-i-transfer-at-once)

**4\.** How many address pairs can I transfer at once?

*   check
    
    **Answer**：The system supports uploading an unlimited number of address pairs at a time, making it suitable for large-scale batch operations.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/multisender/many-to-many#id-5.-can-i-import-xls-xlsx-files)

**5\.** Can I import xls, xlsx files?

*   check
    
    **Answer**：Yes. Both send private keys and recipient addresses support xls, xlsx format import, improving efficiency.

# Batch Swap Tutorial「 v2 and v3」 | 「EVM」Tutorial | CiaoTool

circle-check

**Batch Swap V2：**[https://bsc.ciaotool.io/swap/batch-swap-v2arrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/swap/batch-swap-v2)

circle-check

**Batch Swap V3**: [https://bsc.ciaotool.io/swap/v3/batch-swap-v3arrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/swap/v3/batch-swap-v3)

circle-exclamation

If you prefer learning through videos, feel free to watch this tutorial.

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/swap/batch-swap-v2-v3-1#how-to-use-the-bsc-batch-swap)

✅ How to Use the BSC Batch Swap


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/swap/batch-swap-v2-v3-1#id-1.-import-wallet-private-key)

1\. Import Wallet Private Key

*   Import the private key of the wallet used to pay transaction fees (the private key must be different from the trading wallet’s private key).
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FcL6r1KVJmw4jLFWVpQbl%2Fblobs%2FDUsBPrrSsL8TBhGcsJyi%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=bfc79f3e&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/swap/batch-swap-v2-v3-1#id-2.-select-token)

2\. Select Token

*   Enter the target token address in the input box or select from the dropdown menu of tokens held by the current wallet.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FcL6r1KVJmw4jLFWVpQbl%2Fblobs%2FlxlyS2VikoA7u0rw6jSv%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a8da7505&sv=2)

*   Quickly switch between trade directions (From: token to spend, To: token to receive).
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FcL6r1KVJmw4jLFWVpQbl%2Fblobs%2FGnKiXsXEQ8FanlcvsW8c%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2a6b4ebe&sv=2)

circle-exclamation

**Note:** For V3 batch trading, only the trading pair address needs to be imported.

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FcL6r1KVJmw4jLFWVpQbl%2Fblobs%2FWUWsqbRaiECIbnSEm26j%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=708e2ea8&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/swap/batch-swap-v2-v3-1#id-3.-set-trade-parameters)

3\. Set Trade Parameters

*   Choose the trade amount mode: **Fixed Amount、Fixed Retain、All Amount.**
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FcL6r1KVJmw4jLFWVpQbl%2Fblobs%2FbEwC0xDtQdag6ycXLc1O%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=75b8af00&sv=2)

*   Set slippage, transaction speed, and timeout duration.
    

circle-info

Timeout duration refers to the maximum waiting time for the transaction. If not completed within this time, the transaction may fail.

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FcL6r1KVJmw4jLFWVpQbl%2Fblobs%2Fs9rxRGA6K0hIYJoatHL0%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2f45354c&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/swap/batch-swap-v2-v3-1#id-4.import-wallets-for-batch-trading)

4.Import Wallets for Batch Trading

*   You can upload a private key file for import.
    

circle-info

Each trading wallet needs to have some BNB to pay for transaction gas fees.

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FcL6r1KVJmw4jLFWVpQbl%2Fblobs%2FPm5Hb6mxmdR7oVOUdZOu%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=90aff84d&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/swap/batch-swap-v2-v3-1#id-5.-start-batch-trading)

5\. Start Batch Trading

*   **Token Authorization:** If the token to be spent is not BNB, token authorization is required first to facilitate faster batch trading.
    
*   Transaction speed may be affected by on-chain congestion. During periods of congestion, transactions may be slower; please be patient.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/swap/batch-swap-v2-v3-1#frequently-asked-questions-faq)

❓Frequently Asked Questions (FAQ)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/swap/batch-swap-v2-v3-1#id-1.-what-is-batch-swap)

**1\.** What is Batch Swap?

*   check
    
    **Answer**：Batch Swap V2 allows users to initiate token swap transactions simultaneously across multiple wallet addresses, suitable for volume brushing, market control, and other multi-address operations.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/swap/batch-swap-v2-v3-1#id-2.-which-types-of-wallets-are-supported)

**2\.** Which types of wallets are supported?

*   check
    
    **Answer**：Wallets that support private key import are supported. Operations can also be performed using the currently connected wallet. Manual input or CSV file upload is supported.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/swap/batch-swap-v2-v3-1#id-3.-does-it-support-custom-swap-parameters)

**3\.** Does it support custom Swap parameters?

*   check
    
    **Answer**：Yes. You can set the Swap amount, timeout duration, slippage, and other parameters for each transaction, allowing for flexible strategy configuration.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/swap/batch-swap-v2-v3-1#id-4.-is-the-swap-operation-secure-will-my-private-keys-be-uploaded)

**4\.** Is the Swap operation secure? Will my private keys be uploaded?

*   check
    
    **Answer**：Yes. All operations are signed locally in your browser. Private keys are not uploaded or stored on the server, ensuring asset security.

# Create/Add Liquidity v3 Tutorial | 「EVM」Tutorial | CiaoTool

circle-check

**Create Liquidity v3：**[https://bsc.ciaotool.io/swap/v3/create-liquidity-v3arrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/swap/v3/create-liquidity-v3)

circle-check

**Add Liquidity v3：**[https://bsc.ciaotool.io/swap/v3/add-liquidity-v3arrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/swap/v3/add-liquidity-v3)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/swap/create-add-liquidity-v3#create-add-liquidity-detailed-guide)

✅ **Create / Add Liquidity – Detailed Guide**

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/swap/create-add-liquidity-v3#id-1.-connect-wallet)

1\. **Connect Wallet**

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FcL6r1KVJmw4jLFWVpQbl%2Fblobs%2F3Dy7JjQ4D457mBbqu42Y%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7adb871b&sv=2)

*   Enter the private key used to create or add liquidity.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FcL6r1KVJmw4jLFWVpQbl%2Fblobs%2Fuop9eBfw4iw9169lSLrz%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4cac70c&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/swap/create-add-liquidity-v3#id-2.-select-the-two-tokens-for-the-pool)

2\. Select the Two Tokens for the Pool

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FcL6r1KVJmw4jLFWVpQbl%2Fblobs%2FDq22nR8zTxMz4CTI5htG%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b49849f&sv=2)

*   When adding liquidity: simply enter the **pair contract address**.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FcL6r1KVJmw4jLFWVpQbl%2Fblobs%2Fnyh8b2Zh99IccUulwiQ1%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8fed7439&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/swap/create-add-liquidity-v3#id-3.-select-fee-tier)

**3\.** Select Fee Tier

LP fees in **V3** are different from **V2** and are no longer compounded.

*   **Trading fees differ:**
    
    *   **V3** offers four different fee tiers, with fees reduced by up to **25×**.
        
    *   **V2** charges a fixed **0.25%** fee per trade.
        
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FcL6r1KVJmw4jLFWVpQbl%2Fblobs%2FK2cxlnV8YwAwN1E13Uz0%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=eb34b6de&sv=2)

circle-exclamation

**Note:** The default slippage setting for creating liquidity in **Swap v3** is **1%**.

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/swap/create-add-liquidity-v3#id-4.-set-initial-price-and-price-range)

**4\. Set Initial Price & Price Range**

1.  **Range width determines returns** (Applicable to both LP fee rewards and CAKE rewards)
    

*   Narrower range → higher returns, higher impermanent loss
    
*   Wider range → lower returns, lower impermanent loss
    
*   Full-range setup behaves similarly to V2, with very low returns
    

1.  **When price moves out of range**
    

*   No rewards are generated
    
*   The liquidity position becomes a single-asset holding
    
*   You can remove liquidity and re-add it, or wait for the price to return to the range
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FcL6r1KVJmw4jLFWVpQbl%2Fblobs%2FEUeS6Z63qDsVYOriNiUG%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7c429dc&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/swap/create-add-liquidity-v3#id-5.-enter-liquidity-amounts)

5\. Enter Liquidity Amounts

*   Input the token amounts.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FcL6r1KVJmw4jLFWVpQbl%2Fblobs%2FoKtxCU92I8yA0ATvjfFT%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=afb664d8&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/swap/create-add-liquidity-v3#id-6.-approve-tokens)

6\. Approve Tokens

*   For the first operation, you must authorize the contract to use your tokens.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/swap/create-add-liquidity-v3#id-7.-start-swap)

7\. Start **Swap**

*   After verifying all details, click the **“Start Swap”** button.
    

💬 **Need help? Join our community for real-time support:** [https://t.me/ciaotoolarrow-up-right](https://t.me/ciaotool)

*   **Email:** [support@ciaotool.ioenvelope](mailto:support@ciaotool.io)
    
*   **Website:** [https://ciaotool.ioarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/)
    
*   **X (Twitter):** [https://x.com/CiaoToolarrow-up-right](https://x.com/CiaoTool)

*   **Blog**: [https://www.ciaoailiquidity.com/blogarrow-up-right](https://www.ciaoailiquidity.com/blog)
    
*   **YouTube:** [https://www.youtube.com/@CiaoToolarrow-up-right](https://www.youtube.com/@CiaoTool)

# 多地址捆绑买入-BNB/USD1教程 | 「EVM」使用教程 | CiaoTool

circle-check

**FourMeme多地址捆绑买入-BNB：**[https://bsc.ciaotool.io/fourmeme/bnb/multi-address-buyarrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/fourmeme/bnb/multi-address-buy)

circle-check

**FourMeme多地址捆绑买入-USD1：**[https://bsc.ciaotool.io/fourmeme/usd1/multi-address-buyarrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/fourmeme/usd1/multi-address-buy)

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/fourmeme/multi-address-buy#duo-di-zhi-kun-bang-mai-ru-jiao-cheng)

🪜 多地址捆绑买入教程


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/fourmeme/multi-address-buy#di-yi-bu-dao-ru-si-yao)

🧩 第一步：导入私钥

*   手动粘贴私钥，粘贴完成后会显示当前钱包的余额，可刷新余额。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2F6V9nhvX1IejVTKNhhv3d%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6a7f6cf2&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/fourmeme/multi-address-buy#di-er-bu-dao-ru-dai-bi-he-yue-di-zhi)

🌐 第二步：导入代币合约地址

*   在代币输入框中 **粘贴目标代币的合约地址**。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FsFsc7Pp1ZfvAtvcTcmEZ%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5fd6f5c4&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/fourmeme/multi-address-buy#di-san-bu-dao-ru-mai-ru-qian-bao-si-yao)

🏷 第三步：导入买入钱包私钥

*   选择批量导入方式，可以 **手动粘贴多个私钥**，也可以 **上传包含私钥的表格文件（**xls、xlsx格式**）**。
    
*   系统将自动识别每个钱包的 BNB 余额与授权状态。
    

circle-info

注意：单次最多支持导入 **20 个钱包地址**。

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/fourmeme/multi-address-buy#di-si-bu-she-zhi-mai-ru-can-shu)

💰 第四步：设置买入参数

**配置方式：**

1.  为每个地址设置「买入金额」 ，单个地址无上限买入金额，刷新余额查看即可
    
2.  可选择刷新余额或调整买入比例
    
3.  系统将展示每个地址的状态 + 操作按钮
    

triangle-exclamation

💡 注意：买入地址的BNB余额必须大于 0.0008！

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FOYjRcDiNMPaZxJoIGuFX%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3adf0586&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/fourmeme/multi-address-buy#di-wu-bu-zhi-xing-mai-ru-cao-zuo)

🛠 第五步：执行买入操作

*   点击 **“执行（代币买入）”** 按钮。
    
*   系统会自动为每个钱包生成交易并执行捆绑买入操作。
    
*   执行完成后，可实时查看各钱包的买入状态
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2Fa4AbPzlrGYNhEhe3VOXX%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6ebc8f5a&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/fourmeme/multi-address-buy#chang-jian-wen-ti-faq)

❓ 常见问题 FAQ

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/fourmeme/multi-address-buy#id-1.-shen-me-shi-duo-di-zhi-kun-bang-mai-ru)

1\. 什么是多地址捆绑买入？

*   check
    
    答：指多个钱包同时买入同一代币，以批量执行交易，提高交易成功率与速度。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/fourmeme/multi-address-buy#id-2.-yi-ci-zui-duo-zhi-chi-ji-ge-qian-bao)

2\. 一次最多支持几个钱包？

*   check
    
    答：单次操作最多可导入 **20 个钱包地址** 进行同步买入。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/fourmeme/multi-address-buy#id-3.-wei-shen-me-mai-ru-di-zhi-de-bnb-yuebi-xu-da-yu-0.0008)

**3\.** 为什么买入地址的BNB余额必须大于 0.0008？

*   check
    
    答：每个钱包至少保留 0.0008 BNB 以上余额，以确保足够支付交易 Gas 费用。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/fourmeme/multi-address-buy#id-4.-dai-bi-di-zhi-shu-ru-cuo-wu-zen-me-ban)

4\. 代币地址输入错误怎么办？

*   check
    
    答：请在执行前确认代币合约地址正确无误。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/fourmeme/multi-address-buy#id-5.-shi-fou-zhi-chi-zi-ding-yi-mai-ru-jine)

5\. 是否支持自定义买入金额？

*   check
    
    答：支持。你可以为不同钱包单独设定买入金额，也可以统一设定同样的买入数额。
    

**💬 如遇到问题？加入社群实时咨询**：[https://t.me/ciaotoolarrow-up-right](https://t.me/ciaotool)

*   **Email**：[support@ciaotool.ioenvelope](mailto:support@ciaotool.io)
    
*   **官网**：[https://ciaotool.ioarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/)
    
*   **X（Twitter）**：[https://x.com/CiaoToolarrow-up-right](https://x.com/CiaoTool)
    
*   **Medium**： [https://medium.com/@ciaotoolarrow-up-right](https://medium.com/@ciaotool)
    
*   **Blog**：[https://www.ciaoailiquidity.com/zh/blogarrow-up-right](https://www.ciaoailiquidity.com/zh/blog)
    
*   **YouTube**：[https://www.youtube.com/@CiaoToolarrow-up-right](https://www.youtube.com/@CiaoTool)
    
*   **WhatsApp**：[https://whatsapp.com/channel/0029VbAuLrVAojYxRNw95W1Jarrow-up-right](https://whatsapp.com/channel/0029VbAuLrVAojYxRNw95W1J)
