# 多地址捆绑买入-BNB/USD1/USDT 教程 | 「EVM」使用教程 | CiaoTool

circle-check

**Flap多地址捆绑买入-BNB:** [https://bsc.ciaotool.io/flap/bnb/multi-address-buyarrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/flap/bnb/multi-address-buy)

circle-check

**Flap多地址捆绑买入-USD1:** [https://bsc.ciaotool.io/flap/usd1/multi-address-buyarrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/flap/usd1/multi-address-buy)

circle-check

**Flap多地址捆绑买入-USDT:** [https://bsc.ciaotool.io/flap/usdt/multi-address-buyarrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/flap/usdt/multi-address-buy)

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/flap/multi-address-buy#flap-duo-di-zhi-kun-bang-mai-ru-jiao-cheng)

🪜 Flap 多地址捆绑买入教程


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/flap/multi-address-buy#di-yi-bu-dao-ru-si-yao)

🧩 第一步：导入私钥

*   手动粘贴私钥，粘贴完成后会显示当前钱包的余额，可刷新余额。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2F6V9nhvX1IejVTKNhhv3d%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6a7f6cf2&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/flap/multi-address-buy#di-er-bu-dao-ru-dai-bi-he-yue-di-zhi)

🌐 第二步：导入代币合约地址

*   在代币输入框中 **粘贴目标代币的合约地址**。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FsFsc7Pp1ZfvAtvcTcmEZ%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5fd6f5c4&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/flap/multi-address-buy#di-san-bu-dao-ru-mai-ru-qian-bao-si-yao)

🏷 第三步：导入买入钱包私钥

*   选择批量导入方式，可以 **手动粘贴多个私钥**，也可以 **上传包含私钥的表格文件（xls、xlsx格式）**。
    
*   系统将自动识别每个钱包的 USD1 余额与授权状态。
    

circle-info

注意：单次最多支持导入 **20 个钱包地址**。

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/flap/multi-address-buy#di-si-bu-she-zhi-mai-ru-can-shu)

💰 第四步：设置买入参数

**配置方式：**

1.  为每个地址设置「买入金额」 ，单个地址无上限买入金额，刷新余额查看即可
    
2.  可选择刷新余额
    
3.  系统将展示每个地址的状态 + 操作按钮
    

triangle-exclamation

💡 注意：买入地址的USD1余额必须大于 0.0008！

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FBNOv1yV8206r8rI8pqvh%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f5cd238f&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/flap/multi-address-buy#di-wu-bu-zhi-xing-mai-ru-cao-zuo)

🛠 第五步：执行买入操作

*   点击 **“执行（代币买入）”** 按钮。
    
*   系统会自动为每个钱包生成交易并执行捆绑买入操作。
    
*   执行完成后，可实时查看各钱包的买入状态
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2Fa4AbPzlrGYNhEhe3VOXX%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6ebc8f5a&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/flap/multi-address-buy#chang-jian-wen-ti-faq)

❓ 常见问题 FAQ

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/flap/multi-address-buy#id-1.-shen-me-shi-duo-di-zhi-kun-bang-mai-ru)

1\. 什么是多地址捆绑买入？

*   check
    
    答：指多个钱包同时卖出同一代币，以批量执行交易，提高交易成功率与速度。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/flap/multi-address-buy#id-2.-yi-ci-zui-duo-zhi-chi-ji-ge-qian-bao)

2\. 一次最多支持几个钱包？

*   check
    
    答：单次操作最多可导入 **20 个钱包地址** 进行同步买入。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/flap/multi-address-buy#id-3.-wei-shen-me-mai-ru-di-zhi-de-yuebi-xu-da-yu-0.0008)

**3\.** 为什么买入地址的余额必须大于 0.0008？

*   check
    
    答：每个钱包至少保留 0.0008 USD1 以上余额，以确保足够支付交易 Gas 费用。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/flap/multi-address-buy#id-4.-dai-bi-di-zhi-shu-ru-cuo-wu-zen-me-ban)

4\. 代币地址输入错误怎么办？

*   check
    
    答：请在执行前确认代币合约地址正确无误。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/flap/multi-address-buy#id-5.-shi-fou-zhi-chi-zi-ding-yi-mai-ru-jine)

5\. 是否支持自定义买入金额？

*   check
    
    答：支持。你可以为不同钱包单独设定买入金额，也可以统一设定同样的买入数额。

# 黑洞分红代币创建教程 - BSC | 「EVM」使用教程 | CiaoTool

circle-check

**黑洞分红代币**：[https://bsc.ciaotool.io/token/black-holearrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/token/black-hole)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/token/black-hole#shen-me-shi-hei-dong-fen-hong-dai-bi)

🛠 什么是**黑洞分红**代币？

*   黑洞分红指的是，用户将持有的代币转入黑洞地址后，才能获得分红资格。具体分红哪种代币，可以在创建合约的时候填写。
    

circle-exclamation

**黑洞地址：**_0x000000000000000000000000000000000000dEaD_

**检测风险：**

*   该类型代币可能存在安全检测风险。如果你在意检测结果，可以选择创建标准代币，标准币没有风险。 创建燃烧代币即表示你接受可能的检测风险。
    

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/token/black-hole#ru-he-chuang-jian-di-hei-dong-fen-hong-dai-bi)

🎯 **如何创建**底**黑洞分红**代币**？**

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/token/black-hole#yi-lian-jie-qian-bao)

一、连接钱包

1.  **打开发币页面**：[https://bsc.ciaotool.io/token/black-holearrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/token/black-hole)
    
2.  点击右上角**【连接钱包】**，在弹窗中确认钱包地址
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2Fqi5y1ACYR5j7KFkJrdrN%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=cd88c116&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/token/black-hole#er-shu-ru-dai-bi-ji-chu-xin-xi)

二、输入代币基础**信息**

*   **代币全称**：如 CiaoTool，支持中文、英文及中英混合
    
*   **代币符号**：如 C，在钱包和交易所显示
    
*   **发行总量**：固定总供应量，创建后不可增发
    
*   **精度**：代币最小单位，如 0.000001 精度为 6，默认一般为 18
    
*   **收币地址**：代币创建完成后接收代币的钱包地址 (可设置当前钱包地址，默认白名单）
    
*   **分红代币：**填写分红币合约地址（必须与BNB有交易对且流动性充足，即流动性较好的主流币，如果流动性过低，则可能**无法分红**）
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FiBr92if1s8keGH08kF8U%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e739eaf4&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/token/black-hole#san-mai-ru-shuil0x25)

三、买入税率**（0**≤x<**25%）**

*   **营销税率**：买入扣除后，合约触发阈值自动卖出换成分红币发到营销钱包
    
*   **回流税率**：交易中指定额度的代币将会自动添加到流动池内,保证交易始终存在流动性
    
*   **分红税率**：交易中指定额度的代币会按持币比例分配给所有持币者,实现持币分红
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FsG6hGn0Phc9asGumjRtI%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6591f87&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/token/black-hole#si-mai-chu-shuil0x25)

四、卖出税率**（0**≤x<**25%）**

*   包括营销、分红、回流，与买入税率逻辑相同，只在卖出交易时生效
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FCvKuKgeO9ZX6LQ1MVnC7%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=22d4029f&sv=2)

circle-exclamation

买入和卖出税率不能超过25%,交易总税率不能超过50%

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/token/black-hole#wu-qi-ta-can-shu)

五、其他参数

*   **营销钱包**：接收营销税率对应的本币（可设置当前钱包）
    
*   **选择交易所**：PancakeSwap
    
*   **选择底池代币**：WBNB / USDT 等，后续添加流动性需使用同样代币
    
*   **黑洞分红最小销毁量**：即销毁阈值，指的是**销毁**多少代币才能获得分红资格(第一次转入黑洞的地址必须大于这个数值，否则不能获得分红）
    

triangle-exclamation

**注：**黑洞分红最小销毁量在合约创建完成后，数值**不可修改！！！**

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FZqK4guoKSKG4TyXtAocN%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1e11d5c1&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/token/black-hole#liu-xiang-guan-gong-neng-kai-guan-can-shu)

六、相关功能开关参数

**1\. 手动开启交易**

*   check
    
    打开：添加池子后的首次交易需要在控制台手动开启
    
*   关闭：则添加流动性后立即可以进行交易
    

**2\. 税率开关**

*   check
    
    打开：创建后可手动调整买卖税率，但是买卖税率都需要为0≤25%
    
*   关闭：无法修改滑点，后期也不能再次开启
    

circle-exclamation

注：开启后无法再关闭

**3\. 黑名单功能**

*   check
    
    打开：可添加/解除黑名单，被拉黑地址无法转账或卖币
    
*   关闭：无法使用
    

**4\. 最大持币量**

*   check
    
    打开：可添加/解除黑名单，被拉黑地址无法转账或卖币
    
*   关闭：无法使用
    

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/token/black-hole#chang-jian-wen-ti-faq)

❓常见问题 FAQ

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/token/black-hole#id-1.-liang-ge-hei-dong-di-zhi-dou-zhi-chi-fen-hong-ma)

**1\. 两个黑洞地址都支持分红吗？**

*   check
    
    不是的，目前只支持1个黑洞地址，即：0x000000000000000000000000000000000000dE，另一个黑洞地址是不支持的，不要往里面转币
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/token/black-hole#id-2.-wei-shen-me-jiao-yi-le-hen-duo-bi-hai-shi-mei-you-fen-hong)

**2\. 为什么交易了很多笔还是没有分红？**

*   check
    
    不要使用白名单地址交易；不要只买，必须有卖单，才能分红；请确保具有分红资格；可以等待一段时间看看。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/token/black-hole#id-3.-zhuan-ru-hei-dong-hou-di-zhi-xu-yao-ji-huo-ma)

**3\. 转入黑洞后地址需要激活吗？**

*   check
    
    不需要，将代币转入黑洞之后，等着就行
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/token/black-hole#id-4.-zhuan-ru-hei-dong-de-fen-hong-yu-zhi-hai-neng-xiu-gai-ma)

**4\. 转入黑洞的分红阈值还能修改吗？**

*   check
    
    注意，该数值不支持修改，有权限也不行，所以创建合约的时候一定要控制好
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/token/black-hole#id-5.-zhuan-ru-hei-dong-de-bi-you-lai-yuan-xian-zhi-huo-zhe-shi-jian-xian-zhi)

**5\. 转入黑洞的币有来源限制或者时间限制？**

*   check
    
    有的。不论是他人转给你的币，还是你自己买入的币，都可以转入黑洞参与分红；无论在开启交易前还是开启交易后转入，均不受任何限制。
    

**💬 如遇到问题？加入社群实时咨询**：[https://t.me/ciaotoolarrow-up-right](https://t.me/ciaotool)

*   **Email**：[support@ciaotool.ioenvelope](mailto:support@ciaotool.io)
    
*   **官网**：[https://ciaotool.ioarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/)
    
*   **X（Twitter）**：[https://x.com/CiaoToolarrow-up-right](https://x.com/CiaoTool)
    
*   **Medium**： [https://medium.com/@ciaotoolarrow-up-right](https://medium.com/@ciaotool)
    
*   **Blog**：[https://www.ciaoailiquidity.com/zh/blogarrow-up-right](https://www.ciaoailiquidity.com/zh/blog)
    
*   **YouTube**：[https://www.youtube.com/@CiaoToolarrow-up-right](https://www.youtube.com/@CiaoTool)
    
*   **WhatsApp**：[https://whatsapp.com/channel/0029VbAuLrVAojYxRNw95W1Jarrow-up-right](https://whatsapp.com/channel/0029VbAuLrVAojYxRNw95W1J)
    

triangle-exclamation

CiaoTool 致力于提供便捷的工具服务，但不构成任何投资建议。平台内容可能根据产品迭代进行调整，敬请用户自行判断并留意更新。

# Market Making Tutorial「 v2 and v3」 | 「EVM」Tutorial | CiaoTool

circle-check

**Market Making v2：**[https://bsc.ciaotool.io/swap/v2/market-making-manage-v2arrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/swap/v2/market-making-manage-v2)

circle-check

**Market Making v3:** [https://bsc.ciaotool.io/swap/v3/market-making-manage-v3arrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/swap/v3/market-making-manage-v3)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/swap/batch-swap-v2-v3#how-to-use-the-market-making-management)

✅ How to Use the Market Making Management?

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/swap/batch-swap-v2-v3#id-1.-select-token)

1\. Select Token

*   Enter the target token address in the input box or select from the dropdown menu of tokens held by the current wallet.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FcL6r1KVJmw4jLFWVpQbl%2Fblobs%2FUiZLQvqfngtYMx3wETKq%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6d863ffd&sv=2)

*   Quickly switch between trade directions (From: token to spend, To: token to receive).
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FcL6r1KVJmw4jLFWVpQbl%2Fblobs%2F7daW2BmHizYa4mhSEMnT%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6821d794&sv=2)

circle-exclamation

**Note:** For V3 batch trading, only the trading pair address needs to be imported.

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FcL6r1KVJmw4jLFWVpQbl%2Fblobs%2FZrw3YaNAbg1tB1p4pme1%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=782460a2&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/swap/batch-swap-v2-v3#id-2.-set-trade-parameters)

2\. Set Trade Parameters

*   Choose the trade amount mode: **Fixed Amount、Fixed Retain、All Amount.**
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FcL6r1KVJmw4jLFWVpQbl%2Fblobs%2FbEwC0xDtQdag6ycXLc1O%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=75b8af00&sv=2)

*   Set transaction speed, and trade Interval (Unit: seconds ⏱️).
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FcL6r1KVJmw4jLFWVpQbl%2Fblobs%2F7F2mVb6jB4sekvYpbwgd%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=54e4c8c1&sv=2)

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FcL6r1KVJmw4jLFWVpQbl%2Fblobs%2FTvBVJneKBth2NgEOApu9%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e1cd422d&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/swap/batch-swap-v2-v3#id-3.-import-wallet-private-key)

3\. Import Wallet Private Key

*   Import the private key of the wallet used to pay transaction fees (the private key must be different from the trading wallet’s private key).
    

circle-info

Please ensure the security of your private key and do not disclose it to unauthorized parties.

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/swap/batch-swap-v2-v3#id-4.-set-stop-method-and-loop-execution-count)

4\. Set Stop Method and Loop Execution Count

*   Stop by Execution Count: Control Trading Intensity and Rhythm
    
*   Stop by Price Range: Avoid Overbought Conditions or Price Band Breaches
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FcL6r1KVJmw4jLFWVpQbl%2Fblobs%2FFYRaRnKHdjbV5y729aUr%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=efc45e7e&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/swap/batch-swap-v2-v3#id-5.-import-wallets-for-batch-trading)

5\. Import Wallets for Batch Trading

*   You can upload a private key file for import.
    

circle-info

Each wallet involved in a transaction must hold a sufficient amount of BNB (0.0008 BNB) to cover transaction gas fees.

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FcL6r1KVJmw4jLFWVpQbl%2Fblobs%2FHWUYazUiUTdjgrWTlFmq%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3ac57baa&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/swap/batch-swap-v2-v3#id-6.-start-swap)

6\. Start Swap

*   Transaction speed may be affected by on-chain congestion. During periods of congestion, transactions may be slower; please be patient.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/swap/batch-swap-v2-v3#frequently-asked-questions-faq)

❓Frequently Asked Questions (FAQ)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/swap/batch-swap-v2-v3#id-1.-can-i-pause-operations-mid-run)

**1\.** Can I pause operations mid-run??

*   check
    
    **Answer**：Yes, you can pause or terminate immediately at any time without affecting asset reserves.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/swap/batch-swap-v2-v3#id-2.-why-does-market-capitalization-management-recommend-using-multiple-wallets)

**2\.** Why does market capitalization management recommend using multiple wallets??

*   check
    
    **Answer**：To diversify holdings, create more natural trading patterns, achieve more realistic order book depth, and avoid “single-wallet manipulation.”
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/swap/batch-swap-v2-v3#id-3.-what-is-the-purpose-of-the-fixed-retention-mode)

**3\.** What is the purpose of the fixed retention mode?

*   check
    
    **Answer**：YIt maintains consistent holding structures across wallets, presenting a more natural appearance externally and reducing panic selling pressure.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/swap/batch-swap-v2-v3#id-4.-what-are-common-reasons-for-execution-failures)

**4\.** What are common reasons for execution failures?

*   check
    
    **Answer**：Excessively low slippage tolerance, insufficient balance, RPC congestion, or inadequate Gas fees.

# 代币怎么上头像 (Logo) ？ | 「EVM」使用教程 | CiaoTool

circle-check

**一键发币：**[https://ciaotool.io/arrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/start/update-logo#wei-shen-me-dai-bi-ben-shen-mei-you-logo)

🔍 为什么代币本身没有 Logo？

*   在 **BSC、Ethereum 等链**上，代币的本质只是一个**智能合约**，链上**并不存在 Logo、简介、官网这些信息**。你在钱包、交易所、行情网站里看到的所有代币头像，其实都是：
    

> 由各个平台自行维护和展示的“元数据”

*   这些平台给代币加 Logo，主要是为了三件事：提升识别度、降低用户误操作风险，以及增强项目在用户心中的专业感和可信度。
    

**因此：想让代币显示 Logo，唯一的方法就是——去各个平台单独申请。**

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/start/update-logo#cong-ji-chu-zhan-shi-dao-ping-tai-ren-ke)

🧩 从基础展示到平台认可

1.  很多项目方在发币后，第一反应就是去申请 CMC、CoinGecko，或者希望 PancakeSwap、Uniswap 能立刻显示 Logo。
    
2.  不建议一上来就冲顶级平台，而是按**显示优先级 + 审核通过率**来推进。
    
3.  一个常见、合理的顺序是：**钱包 / 信息平台 → 区块浏览器 → 数据聚合平台 → 自动抓取**
    

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/start/update-logo#chang-jian-de-qian-bao-yu-xin-xi-ping-tai)

🎯 常见的钱包与信息平台

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/start/update-logo#id-1.-ave.ai-xin-xi-ju-he-ping-tai)

**1\. Ave.ai（信息聚合平台）**

**Ave.ai 信息聚合平台:** 通常会同时展示代币 Logo、简介、官网和社交链接，流程简单、审核友好，非常适合新项目或 Meme 代币。

*   **申请方式：**自行联系 Ave 客服
    
*   **要求：**基本没要求
    
*   **成功率：**高
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252FimYfa0eUmuWCkMCH0UCs%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dcc9754a7-97fa-4be5-86c8-f3fc85317c7a&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=2fa9efc2&sv=2)

circle-info

一旦 Ave 显示成功，**很多第三方工具和插件也会同步抓取信息**。

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/start/update-logo#id-2.-tokenpockettp-qian-bao)

**2\. TokenPocket（TP 钱包）**

**TP 钱包**的代币 Logo 是通过官方申请表提交，需要严格按文档格式提交，会检查合约是否存在黑名单、暂停交易等高风险逻辑。

*   **申请方式：**自行提交申请表
    
*   **要求：**正规的官网、代币信息，合约没有黑名单/暂停交易等功能
    
*   **成功率：**中高
    

👉 **官方提交文档：**[https://www.tokenpocket.pro/zh/submit/tokenarrow-up-right](https://www.tokenpocket.pro/zh/submit/token)

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252Fmv1I9vyJ6MSRlOAPL26g%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D590575cf-3996-41b3-9376-defdb1d15738&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=c4165da&sv=2)

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/start/update-logo#id-3.-bitget-wallet)

**3\. Bitget Wallet**

**Bitget Wallet** 通常通过其官网后台进行项目资料提交，主要用于钱包内资产列表展示，审核相对友好，但偶尔会被打回。

*   **申请方式：**自行登录提交申请表
    
*   **要求：**正规的官网、代币信息，合约没有黑名单/暂停交易等功能
    
*   **成功率：**中高
    

👉 **官方申请入口:** [https://web3.bitget.com/en/business/service/token-managearrow-up-right](https://web3.bitget.com/en/business/service/token-manage)

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252FSpRQnCHV6FEqcfJwS63C%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D9771ae58-721b-4ba6-af37-ce03eede095c&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=168b5b9c&sv=2)

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/start/update-logo#id-4.-okx-web3-qian-bao-tong-guo-oklink)

**4\. OKX Web3 钱包（通过 OKLink）**

**OKX Web3** 钱包的代币 Logo，**本质来源于 OKLink 区块浏览器**。只要你的代币在 OKLink 浏览器中显示了 Logo，Web3 钱包中通常也会同步展示，审核相对严格。

*   **申请方式：**自行提交申请表
    
*   **要求：**正规的官网、代币信息，合约没有黑名单/暂停交易等功能
    
*   **成功率：**中
    

**👉 官方提交表单**：[https://docs.google.com/forms/d/e/1FAIpQLSclmaci1m0y6JB5A-o7xu4akvhXNlzgyBqP5\_9fpf\_6TTNSMQ/viewformarrow-up-right](https://docs.google.com/forms/d/e/1FAIpQLSclmaci1m0y6JB5A-o7xu4akvhXNlzgyBqP5_9fpf_6TTNSMQ/viewform)

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252FDMvpzVPzFnCfnv32zZlX%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D25bdabda-636e-4b8e-985d-2ae9dbd138ae&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=84d9e616&sv=2)

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/start/update-logo#id-5.-imtoken-qian-bao)

**5\. imToken 钱包**

imToken 的逻辑比较特殊，只要符合 **ERC20和 EOS 代币标准，**并且链上存在**成功的转账记录，**钱包就能自动识别并显示代币。

imToken 还支持项目方通过 **GitHub** 自主提交或修改 Token 信息，包括：**Token 名称、Symbol、Logo。**

*   **申请方式：**自行提交申请表
    
*   **要求：**符合 **ERC20和 EOS 代币标准，**并且链上存在**成功的转账记录**
    
*   **成功率：高**
    

**👉 官方教程：**[https://github.com/consenlabs/token-profile/blob/master/README.zh-CN.mdarrow-up-right](https://github.com/consenlabs/token-profile/blob/master/README.zh-CN.md)

* * *

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/start/update-logo#id-6.-trust-wallet)

**6\. Trust Wallet**

Trust Wallet 使用的是一个**社区维护的 Token 信息库**，需要通过 GitHub 提交审核维度非常多（官网、社交、邮箱、创建者钱包等），审核周期长，通过率相对较低。

*   **申请方式：**自行提交
    
*   **要求：**正规的官网、代币信息，社交媒体链接、官网邮箱、创建者钱包
    
*   **成功率：低**
    

**👉 官网：**[https://assets.trustwallet.com/arrow-up-right](https://assets.trustwallet.com/)

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252FKjaozyj4uiwXsEIpWPRk%252Ftelegram-cloud-photo-size-5-6282633703842320239-y.jpg%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2e05e2f3-6014-4cf1-8055-36c36571fd1d&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=e0f00499&sv=2)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/start/update-logo#qu-kuai-liu-lan-qi-de-dai-bi-logo-shen-qing)

🔗 区块浏览器的代币 Logo 申请

所谓“区块浏览器 Logo”，指的是在对应公链的**官方区块浏览器**中显示代币图标，例如：

*   **BSC** → [BscScanarrow-up-right](https://bscscan.com/)
    
*   **Ethereum** → [Etherscanarrow-up-right](https://etherscan.io/)
    

一旦浏览器侧成功显示：钱包、数据平台、DEX等**都有更高概率自动抓取你的代币 Logo。**但需要注意：审核要求通常较高、更偏向“有官网、有社交、有持续运营”的项目。

*   **申请方式：**自行提交申请表
    
*   **要求：**正规的官网、代币信息，社交媒体链接、官网邮箱、创建者钱包
    
*   **成功率：低**
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/start/update-logo#bsc-bscscan-xiang-xi-jiao-cheng)

**BSC →** [**BscScan**arrow-up-right](https://bscscan.com/)
 **详细教程**

1.  找到 Info 页面，点击更新信息。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252FmPgUikbfzBS9hI9t8zVt%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddf878a5b-bf4a-4dda-95c9-749b61bd2596&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=dd303391&sv=2)

1.  **登录 BscScan 账户**，使用你的钱包验证Token创建者或合约开发者身份。
    
2.  选择你想提交的表单类型。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252F3lv3KQpZYNfKwMEpBgsM%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4bc0c75e-2fdb-4a97-8721-cbbb4aa2a6c8&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=ae19b69b&sv=2)

1.  填写完整表单及你想更新或新增的信息。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252Fs1P63wMTLgzVUGgSYm5Z%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Daa22273b-a1b1-4b23-9397-f7058cfa1c32&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=5171978&sv=2)![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252FGu00uLyNpGae4sCmGY2x%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db51bf69d-31fb-44f0-aa71-70125e48f6be&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=fdab0032&sv=2)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/start/update-logo#cmc-cg-de-shou-lu)

🌍 CMC / **CG的收录**

[**CoinMarketCap**arrow-up-right](https://coinmarketcap.com/)
**（CMC）**和 [**CoinGecko**arrow-up-right](https://www.coingecko.com/)
**（CG）**本质上是：**全球级的加密数据权威平台**

*   如果代币被成功收录：Logo 会同步展示、PancakeSwap / Uniswap / 钱包类工具更容易抓取、对外宣传和市场信任度显著提升。
    
*   但现实情况是：审核严格、更适合已经有一定交易量和用户基础的项目。
    
*   **申请方式：**自行提交**官方申请表**或**联系我们**：[https://t.me/ciaotoolarrow-up-right](https://t.me/ciaotool)
    
*   **要求：**正规的官网、代币信息，社交媒体链接、官网邮箱、创建者钱包
    
*   **成功率：低**
    

circle-exclamation

**注意：**由于这两个平台的收录费用较高，申请时请务必通过官方或可信渠道，谨防诈骗。

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252FC4AFhOBx4XuA4VARYUgA%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D2fc308b2-4346-41e0-9a85-f3c573298ae1&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=1b9acc9f&sv=2)

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252F4f7zyNCWmnk1Rvd9sqy6%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Da90d2313-d96a-4d6c-bb8b-e8a40ba8d664&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=dbdf358a&sv=2)

* * *

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/start/update-logo#pancakeswap-uniswap-de-geng-xin)

📊 PancakeSwap / Uniswap 的更新

对于普通代币，PancakeSwap / Uniswap 本身没有一个像 Ave.ai 那样的直接付款或简单申请通道，Logo 显示取决于以下因素:

*   **钱包/平台收录：** 代币需要先在 TP钱包、Bitget钱包 等钱包中显示 Logo。
    
*   **数据聚合平台收录：** 代币被 CoinMarketCap (CMC) 或 CoinGecko (CG) 收录，有时会同步这些数据。
    
*   **去中心化收录（DEX聚合）：** 通过 DEXTools 等工具间接或项目方自行更新资料来影响显示。
    

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/start/update-logo#metamask-xiao-hu-li-qian-bao-logo-geng-xin)

💡 MetaMask（小狐狸钱包）logo更新

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/start/update-logo#deng-dai-guan-fang-shu-ju-jian-suo-huo-shou-dong-geng-xin)

**⬆️ 等待官方数据检索或手动更新**

*   代币已经被收录在主流平台（如 CG、CMC、Etherscan 等），等待更新即可。
    
*   如果未更新，用户可通过这些平台去一键添加，将代币及其官方 Logo 自动添加进钱包，确认钱包弹窗即可。
    

circle-exclamation

**注意：**手动更新的前提是已被主流平台收录。

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252FFsqVUUOd6qNLPxrh6cH7%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D70673c8c-01e4-468b-a5a0-0fe18aa65431&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=dfc06159&sv=2)

# 移除流动性「v2」教程 | 「EVM」使用教程 | CiaoTool

circle-check

**移除流动性 v2：**[https://bsc.ciaotool.io/swap/v2/create-liquidity-v2arrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/swap/v2/create-liquidity-v2)

circle-exclamation

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/remove-liquidity-v2#bi-xu-que-bao-yuechong-zu-qian-bao-nei-zhi-shao-you-0.03-bnb)

**必须确保余额充足，钱包内至少有 0.03 BNB**

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/remove-liquidity-v2#yi-chu-liu-dong-xing-v2-xiang-xi-liu-cheng)

**🛠️ 移除流动性 v2 详细流程**

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/remove-liquidity-v2#id-1-lian-jie-qian-bao)

**1️⃣ 连接钱包**

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2F8AhGayayJ4AHNtEmNeFz%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7c71d944&sv=2)

*   输入用于移除流动性的私钥
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2Fp6nIIrKtBcHbEb8o9ze8%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=aeb41112&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/remove-liquidity-v2#id-2-xuan-ze-yi-chu-de-dai-bi)

**2️⃣ 选择移除的代币**

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2Fp68nasda5YuTULUxIfzc%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a1294194&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/remove-liquidity-v2#id-3-she-zhi-yi-chu-bi-li)

**3️⃣ 设置移除比例**

*   设置移除比例：25%、50%、75%、100%
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2F5ycY8rdTYLhmVyf6gced%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=ea3bd510&sv=2)

circle-info

**关于比例：**假设池子都是您一个人加的， 那么这个百分比=池子的百分比。如果池子是多个人加的，就需要另外算的。比如，您本身占有池子份额的20%。那么您即便选择100%，整个池子也只是锁了20%的流动性而已。如果您选择20%，那么整个池子也就是锁了4%的流动性。

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/remove-liquidity-v2#id-4-shou-quan-dai-bi)

**4️⃣ 授权代币**

*   第一次操作时，需要授权合约使用你的代币。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/remove-liquidity-v2#id-5-yi-chu-liu-dong-xing)

**5️⃣ 移除流动性**

*   检查无误后，点击 **“开始交易”** 按钮。
    

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/remove-liquidity-v2#chang-jian-wen-ti-faq)

❓ 常见问题**FAQ**

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/remove-liquidity-v2#id-1.-che-chi-hou-dai-bi-hai-neng-jiao-yi-ma)

**1\. 撤池后代币还能交易吗？**

*   check
    
    如果全部移除是不能交易的，只是移除添加一部分是还能交易的。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/remove-liquidity-v2#id-2.-yi-chu-hui-shou-qu-fei-yong-ma)

**2\. 移除会收取费用吗？**

*   check
    
    会的，移除流动性是按次收费，每次0.024BNB

*   **官网**：[https://ciaotool.ioarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/)

*   **YouTube**：[https://www.youtube.com/@CiaoToolarrow-up-right](https://www.youtube.com/@CiaoTool)

# 一键冷换仓教程-通用版 | 「EVM」使用教程 | CiaoTool

circle-check

**BSC 冷换仓**：[https://bsc.ciaotool.io/assert-migration/assert-migration-coldarrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/assert-migration/assert-migration-cold)

**Base 冷换仓**：[https://base.ciaotool.io/assert-migration/assert-migration-coldarrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/assert-migration/assert-migration-cold)

**X Layer 冷换仓**：[https://xlayer.ciaotool.io/assert-migration/assert-migration-coldarrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/assert-migration/assert-migration-cold)

**IoTeX 冷换仓**：[https://iotex.ciaotool.io/assert-migration/assert-migration-coldarrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/assert-migration/assert-migration-cold)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/migration/assert-migration-cold#gong-neng-jian-jie)

📁 功能简介

CiaoTool 提供的「一键冷换仓」工具，帮助您将持有的代币从指定钱包地址中，**快速迁移至多个新生成地址**，从而：

*   降低单地址持仓比例，分散风险
    
*   美化气泡图，减少项目“控盘”嫌疑
    
*   为换仓后钱包提供干净操作起点
    

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/migration/assert-migration-cold#yi-jian-leng-huan-cang-cao-zuo-liu-cheng)

🔗 一键冷换仓操作流程

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/migration/assert-migration-cold#di-1-bu-xuan-ze-yao-huan-cang-de-dai-bi)

第 1 步：选择要换仓的代币

在代币选择列表中，挑选你希望分散的**代币**，或输入代币地址，系统将自动识别余额。

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FeTv3B2zlLbfEhHHAgP5u%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b7296ab&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/migration/assert-migration-cold#di-2-bu-dao-ru-zhuan-chu-qian-bao-jiu-di-zhi)

第 2 步：导入转出钱包（旧地址）

你可以通过以下任意方式导入转出钱包列表：

*   **手动输入私钥**
    
*   **上传私钥 xls、xlsx格式文件**
    

系统会校验所有钱包地址及对应代币余额，仅对有余额的钱包发起换仓操作。

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FJlRstZYPeW638ZcaF0nn%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=75bacc17&sv=2)

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2F6tuRTAoTzQLhuhabHMOg%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8fdce871&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/migration/assert-migration-cold#di-3-bu-she-zhi-mei-ge-di-zhi-de-huan-cang-shu-liang)

第 3 步：设置每个地址的换仓数量

在界面中输入你希望分散到每个地址的代币数量：

circle-info

举例：如果你导入了一个持有 1000 枚代币的钱包，并选择每个地址分配 10 枚，系统将自动生成 100 个地址来接收资产。

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/migration/assert-migration-cold#di-4-bu-sheng-cheng-mu-biao-jie-shou-di-zhi-xin-qian-bao)

第 4 步：生成目标接收地址（新钱包）

点击【一键生成钱包】，系统会自动创建所需数量的新地址，作为换仓目标地址。所有钱包密钥将在本地生成，并可导出备份。

你也可以选择【上传地址】或【粘贴地址列表】，使用自己预先准备好的目标地址。

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/migration/assert-migration-cold#di-5-bu-que-ren-bing-zhi-xing)

第 5 步：确认并执行

在页面底部预览交易总数和目标地址分布后，点击【开始换仓】。系统将：

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2F9dCcJDpHaPMVzSZnjiAt%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=331fa940&sv=2)

按设置的数量从源钱包转出代币。

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/migration/assert-migration-cold#dao-chu-huan-cang-jie-guo-ke-xuan)

📁 导出换仓结果（可选）

完成后你可以导出所有新生成地址和对应余额的表格（xls、xlsx格式），便于后续管理或转回。

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/migration/assert-migration-cold#chang-jian-wen-ti)

❓ 常见问题

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/migration/assert-migration-cold#id-1.-yi-jian-leng-huan-cang-de-zuo-yong-shi-shen-me)

1\. 一键冷换仓的作用是什么？

*   check
    
    答： 冷换仓可将代币从当前地址分散转移至大量新地址，降低单一地址持仓比例，优化链上分布结构，增强项目安全性和隐蔽性。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/migration/assert-migration-cold#id-2.-wei-shen-me-huan-cang-hou-yao-shi-yong-xin-sheng-cheng-de-qian-bao-di-zhi)

2\. 为什么换仓后要使用新生成的钱包地址？

*   check
    
    答： 新地址无历史交易记录，可避免被链上工具标记为“关联钱包”，更适合用于策略重建和分散操作。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/migration/assert-migration-cold#id-3.-huan-cang-guo-cheng-zhong-shi-fou-hui-xie-lou-si-yao)

3\. 换仓过程中是否会泄露私钥？

*   check
    
    答： 不会。CiaoTool 所有交易均在本地浏览器完成签名，**不会上传或存储私钥**，确保资产安全。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/migration/assert-migration-cold#id-4.-shi-fou-ke-yi-zi-ding-yi-huan-cang-di-zhi-he-zhuan-zhang-jine)

4\. 是否可以自定义换仓地址和转账金额？

*   check
    
    答： 可以。你可以选择系统自动生成钱包，每笔转账金额可选固定值或输入自定义数量。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/migration/assert-migration-cold#id-5.-huan-cang-guo-cheng-zhong-wang-luo-zhong-duan-hui-ying-xiang-cao-zuo-ma)

5\. 换仓过程中网络中断会影响操作吗？

*   check
    
    答： 不会。CiaoTool 支持断点恢复机制，系统会在中断后记录未完成的地址，并允许你重新发起剩余部分的换仓任务。
    

**💬 如遇到问题？加入社群实时咨询**：[https://t.me/ciaotoolarrow-up-right](https://t.me/ciaotool)

*   **Email**：[support@ciaotool.ioenvelope](mailto:support@ciaotool.io)
    
*   **官网**：[https://ciaotool.ioarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/)
    
*   **X（Twitter）**：[https://x.com/CiaoToolarrow-up-right](https://x.com/CiaoTool)
    
*   **Medium**： [https://medium.com/@ciaotoolarrow-up-right](https://medium.com/@ciaotool)
    
*   **Blog**：[https://www.ciaoailiquidity.com/zh/blogarrow-up-right](https://www.ciaoailiquidity.com/zh/blog)
    
*   **YouTube**：[https://www.youtube.com/@CiaoToolarrow-up-right](https://www.youtube.com/@CiaoTool)
    
*   **WhatsApp**：[https://whatsapp.com/channel/0029VbAuLrVAojYxRNw95W1Jarrow-up-right](https://whatsapp.com/channel/0029VbAuLrVAojYxRNw95W1J)

# 标准代币创建教程-通用版 | 「EVM」使用教程 | CiaoTool

circle-check

**BSC标准代币**：[https://bsc.ciaotool.io/token/create-tokenarrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/token/create-token)

**Base标准代币**：[https://base.ciaotool.io/token/create-tokenarrow-up-right](https://base.ciaotool.io/token/create-token)

**X Layer标准代币**：[https://xlayer.ciaotool.io/token/create-tokenarrow-up-right](https://xlayer.ciaotool.io/token/create-token)

**IoTeX标准代币**：[https://iotex.ciaotool.io/token/create-tokenarrow-up-right](https://iotex.ciaotool.io/token/create-token)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/token/create-token#ru-he-chuang-jian-biao-zhun-dai-bi)

🪙 **如何创建标准代币**

1\. 选择你要创建代币的**区块链**

1\. 打开 **【代币管理】**操作界面

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2F3ZcOw04Q2FVpH5YmTHnR%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=731f9378&sv=2)

2\. 连接支持 **EVM链** 的钱包（**小狐狸-Metamask**）

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FxXSBvC74ceYqinGhAUfh%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=42562c45&sv=2)

**3.输入代币信息**：包括项目代币的全称、简称、发行总量与精度。

circle-exclamation

**示例：假设你想创建一个名称为** [**CiaoTool** arrow-up-right](https://www.ciaotool.io/)
**的代币**

代币全称：CiaoTool

代币简称：C

精度：18

发行量：10000000（10M)

circle-info

精度：代币精度（Token Decimals）指的是一种代币最小可以分割到的小数位数。简单来说，它决定了你可以将一枚代币分成多小的单位。

**BSC、ETH等EVM公链**：最大精度通常为18。这意味着1个代币可以被分割为10^18个最小单位。

circle-exclamation

**发行总量：你想让用户看到的代币总量。**

**4.创建代币：确认信息及**确认交易并签名

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FnaGszS1glseZrYk0gv9W%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=47d1165b&sv=2)

**5\. 完成后怎么在钱包查看代币？（以小狐狸- Metamask为例）**

1.  打开你的钱包，插件钱包或APP程序
    
2.  找到代币页面-选择添加代币
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FAPA2BpGAbSxRd0loKfVb%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=71aaa5bf&sv=2)

1.  选择你创建代币所在的链，两种模式添加，这里我们选择自定义代币
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FVNbphA0SsBNOaX6ciKZV%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=80a2491c&sv=2)

1.  粘贴你的代币合约，即可查看你的代币信息，点击导入即可
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FQWAT0R7sx45q3vHRzjDU%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1f524049&sv=2)

**6\. 添加流动性**

*   代币创建完成之后，只能转账，还不能交易。要想使代币可以交易，需要前往创建一个流动性资金池才可以。
    
*   目前CiaoTool-BSC链已经支持加池了，V2或V3池子, [详细的操作步骤请查看](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/create-add-liquidity-v2)
    

circle-check

**创建流动性V2:** [https://bsc.ciaotool.io/swap/v2/create-liquidity-v2arrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/swap/v2/create-liquidity-v2)

**创建流动性V3:** [https://bsc.ciaotool.io/swap/v3/add-liquidity-v3arrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/swap/v3/add-liquidity-v3)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/token/create-token#chang-jian-wen-ti-faq)

❓常见问题 FAQ

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/token/create-token#id-1.-shen-me-shi-biao-zhun-dai-bi-chuang-jian-gong-ju)

1\. 什么是标准代币创建工具？

*   check
    
    这是一个零代码的快速发币工具，让你几分钟内创建属于自己的代币。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/token/create-token#id-2.-chuang-jian-dai-bi-an-quan-ma)

2\. 创建代币安全吗？

*   check
    
    是的，所有操作通过本地签名完成，合约开源透明，并支持外部审计。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/token/create-token#id-3.-fa-bi-liu-cheng-yao-duo-jiu)

3\. 发币流程要多久？

*   check
    
    通常只需 2-5 分钟，代币部署完成后可立即在链上查看。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/token/create-token#id-4.-chuang-jian-dai-bi-xu-yao-duo-shao-qian)

4\. 创建代币需要多少钱？

*   check
    
    在 BSC 只需 0.024 BNB 服务费，另加链上 Gas 费（根据网络情况浮动）。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/token/create-token#id-5.-ru-he-she-zhi-fa-xing-liang-he-jing-du)

5\. 如何设置发行量和精度？

*   check
    
    发币界面支持自定义总量和小数精度，常用设置为 18 位。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/token/create-token#id-6.-wo-ke-yi-chuang-jian-duo-ge-dai-bi-ma)

6\. 我可以创建多个代币吗？

*   check
    
    当然可以，每次创建都是独立的代币合约，互不影响。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/token/create-token#id-7.-fa-bi-hou-hai-neng-gai-can-shu-ma)

7\. 发币后还能改参数吗？

*   check
    
    不能，代币总量和精度是不可变的。修改需重新创建新代币。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/token/create-token#id-8.-dai-bi-ru-he-guan-li)

8\. 代币如何管理？

*   check
    
    你可以用钱包发送代币，也可结合批量转账工具空投或进行社区治理。
    

**💬 如遇到问题？加入社群实时咨询**：[https://t.me/ciaotoolarrow-up-right](https://t.me/ciaotool)

# Remove Liquidity v3 Tutorial | 「EVM」Tutorial | CiaoTool

circle-check

**Remove Liquidity v2：**[https://bsc.ciaotool.io/swap/v3/remove-liquidity-v3arrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/swap/v3/remove-liquidity-v3)

*   If all liquidity is removed, the token will **no longer be tradable**.
    
*   All withdrawn tokens belong to the **wallet that performs the removal**.
    

circle-exclamation

⚠️ **Make sure your wallet balance is sufficient**: at least **0.03 BNB** is required.

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/swap/removing-liquidity-v3#remove-liquidity-v3-detailed-guide)

🛠️ **Remove Liquidity v3 – Detailed Guide**

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/swap/removing-liquidity-v3#id-1.-connect-wallet)

1\. **Connect Wallet**

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FcL6r1KVJmw4jLFWVpQbl%2Fblobs%2FIaACxCq8YoqfmZOx0TLf%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b13638ea&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/swap/removing-liquidity-v3#id-2.-enter-the-private-key-used-to-create-or-add-liquidity)

2\. Enter the private key used to create or add liquidity.

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FcL6r1KVJmw4jLFWVpQbl%2Fblobs%2Fuop9eBfw4iw9169lSLrz%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4cac70c&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/swap/removing-liquidity-v3#id-3.-set-removal-percentage)

**3\.** Set Removal Percentage

*   Enter the liquidity ratio to remove: Custom, **max 100%**. Click Max to set.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FcL6r1KVJmw4jLFWVpQbl%2Fblobs%2F4EGgUdHJauSaLW4MnKsb%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=bd2dc5d3&sv=2)

circle-info

**About the percentage:**

*   If you are the **only liquidity provider**, the selected percentage equals the same percentage of the entire pool.
    
*   If there are **multiple liquidity providers**, the percentage applies only to **your share** of the pool.
    

**Example:** If you own **20%** of the pool:

*   Selecting **100%** removes only **20%** of the total pool liquidity.
    
*   Selecting **20%** removes **4%** of the total pool liquidity.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/swap/removing-liquidity-v3#id-4.-select-the-liquidity-to-be-removed)

4\. Select the liquidity to be removed.

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/swap/removing-liquidity-v3#id-5.-remove-liquidity)

5\. Remove Liquidity

After verifying all details, click the **“Start Swap”** button.

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/swap/removing-liquidity-v3#frequently-asked-questions-faq)

❓ Frequently Asked Questions (FAQ)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/swap/removing-liquidity-v3#id-1.-can-the-token-still-be-traded-after-removing-liquidity)

1\. Can the token still be traded after removing liquidity?

*   check
    
    **Answer**：If **all liquidity** is removed, trading is **no longer possible**. If only **part** of the liquidity is removed, the token can still be traded.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/swap/removing-liquidity-v3#id-2.-is-there-a-fee-for-removing-liquidity)

2\. Is there a fee for removing liquidity?

*   check
    
    **Answer**：Yes. Removing liquidity is charged **per transaction**, at **0.024 BNB** each time.
    

💬 **Need help? Join our community for real-time support:** [https://t.me/ciaotoolarrow-up-right](https://t.me/ciaotool)

*   **Email:** [support@ciaotool.ioenvelope](mailto:support@ciaotool.io)
    
*   **Website:** [https://ciaotool.ioarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/)
    
*   **X (Twitter):** [https://x.com/CiaoToolarrow-up-right](https://x.com/CiaoTool)

# 创建并买入-BNB/USD1/USDT教程 | 「EVM」使用教程 | CiaoTool

circle-check

**Flap创建并买入-BNB:** [https://bsc.ciaotool.io/flap/bnb/create-and-buyarrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/flap/bnb/create-and-buy)

circle-check

**Flap创建并买入-USD1:** [https://bsc.ciaotool.io/flap/usd1/create-and-buyarrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/flap/usd1/create-and-buy)

circle-check

**Flap创建并买入-USDT:** [https://bsc.ciaotool.io/flap/usdt/create-and-buyarrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/flap/usdt/create-and-buy)

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/flap/create-and-buy#ru-he-zai-flap-chuang-jian-bing-mai-ru)

🪜 如何在Flap创建并买入?


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/flap/create-and-buy#id-1.-lian-jie-qian-bao)

1.连接钱包

*   点击右上角【连接钱包】，选择钱包地址并确认授权。
    
*   页面右上角显示钱包地址即表示绑定成功。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/flap/create-and-buy#id-2.-tian-xie-dai-bi-ji-chu-xin-xi)

2\. **填写代币基础信息**

*   **私钥：**输入用于发币的控制地址私钥。注意安全，建议使用测试钱包或专用地址
    
*   **钱包地址 & 余额：**系统自动解析私钥生成钱包地址，并显示当前 BNB 余额
    
*   **Dev买入：**设置Dev买入数值
    
*   **代币名称：**Token 的完整名称（如：CiaoTool ）
    
*   **代币简称：**Token 符号（如：CIAO）
    
*   **描述：**简要介绍代币用途、故事或 Meme 背景（选填）
    
*   **上传图片：**上传 Token 图标，建议 1000×1000 像素，支持 jpg/png/webp/gif
    
*   **添加社交链接**：虽为可选项但强烈建议填写，**官网、X / Twitter、Telegram**
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2086467048-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%252Fuploads%252FIcYgm2idyzkt35gNq4cM%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D37af8e27-5b81-43cc-91f2-12b4c30c039b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8cb6252a&sv=2)

circle-exclamation

小贴士：一个完整的视觉资产（图标+命名）可以帮助你更快获得 Birdeye 图表站收录，提高用户点击率与传播潜力。即便是 Meme 项目，也建议预设一个 TG 群组 + 备用 Twitter 页面，有助于 CMC/CG 审核与用户获取信息。

circle-info

建议：即便是 Meme 项目，也建议预设一个 TG 群组 + 备用 Twitter 页面，有助于 CMC/CG 审核与用户获取信息。

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/flap/create-and-buy#id-3.-nei-pan-mai-ru-can-shu-pei-zhi)

3\. 内盘买入参数配置

*   内盘买入意味着：**你提前布局，控制初期价格走势**，在图表上线前通过脚本抢先买入。
    
*   **点击导入私钥**，批量添加最多 20 个参与地址
    
*   设置 USD1 买入金额
    
*   等待代币创建完成后，系统自动按参数挂单买入
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2086467048-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%252Fuploads%252FW4H1L9jVcbYGkLEXuEP0%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Ddbbcf447-6acd-4a35-ab7d-cc46cc18b7c0&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d3a8afaa&sv=2)

circle-info

**建议：** 内盘买入不宜过多，适合做图表“爬坡”用，控制节奏。

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/flap/create-and-buy#id-4.-wai-pan-mai-ru-can-shu-pei-zhi)

4\. 外盘买入参数配置

*   外盘买入代表：**当代币创建并上线类似 PancakeSwap后，**系统立即调用钱包发起真实交易行为**，模拟狙击或拉盘行为。**
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2086467048-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%252Fuploads%252FlPQEIISRJoSPCW27oknL%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dbd8bc3a9-699e-495c-8ae5-2848a5d39244&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8f275bed&sv=2)

**配置方式：**

*   添加私钥（最多 5 个）
    
*   设置 USD1 买入金额
    
*   等待代币创建完成后，系统自动按参数挂单买入
    

triangle-exclamation

买入地址的BNB余额必须大于 0.0008！

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/flap/create-and-buy#id-5.-dian-ji-chuang-jian-bing-mai-ru)

5\. 点击“创建并买入”

*   完成所有信息后，点击页面底部按钮
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FVtJda1FlsvZPB6NKQiep%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=3d323edd&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/flap/create-and-buy#chang-jian-wen-ti-faq)

❓ 常见问题 FAQ

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/flap/create-and-buy#id-1.-shen-me-shi-dev-mai-ru-kai-qi-hou-you-shen-me-zuo-yong)

1\. 什么是「Dev 买入」？开启后有什么作用？

*   check
    
    答：Dev 地址直接发起买入，确保创建后立即持仓，防止被抢跑。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/flap/create-and-buy#id-2.-nei-pan-mai-ru-he-wai-pan-mai-ru-de-qu-bie-shi-shen-me)

2\. 内盘买入和外盘买入的区别是什么？

*   check
    
    答：内盘是在 bonding curve 上预买入；外盘是在毕业后于 Pancake 上买入。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/flap/create-and-buy#id-3.-wei-shen-me-she-zhi-zui-duo-zhi-neng-tian-jia-5-ge-di-zhi)

**3\.** 为什么设置最多只能添加 5 个地址？

*   check
    
    答：由于交易打包容量有限，为保证成功率，目前限制为 5 个买入地址。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/flap/create-and-buy#id-4.-mai-ru-jinezen-me-pei-zhi-zui-he-shi)

4\. 买入金额怎么配置最合适？

*   check
    
    答：建议直接点击 `MAX`，内盘买入建议金额大于 10,500 USD1 或等值 BNB。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/flap/create-and-buy#id-5.-zhi-chi-quan-xian-pei-zhi-ma)

5\. 支持权限配置吗？

*   check
    
    答：暂不支持权限开关，所有代币为默认配置，适用于标准 Meme 场景。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/flap/create-and-buy#id-6.-flap-de-fa-pan-chu-shi-jia-ge-shi-duo-shao)

6\. Flap的发盘初始价格是多少？

*   check
    
    答：flap的发盘初始价格大约为 0.0000035.

# Multi-Address Bundled Buy Tutorial「v2 and v3」 | 「EVM」Tutorial | CiaoTool

circle-check

**Multi-Address Bundled Buy v2：**[https://bsc.ciaotool.io/swap/v2/multi-address-buy-v2arrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/swap/v2/multi-address-buy-v2)

circle-check

**Multi-Address Bundled Buy v3：**[https://bsc.ciaotool.io/swap/v3/multi-address-buy-v3arrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/swap/v3/multi-address-buy-v3)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/swap/multi-address-buy-v2-v3#multi-address-bundled-buy-tutorial)

🪜 Multi-Address Bundled Buy Tutorial

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/swap/multi-address-buy-v2-v3#id-1.-import-private-keys)

**1\.** Import Private Keys

*   Import the private key of the wallet used to pay for market value operation fees.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FcL6r1KVJmw4jLFWVpQbl%2Fblobs%2FnKtIRPfKGnHbO5W9ngvJ%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d5cea068&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/swap/multi-address-buy-v2-v3#id-2.-import-the-token-pair-address-or-select-the-token-pair)

2\. Import the Token pair address or select the Token pair.

*   v2-Enter the target token address in the input field, or click the dropdown menu to select a token currently held in your wallet.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FcL6r1KVJmw4jLFWVpQbl%2Fblobs%2FQqDZSL95cu2uytvo4vt1%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2db87b32&sv=2)

*   v3-Paste the target currency pair into the currency pair input field.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FcL6r1KVJmw4jLFWVpQbl%2Fblobs%2FNV3i5jlNxjLRetpEeJSU%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=542f55c7&sv=2)

circle-exclamation

The difference between v2 and v3 in the second step is as follows: v2 involves manually selecting two tokens, while v3 requires entering the coin pair address.

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/swap/multi-address-buy-v2-v3#id-3.-import-buying-wallet-private-keys)

3\. Import Buying Wallet Private Keys

*   Choose the batch import option — you can either manually paste multiple private keys or upload a file (xls、xlsx) containing the private keys.
    

circle-info

Note: Up to 20 wallet addresses can be imported in a single operation.

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/swap/multi-address-buy-v2-v3#id-4.-set-buy-in-parameters)

4\. Set Buy-in Parameters

**Configuration options:**

1.  Set a “buy-in amount” for each address. There is no upper limit for a single address; just refresh the balance to check.
    
2.  You can choose to refresh balances or adjust the buy-in proportion.
    
3.  The system will display the status of each address plus action buttons.
    

triangle-exclamation

Note: Each buying address must have **more than 0.0008 BNB** in balance!

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FcL6r1KVJmw4jLFWVpQbl%2Fblobs%2FfXcQBKxD21NGbe3TB5Qw%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=25e7d393&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/swap/multi-address-buy-v2-v3#id-5.-start-swap)

5\. Start Swap

*   Click the “Start Swap” button.
    
*   After execution, you can monitor each wallet’s buy-in status in real-time.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FcL6r1KVJmw4jLFWVpQbl%2Fblobs%2Fnx1iCWZJAEUlKnXP6jkN%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=41eb027c&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/swap/multi-address-buy-v2-v3#frequently-asked-questions-faq)

❓ Frequently Asked Questions (FAQ)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/swap/multi-address-buy-v2-v3#id-1.-what-is-multi-address-bundled-buy-in)

1\. What is multi-address bundled buy-in?

*   check
    
    **Answer**：It means multiple wallets perform a purchase of the same token simultaneously, via batch transaction execution, improving success rate and speed.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/swap/multi-address-buy-v2-v3#id-2.-how-many-wallets-can-be-supported-in-one-operation)

2\. How many wallets can be supported in one operation?

*   check
    
    **Answer**：You can import up to **20** wallet addresses for synchronous buy-in in a single operation.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/swap/multi-address-buy-v2-v3#id-3.-why-must-the-buying-addresss-bnb-balance-be-more-than-0.0008)

**3\.** Why must the buying address’s BNB balance be more than 0.0008?

*   check
    
    **Answer**：Because each wallet needs at least 0.0008 BNB to ensure sufficient gas fees for transactions.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/swap/multi-address-buy-v2-v3#id-4.-what-if-the-token-address-input-is-incorrect)

4\. What if the token address input is incorrect?

*   check
    
    **Answer**：Please confirm that the token contract address is correct **before** executing.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/swap/multi-address-buy-v2-v3#id-5.-is-custom-buy-in-amount-supported)

5\. Is custom buy-in amount supported?

*   check
    
    **Answer**：Yes. You can set a separate buy-in amount for each wallet, or you can uniformly set the same amount for all.

# Create/Add Liquidity v2 Tutorial | 「EVM」Tutorial | CiaoTool

circle-check

**Create Liquidity v2：**[https://bsc.ciaotool.io/swap/v2/create-liquidity-v2arrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/swap/v2/create-liquidity-v2)

circle-check

**Add Liquidity v2：**[https://bsc.ciaotool.io/swap/v2/add-liquidity-v2arrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/swap/v2/add-liquidity-v2)

circle-exclamation

If you prefer learning through videos, feel free to watch this tutorial.

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/swap/create-add-liquidity-v2#create-add-liquidity-detailed-guide)

🛠️ **Create / Add Liquidity – Detailed Guide**

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/swap/create-add-liquidity-v2#id-1.-connect-wallet)

1\. **Connect Wallet**

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FcL6r1KVJmw4jLFWVpQbl%2Fblobs%2F3Dy7JjQ4D457mBbqu42Y%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7adb871b&sv=2)

*   Enter the private key used to create or add liquidity.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FcL6r1KVJmw4jLFWVpQbl%2Fblobs%2Fuop9eBfw4iw9169lSLrz%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4cac70c&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/swap/create-add-liquidity-v2#id-2.-select-the-two-tokens-for-the-pool)

2\. Select the Two Tokens for the Pool

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FcL6r1KVJmw4jLFWVpQbl%2Fblobs%2FDq22nR8zTxMz4CTI5htG%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b49849f&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/swap/create-add-liquidity-v2#id-3.-enter-liquidity-amounts)

**3\. Enter Liquidity Amounts**

*   Input the amounts for both tokens.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FcL6r1KVJmw4jLFWVpQbl%2Fblobs%2FTcb1RElgrQq3FSNmXs8O%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7540d326&sv=2)

circle-exclamation

**Note:** Please calculate an appropriate ratio before creating liquidity.

*   When **adding liquidity**: existing pool details will be shown and the price is fixed — you only need to enter the amount of **Token A**.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FcL6r1KVJmw4jLFWVpQbl%2Fblobs%2FcY6RjEkVK33q7V9yO9N8%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d861cc22&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/swap/create-add-liquidity-v2#id-4.-approve-tokens)

4\. Approve Tokens

*   For the first operation, you need to approve the contract to use your tokens.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/swap/create-add-liquidity-v2#id-5.-create-add-liquidity)

5\. Create/Add Liquidity

After verifying all details, click the **“Start Swap”** button.

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/swap/create-add-liquidity-v2#frequently-asked-questions-faq)

❓ Frequently Asked Questions (FAQ)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/swap/create-add-liquidity-v2#id-1.-why-does-adding-liquidity-fail)

1\. Why does adding liquidity fail?

*   check
    
    **Answer**：Make sure your wallet has enough **BNB / WBNB**.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/swap/create-add-liquidity-v2#id-2.-if-i-create-a-wbnb-pair-can-users-buy-the-token-with-usdt)

2\. If I create a WBNB pair, can users buy the token with USDT?

*   check
    
    **Answer**：Yes. Even if the pool is WBNB-based, users can still trade via
    
*   check
    
    **USDT → BNB → Your Token**. On-chain routing is automatic and the result is the same.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/swap/create-add-liquidity-v2#id-3.-is-there-a-minimum-token-amount-required-for-adding-liquidity)

**3\.** Is there a minimum token amount required for adding liquidity?

*   check
    
    **Answer**：No strict requirement. You can decide flexibly based on your tokenomics, desired initial price, and market cap target.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/swap/create-add-liquidity-v2#id-4.-will-the-estimated-price-change-later)

4\. Will the estimated price change later?

*   check
    
    **Answer**：Yes. The estimated price is the **initial launch price**. As users continue trading, the price updates in real time — more trades mean more realistic price movement.

# RobotPump创建并买入-IOTX教程 | 「EVM」使用教程 | CiaoTool

circle-check

**RobotPump创建并买入**：[https://iotex.ciaotool.io/robotpump/iotex/create-and-buyarrow-up-right](https://iotex.ciaotool.io/robotpump/iotex/create-and-buy)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/robotpump/bundler#ru-he-zai-robotpump-chuang-jian-bing-mai-ru)

🧩如何在RobotPump创建并买入？

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/robotpump/bundler#id-1.-lian-jie-qian-bao)

**1.连接钱包**

*   点击右上角【连接钱包】，选择钱包地址并确认授权。
    
*   页面右上角显示钱包地址即表示绑定成功。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2086467048-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%252Fuploads%252FesbfU8eFw9sZbDQR0qCQ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Dc6e24947-5235-44f9-aa40-6222425de074&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=bdc01360&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/robotpump/bundler#di-er-bu-tian-jia-she-jiao-lian-jie-ke-xuan-dan-qiang-lie-jian-yi-tian-xie)

2.**填写代币基础信息**

*   **私钥：**输入用于发币的控制地址私钥。注意安全，建议使用测试钱包或专用地址
    
*   **钱包地址 & 余额：**系统自动解析私钥生成钱包地址，并显示当前 IOTX 余额
    
*   **Dev买入：**设置Dev买入数值
    
*   **代币名称：**Token 的完整名称（如：CiaoTool ）
    
*   **代币简称：**Token 符号（如：CIAO）
    
*   **描述：**简要介绍代币用途、故事或 Meme 背景（选填）
    
*   **上传图片：**上传 Token 图标，建议 1000×1000 像素，支持 jpg/png/webp/gif
    
*   **添加社交链接**：虽为可选项但强烈建议填写，**官网、X / Twitter、Telegram**
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2086467048-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%252Fuploads%252FFiW7wJaroq0dmaYYJZi1%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Db3436b35-6bee-4200-bd2b-f5931ca1e89d&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4c2fe4ca&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/robotpump/bundler#di-san-bu-pei-zhi-nei-pan-mai-ru-can-shu)

3\. 配置内盘买入参数

*   内盘买入意味着：**你提前布局，控制初期价格走势**，在图表上线前通过脚本抢先买入。
    
*   **点击导入私钥**，批量添加最多 20 个钱包地址
    
*   设置 买入金额
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2086467048-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%252Fuploads%252FznwUxqiKM6o4fQ2tL5V1%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D76d10fca-2c30-42f5-b066-264bdf007f0b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d0a4a40&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/robotpump/bundler#di-si-bu-pei-zhi-wai-pan-mai-ru-can-shu)

4\. 配置外盘买入参数

*   这是此功能的核心亮点，允许你批量导入多个地址（最多5个地址），在代币创建的瞬间 **「自动完成买入」**，实现抢跑保护 + 初始建仓。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2086467048-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%252Fuploads%252FklkJ2E8AVWcluIVvexKx%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D70f9076c-3678-41ed-9a65-680175c2d59b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1fcd2403&sv=2)

**配置方式：**

1.  点击“导入私钥”，支持批量粘贴多个私钥
    
2.  系统自动读取每个私钥的 IOTX 余额
    
3.  为每个地址设置「买入金额」 ，单个地址无上限买入金额，刷新余额查看即可
    
4.  可选择刷新余额或调整买入比例
    
5.  系统将展示每个地址的状态 + 操作按钮
    

circle-info

买入地址的IOTX余额必须大于 1！

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/robotpump/bundler#di-wu-bu-dian-ji-yi-jian-chuang-jian-bing-mai-ru)

5\. 点击“创建并买入”

*   完成所有信息后，点击页面底部按钮
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/robotpump/bundler#chang-jian-wen-ti-faq)

❓ 常见问题 FAQ

**1\. IoTeX 创建代币后多久可以交易？**

*   答：创建后代币会立即上线，完成买入后即可在链上自由流通。
    

**2\. 买入代币的钱包可以设置多个吗？**

*   答：可以，可添加多个钱包进行同步买入，适用于控盘或分发策略。
    

**3\. 如何查看创建成功的代币？**

*   答：您可在交易成功后跳转查看代币合约地址，或在 IoTeX 区块浏览器查询。
    

**4\. 创建失败会扣 Gas 吗？**

*   答：若交易未成功，链上仍可能产生一定的 Gas 消耗，请确保钱包余额充足
    

​

**💬 如遇到问题？加入社群实时咨询**：[https://t.me/ciaotoolarrow-up-right](https://t.me/ciaotool)

*   **Email**：[support@ciaotool.ioenvelope](mailto:support@ciaotool.io)
    
*   **官网**：[https://ciaotool.ioarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/)
    
*   **X（Twitter）**：[https://x.com/CiaoToolarrow-up-right](https://x.com/CiaoTool)
    
*   **Medium**： [https://medium.com/@ciaotoolarrow-up-right](https://medium.com/@ciaotool)
    
*   **Blog**：[https://www.ciaoailiquidity.com/zh/blogarrow-up-right](https://www.ciaoailiquidity.com/zh/blog)
    
*   **YouTube**：[https://www.youtube.com/@CiaoToolarrow-up-right](https://www.youtube.com/@CiaoTool)
    
*   **WhatsApp**：[https://whatsapp.com/channel/0029VbAuLrVAojYxRNw95W1Jarrow-up-right](https://whatsapp.com/channel/0029VbAuLrVAojYxRNw95W1J)

# 多地址捆绑卖出-BNB/USD1/USDT 教程 | 「EVM」使用教程 | CiaoTool

circle-check

**Flap多地址捆绑卖出-BNB:** [https://bsc.ciaotool.io/flap/bnb/multi-address-sellarrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/flap/bnb/multi-address-sell)

circle-check

**Flap多地址捆绑卖出-USD1:** [https://bsc.ciaotool.io/flap/usd1/multi-address-sellarrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/flap/usd1/multi-address-sell)

circle-check

**Flap多地址捆绑卖出-USDT:** [https://bsc.ciaotool.io/flap/usdt/multi-address-sellarrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/flap/usdt/multi-address-sell)

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/flap/multi-address-sell#flap-duo-di-zhi-kun-bang-mai-chu-jiao-cheng)

🪜 Flap 多地址捆绑卖出教程


----------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/flap/multi-address-sell#di-yi-bu-dao-ru-si-yao)

🧩 第一步：导入私钥

*   手动粘贴私钥，粘贴完成后会显示当前钱包的余额，可刷新余额。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2F6V9nhvX1IejVTKNhhv3d%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6a7f6cf2&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/flap/multi-address-sell#di-er-bu-dao-ru-dai-bi-he-yue-di-zhi)

🌐 第二步：导入代币合约地址

*   在代币输入框中 **粘贴目标代币的合约地址**。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FsFsc7Pp1ZfvAtvcTcmEZ%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5fd6f5c4&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/flap/multi-address-sell#di-san-bu-dao-ru-mai-chu-qian-bao-si-yao)

🏷 第三步：导入卖出钱包私钥

*   选择批量导入方式，可以 **手动粘贴多个私钥**，也可以 **上传包含私钥的表格文件（xls、xlsx格式）**。
    
*   系统将自动识别每个钱包的 USD1 余额与授权状态。
    

circle-info

注意：单次最多支持导入 **20 个钱包地址**。

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/flap/multi-address-sell#di-si-bu-she-zhi-mai-chu-can-shu)

💰 第四步：设置卖出参数

**配置方式：**

1.  为每个地址设置「卖出金额」 ，单个地址无上限卖出金额，刷新余额查看即可
    
2.  可选择刷新余额
    
3.  系统将展示每个地址的状态 + 操作按钮
    

triangle-exclamation

💡 注意：卖出地址的USD1 余额必须大于 0.0008！

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FBNOv1yV8206r8rI8pqvh%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f5cd238f&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/flap/multi-address-sell#di-wu-bu-zhi-xing-mai-chu-cao-zuo)

🛠 第五步：执行卖出操作

*   点击 **“执行（代币卖出）”** 按钮。
    
*   系统会自动为每个钱包生成交易并执行捆绑卖出操作。
    
*   执行完成后，可实时查看各钱包的卖出状态
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2Fa4AbPzlrGYNhEhe3VOXX%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6ebc8f5a&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/flap/multi-address-sell#chang-jian-wen-ti-faq)

❓ 常见问题 FAQ

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/flap/multi-address-sell#id-1.-shen-me-shi-duo-di-zhi-kun-bang-mai-chu)

1\. 什么是多地址捆绑卖出？

*   check
    
    答：指多个钱包同时卖出同一代币，以批量执行交易，提高交易成功率与速度。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/flap/multi-address-sell#id-2.-yi-ci-zui-duo-zhi-chi-ji-ge-qian-bao)

2\. 一次最多支持几个钱包？

*   check
    
    答：单次操作最多可导入 **20 个钱包地址** 进行同步卖出。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/flap/multi-address-sell#id-3.-wei-shen-me-mai-chu-di-zhi-de-yuebi-xu-da-yu-0.0008)

**3\.** 为什么卖出地址的余额必须大于 0.0008？

*   check
    
    答：每个钱包至少保留 0.0008 USD1 以上余额，以确保足够支付交易 Gas 费用。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/flap/multi-address-sell#id-4.-dai-bi-di-zhi-shu-ru-cuo-wu-zen-me-ban)

4\. 代币地址输入错误怎么办？

*   check
    
    答：请在执行前确认代币合约地址正确无误。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/flap/multi-address-sell#id-5.-shi-fou-zhi-chi-zi-ding-yi-mai-chu-jine)

5\. 是否支持自定义卖出金额？

*   check
    
    答：支持。你可以为不同钱包单独设定卖出金额，也可以统一设定同样的卖出数额。
    

**💬 如遇到问题？加入社群实时咨询**：[https://t.me/ciaotoolarrow-up-right](https://t.me/ciaotool)

# Fourmeme 批量交易教程 | 「EVM」使用教程 | CiaoTool

circle-check

**Fourmeme 批量交易：**[https://bsc.ciaotool.io/fourmeme/batch-swap-fourmemearrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/fourmeme/batch-swap-fourmeme)

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/fourmeme/batch-swap-fourmeme#ru-he-shi-yong-fourmeme-pi-liang-jiao-yi-gong-ju)

✅ 如何使用Fourmeme 批量交易工具：


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/fourmeme/batch-swap-fourmeme#id-1.-dao-ru-si-yao)

1\. 导入私钥

*   导入钱包私钥，查看钱包余额
    

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/fourmeme/batch-swap-fourmeme#id-2.-she-zhi-dai-bi)

2\. 设置代币

*   在输入框中填写目标代币地址，或点击下拉菜单选择当前钱包持有的代币。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FeCTD2O8PWFE8g1saAeqr%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4c147172&sv=2)

*   快速切换交易买卖方向**（From**：支出的代币、**To**：获得的代币）
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FPRU1eLLTNlq3b5Yp1TQr%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=5403c1d7&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/fourmeme/batch-swap-fourmeme#id-3.-dao-ru-pi-liang-jiao-yi-qian-bao)

3\. 导入批量交易钱包

*   可上传私钥文件导入或手动输入
    

circle-info

每个交易的钱包中，需要有一些（0.0008） BNB 用于支付交易 GAS

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2F3PJQKa9R6pzKcUTqEiHD%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=1e954b9b&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/fourmeme/batch-swap-fourmeme#id-4.-kai-shi-pi-liang-jiao-yi)

4\. 开始批量交易

*   **代币授权：**如果支出的代币非 BNB，需要先进行代币授权，以便更快速完成批量交易
    
*   交易速度会受到链上拥堵情况影响，链上拥堵时可能交易速度较慢，还请您耐心等待。
    

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/fourmeme/batch-swap-fourmeme#chang-jian-wen-ti-faq)

❓常见问题 FAQ

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/fourmeme/batch-swap-fourmeme#id-1.-ke-yi-tong-shi-zhi-xing-mai-ru-he-mai-chu-ma)

**1\.** 可以同时执行买入和卖出吗？

*   check
    
    答：不建议同一批次同时操作买入和卖出，容易冲突, 建议分批执行，先完成买入，再执行卖出。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/fourmeme/batch-swap-fourmeme#id-2.-zhi-chi-na-xie-lei-xing-de-qian-bao)

**2\. 支持哪些类型的钱包？**

*   check
    
    答：支持导入私钥的钱包，也支持使用当前连接的钱包进行操作，可手动粘贴或上传 xls、xlsx格式文件。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/fourmeme/batch-swap-fourmeme#id-3.-jiao-yi-shi-bai-zen-me-ban)

**3\.** 交易失败怎么办？

*   check
    
    答：常见原因：钱包余额不足 / RPC 节点拥堵, 解决办法：检查余额、切换节点或重试。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/fourmeme/batch-swap-fourmeme#id-4.-zui-duo-neng-dao-ru-duo-shao-ge-qian-bao)

**4\.** 最多能导入多少个钱包？

*   check
    
    答：系统支持一次最多 **20 个钱包** 批量导入。

# Create Wallet - Universal Tutorial | 「EVM」Tutorial | CiaoTool

circle-check

**BSC Wallet Creator:** [https://bsc.ciaotool.io/wallet/wallet-createarrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/wallet/wallet-create)

**Base Wallet Creator:** [https://base.ciaotool.io/wallet/wallet-createarrow-up-right](https://base.ciaotool.io/wallet/wallet-create)

**X Layer Wallet Creator:** [https://xlayer.ciaotool.io/wallet/wallet-createarrow-up-right](https://xlayer.ciaotool.io/wallet/wallet-create)

**IoTeX Wallet Creator:** [https://iotex.ciaotool.io/wallet/wallet-createarrow-up-right](https://iotex.ciaotool.io/wallet/wallet-create)

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/wallet/wallet-create#operation-steps)

🔗 Operation Steps


-------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/wallet/wallet-create#id-1.-enter-the-number-of-wallets-to-create)

1\. Enter the Number of Wallets to Create

*   Input the desired number of wallets to generate and click "Create" to initiate the process.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/wallet/wallet-create#id-2.-download-the-generated-wallets)

2\. Download the Generated Wallets

*   After generation is complete, download the xls, xlsx file containing the wallet information to your local storage for safekeeping.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FcL6r1KVJmw4jLFWVpQbl%2Fblobs%2FuRJsgKeS9bXjesjDoGAW%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=65cf54c2&sv=2)

circle-exclamation

The wallet generation process is entirely performed locally on your computer, ensuring that your mnemonic phrases and private keys remain under your control.

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FcL6r1KVJmw4jLFWVpQbl%2Fblobs%2FziTF2LvUm7D1xAby27SN%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b280866e&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/wallet/wallet-create#faq)

❓FAQ

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/wallet/wallet-create#id-1.-what-is-the-maximum-number-of-wallet-addresses-i-can-create-at-once)

1\. What is the maximum number of wallet addresses I can create at once?

*   check
    
    **Answer**： CiaoTool supports generating up to 10,000 wallet addresses at a time. You can customize the quantity as needed.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/wallet/wallet-create#id-2.-do-the-created-wallets-come-with-private-keys-how-can-i-export-them)

2\. Do the created wallets come with private keys? How can I export them?

*   check
    
    **Answer**： Yes. Each wallet will have a corresponding private key automatically generated. After the operation is complete, you can export them as xls files for backup or subsequent operations.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/wallet/wallet-create#id-3.-are-these-wallets-secure-will-my-private-keys-be-uploaded)

3\. Are these wallets secure? Will my private keys be uploaded?

*   check
    
    **Answer**： Yes. All wallet generation and private key handling are performed locally in your browser. The platform does not upload, save, or access any of your private key information.

# Batch Swap Tutorial | 「EVM」Tutorial | CiaoTool

circle-check

**FourMeme Batch Swap：**[https://bsc.ciaotool.io/fourmeme/batch-swap-fourmemearrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/fourmeme/batch-swap-fourmeme)

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/fourmeme/batch-swap#how-to-use-the-fourmeme-batch-swap-tool)

✅ How to Use the FourMeme Batch Swap Tool?


------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/fourmeme/batch-swap#id-1.-import-private-keys)

1\. Import Private Keys

*   Import your wallet private keys and check the wallet balances.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/fourmeme/batch-swap#id-2.-select-token)

2\. Select Token

*   Enter the target token address in the input box or select from the dropdown menu of tokens held by the current wallet.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FcL6r1KVJmw4jLFWVpQbl%2Fblobs%2FlxlyS2VikoA7u0rw6jSv%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a8da7505&sv=2)

*   Quickly switch between trade directions (From: token to spend, To: token to receive).
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FcL6r1KVJmw4jLFWVpQbl%2Fblobs%2FGnKiXsXEQ8FanlcvsW8c%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=2a6b4ebe&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/fourmeme/batch-swap#id-3.-import-wallets-for-batch-swap)

3\. Import Wallets for Batch Swap

*   You can upload a private key file or enter manually.
    

circle-info

Each wallet must hold a small amount of BNB (≈0.0008) to cover gas fees.

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FcL6r1KVJmw4jLFWVpQbl%2Fblobs%2FPm5Hb6mxmdR7oVOUdZOu%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=90aff84d&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/fourmeme/batch-swap#id-4.-start-batch-trading)

4\. Start Batch Trading

*   **Token Approval:** If the token spent is not BNB, you need to approve it first to enable faster batch trading.
    
*   **Trading Speed:** May be affected by network congestion; transactions could be slower during high congestion, so please be patient.
    

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/fourmeme/batch-swap#frequently-asked-questions-faq)

❓Frequently Asked Questions (FAQ)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/fourmeme/batch-swap#id-1.-can-i-execute-buy-and-sell-simultaneously)

**1\.** Can I execute buy and sell simultaneously?

*   check
    
    **Answer**：Not recommended to buy and sell in the same batch, as it may cause conflicts. It’s better to execute in separate batches: complete buys first, then sells.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/fourmeme/batch-swap#id-2.-what-types-of-wallets-are-supported)

**2\.** What types of wallets are supported?

*   check
    
    **Answer**：Wallets imported via private key are supported, as well as currently connected wallets. You can manually paste keys or upload a CSV file.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/fourmeme/batch-swap#id-3.-what-if-a-trade-fails)

**3\.** What if a trade fails?

*   check
    
    **Answer**：Common reasons: insufficient wallet balance or RPC node congestion. Solutions: check balances, switch nodes, or retry.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/fourmeme/batch-swap#id-4.-whats-the-maximum-number-of-wallets-that-can-be-imported-at-once)

**4\.** What’s the maximum number of wallets that can be imported at once?

*   check
    
    **Answer**：The system supports importing up to 20 wallets per batch.
    

💬 **Need help? Join our community for real-time support:** [https://t.me/ciaotoolarrow-up-right](https://t.me/ciaotool)

*   **Email:** [support@ciaotool.ioenvelope](mailto:support@ciaotool.io)
    
*   **Website:** [https://ciaotool.ioarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/)
