# Solana 放弃权限教程 | 「Solana」使用教程 | CiaoTool

circle-check

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/management/control#solana-fang-qi-quan-xian-httpsciaotool.iozhcntokenrevokepermission)

Solana 放弃权限：[https://ciaotool.io/zh-CN/token/revoke-permissionarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/zh-CN/token/revoke-permission)



--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/management/control#ru-he-fang-qi-dai-bi-quan-xian)

🔓 **如何放弃代币权限？**

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/management/control#id-1.-lian-jie-qian-bao)

1\. 连接**钱包**

*   点击右上角**【连接钱包】**，选择钱包地址并确认授权。
    
*   页面右上角显示钱包地址即表示绑定成功。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252FGWS7w38oRODTISMnkc4G%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D19521323-9a25-4670-8da6-45ba05165887&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f4cd3caf&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/management/control#id-2.-xuan-ze-dai-bi)

2\. 选择代币

*   粘贴代币地址或下拉选择钱包内的代币。
    
*   若有未放弃的权限，您即可打开放弃开关，后点击下方操作按钮即可
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F1318999599-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FSbOZgk4BvxH3NoNkiFR8%252Fuploads%252FM1D54EqPeeIURBcTJcGZ%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D995b86f6-dbf4-450e-a216-efb37d8cc3c5&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=4031a75b&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/management/control#jiao-yi-liu-cheng)

🔁 **交易流程**

*   任务开始执行时，会出现日志弹框为您实时更新交易进度。（需要一次交易签名）。
    
*   任何环节出了问题，我们都会为你清晰透出。操作失败不会收取任何费用。
    

![](https://docs.dogtools.meme/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F4028514454-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252Ft1j9LpucEChNmzQ1XqQO%252Fuploads%252FXeeLJe4zNeykTEOviIGz%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D70040d64-762e-40d0-a678-df4356c88659&width=768&dpr=4&quality=100&sign=b391782a&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/management/control#chang-jian-wen-ti)

❓ 常见问题

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/management/control#id-1.-fang-qi-dai-bi-quan-xian-hou-hai-neng-hui-fu-ma)

**1\. 放弃代币权限后还能恢复吗？**

*   check
    
    答：不能，一旦放弃权限，该操作永久生效，无法撤销。。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/management/control#id-2.-wei-shen-me-yao-fang-qi-dai-bi-quan-xian)

**2\. 为什么要放弃代币权限？**

*   check
    
    答：放弃权限可以提升项目透明度，增强社区信任，吸引更多投资者。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/management/control#id-3.-fang-qi-quan-xian-de-liu-cheng-fu-za-ma)

**3\. 放弃权限的流程复杂吗？**

*   check
    
    答：使用 CiaoTool，一键操作，简化流程，无需编写代码。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/management/control#id-4.-fang-qi-na-xie-quan-xian-zui-zhong-yao)

**4\. 放弃哪些权限最重要？**

*   check
    
    答：通常是 Mint（增发）和 Freeze（冻结）权限，确保代币供应和账户操作安全。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/sol/management/control#id-5.-fang-qi-quan-xian-shi-fou-hui-ying-xiang-dai-bi-jiao-yi)

**5\. 放弃权限是否会影响代币交易？**

*   check
    
    答：不会，代币正常交易和转账不会受到影响。

*   **Email**：[support@ciaotool.ioenvelope](mailto:support@ciaotool.io)

# One-to-Multi - Universal Tutorial | 「EVM」Tutorial | CiaoTool

circle-check

**BSC One-to-Multi:** [https://bsc.ciaotool.io/transfer/one-to-manyarrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/transfer/one-to-many)

**Base One-to-Multi:** [https://base.ciaotool.io/transfer/one-to-manyarrow-up-right](https://base.ciaotool.io/transfer/one-to-many)

**X Layer One-to-Multi:** [https://xlayer.ciaotool.io/transfer/one-to-manyarrow-up-right](https://xlayer.ciaotool.io/transfer/one-to-many)

**IoTex One-to-Multi:** [https://iotex.ciaotool.io/transfer/one-to-manyarrow-up-right](https://iotex.ciaotool.io/transfer/one-to-many)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/multisender/one-to-many#video-tutorial)

📹 Video Tutorial

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/multisender/one-to-many#one-to-multi-tutorial-one-to-many)

🧾 One-to-Multi Tutorial（One-to-Many）

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/multisender/one-to-many#id-1.-connect-wallet)

**1\.** Connect Wallet

*   Connect a wallet that supports the EVM chain.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F467813208-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcL6r1KVJmw4jLFWVpQbl%252Fuploads%252FmjUTeNxM5MU26qYhGzpE%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D51a65dcb-0421-46bf-badb-4eaa71645c66&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=13a84c8e&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/multisender/one-to-many#id-2.-select-wallet)

**2\.** Select Wallet

*   You can use the currently connected wallet or import another wallet's private key.
    

circle-info

*   **Self-Use Wallet**: Limited to 200 recipient addresses.
    
*   **Other Wallet**: Unlimited recipient addresses; add freely.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FcL6r1KVJmw4jLFWVpQbl%2Fblobs%2FUfJpmrXABgiPIi83FYpK%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=6c1514df&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/multisender/one-to-many#id-3.-choose-amount-mode)

**3\.** Choose Amount Mode

*   Supports **"same amount transfer"** or setting **"custom amounts"** for each address. Custom amounts can be enter in the following format:
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FcL6r1KVJmw4jLFWVpQbl%2Fblobs%2FnWJW8KYbT4CmJLHjrYhP%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=44807742&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/multisender/one-to-many#id-4.-enter-token-address)

**4\. Enter** Token Address

*   Select a token (e.g., BUSD, USDT) or manually enter the token contract address.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FcL6r1KVJmw4jLFWVpQbl%2Fblobs%2FTQ0aQgyN7Mo01WHS9obP%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=37832cb6&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/multisender/one-to-many#id-5.-add-recipient-addresses)

**5\.** Add Recipient Addresses**：**

You can manually paste or upload an address list file (xls、xlsx).

1.  Choose "same amount transfer," meaning you need to set the same transfer amount for each recipient.
    
2.  Enter the token amount for each recipient address or upload an address file with amounts.
    
3.  Click "Send," confirm, and sign to complete the batch transfer.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FcL6r1KVJmw4jLFWVpQbl%2Fblobs%2FqnFFfuvZNCSdFBo0Hhqi%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=aa10fe4a&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/multisender/one-to-many#frequently-asked-questions-faq)

❓Frequently Asked Questions (FAQ)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/multisender/one-to-many#id-1.-can-i-transfer-different-amounts-to-different-addresses)

1\. Can I transfer different amounts to different addresses?

*   check
    
    Yes. You can upload xls, xlsx file with custom amounts for each address to have precise control over each transfer.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/multisender/one-to-many#id-2.-is-the-operation-safe)

2\. Is the operation safe?

*   check
    
    Yes. Private keys are only used for local signing; the system does not store any wallet data.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/multisender/one-to-many#id-3.-what-should-i-do-if-the-transfer-fails)

3\. What should I do if the transfer fails?

*   check
    
    Please check if the addresses are valid, ensure sufficient balance, and appropriately increase the gas limit before retrying.

# 底池燃烧代币创建教程 - BSC | 「EVM」使用教程 | CiaoTool

circle-check

**底池燃烧代币**：[https://bsc.ciaotool.io/token/lp-burnarrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/token/lp-burn)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/token/lp-reflection-1#shen-me-shi-di-chi-ran-shao-dai-bi)

🛠 什么是底池燃烧代币？

*   项目方加池后，底池内的代币（自发行币）会按固定周期燃烧/销毁。当代币数量减少而 USDT 或 BNB 不变时，价格会被动上涨。
    
*   燃烧周期：可设置每 1 小时或每 24 小时一次
    
*   燃烧率：每周期最小 0.01%，最大 1%
    
*   燃烧条件：每周期必须有非白名单卖单才会触发
    
*   燃烧停止：当底池剩余 100 个代币时自动停止
    

**检测风险：**

*   该类型代币可能存在安全检测风险。如果你在意检测结果，可以选择创建标准代币，标准币没有风险。 创建燃烧代币即表示你接受可能的检测风险。
    

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/token/lp-reflection-1#ru-he-chuang-jian-di-chi-ran-shao-dai-bi)

🎯 **如何创建**底池燃烧代币**？**

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/token/lp-reflection-1#yi-lian-jie-qian-bao)

一、连接钱包

1.  **打开发币页面**：[https://bsc.ciaotool.io/token/lp-burnarrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/token/lp-burn)
    
2.  点击右上角**【连接钱包】**，在弹窗中确认钱包地址
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2Fqi5y1ACYR5j7KFkJrdrN%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=cd88c116&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/token/lp-reflection-1#er-shu-ru-dai-bi-ji-chu-xin-xi)

二、输入代币基础**信息**

*   **代币全称**：如 CiaoTool，支持中文、英文及中英混合
    
*   **代币符号**：如 C，在钱包和交易所显示
    
*   **发行总量**：固定总供应量，创建后不可增发
    
*   **精度**：代币最小单位，如 0.000001 精度为 6，默认一般为 18
    
*   **收币地址**：代币创建完成后接收代币的钱包地址 (可设置当前钱包地址，默认白名单）
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FdiLXkCcET6B8o7RHQfcb%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7e9902a9&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/token/lp-reflection-1#san-ran-shao-she-zhi)

三、燃烧设置

*   **燃烧周期(小时)**：多久燃烧一次，最大 48 小时
    
*   **燃烧百分比**：每周期燃烧代币比例，0.01%~1%
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2F6T4c0FFvn1Omv4Dcpw7F%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f34c6f19&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/token/lp-reflection-1#si-mai-ru-shuil0x25)

四、买入税率**（0**≤x<**25%）**

*   **营销税率**：买入扣除后，合约触发阈值自动卖出换成分红币发到营销钱包
    
*   **销毁税率**：发送到黑洞地址销毁
    
*   **回流税率**：交易中指定额度的代币将会自动添加到流动池内,保证交易始终存在流动性
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2Firgpws61NewiKBSC4q24%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=70a181a8&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/token/lp-reflection-1#wu-mai-chu-shuil0x25)

五、卖出税率**（0**≤x<**25%）**

*   包括营销、销毁、回流，与买入税率逻辑相同，只在卖出交易时生效
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2086467048-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%252Fuploads%252Fo4jjU6gL7tS35zB8G3WI%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D96a672f7-3627-4cad-8405-841dc5fec8d5&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b391fa8e&sv=2)

circle-exclamation

买入和卖出税率不能超过25%,交易总税率不能超过50%

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/token/lp-reflection-1#liu-qi-ta-can-shu)

六、其他参数

*   **营销钱包**：接收营销税率对应的本币（可设置当前钱包）
    
*   **选择交易所**：PancakeSwap
    
*   **选择底池代币**：WBNB / USDT 等，后续添加流动性需使用同样代币
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2F7xVKqoqzbEFMs0UsVgCc%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=18bbe33b&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/token/lp-reflection-1#qi-xiang-guan-gong-neng-kai-guan-can-shu)

七、相关功能开关参数

**1\. 手动开启交易**

*   check
    
    打开：添加池子后的首次交易需要在控制台手动开启
    
*   关闭：则添加流动性后立即可以进行交易
    

**2\. 杀区块**

*   check
    
    打开：将对开启交易后在n个区块内交易的地址全部拉入黑名单,用于防止机器人抢跑买入,必须手动开启交易
    
*   关闭：无法使用
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FYxnFgCRixHOi9BDQ9JM6%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7a433a7a&sv=2)

**3\. 税率开关**

*   check
    
    打开：创建后可手动调整买卖税率，但是买卖税率都需要为0≤25%
    
*   关闭：无法修改滑点，后期也不能再次开启
    

**4\. 自动空投**

*   check
    
    打开：每笔交易向随机地址空投少量代币（最多 5 个地址）
    
*   关闭：无法使用
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FugcQGacqNVtSebUHKsl8%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d2e93327&sv=2)

circle-exclamation

注：开启后无法再关闭

**5\. 黑名单功能**

*   check
    
    打开：可添加/解除黑名单，被拉黑地址无法转账或卖币
    
*   关闭：无法使用
    

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/token/lp-reflection-1#chang-jian-wen-ti-faq)

❓常见问题 FAQ

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/token/lp-reflection-1#id-1.-wei-shen-me-dai-bi-mei-you-ran-shao)

**1\.** 为什么代币没有燃烧？

*   check
    
    可能没到燃烧时间，也可能没有非白名单卖单。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/token/lp-reflection-1#id-2.-quan-xian-diu-qi-hou-hai-neng-xiu-gai-gong-neng-ma)

**2\.** 权限丢弃后还能修改功能吗？

*   check
    
    权限丢弃后，所有功能（燃烧、税率、交易控制等）无法修改，请谨慎操作。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/token/lp-reflection-1#id-3.-v2-yu-v3-liu-dong-xing-chi-you-shen-me-qu-bie)

**3\.** V2 与 V3 流动性池有什么区别？

*   check
    
    首次加池必须使用 V2，V3 不支持燃烧或其他机制，请注意。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/token/lp-reflection-1#id-4.-ran-shao-zhou-qi-nei-mei-you-mai-dan-zen-me-ban)

**4\.** 燃烧周期内没有卖单怎么办？

*   check
    
    如果一个燃烧周期内没有非白名单卖单，该周期燃烧将不会执行，需等待下一个有卖单的周期。
    

**💬 如遇到问题？加入社群实时咨询**：[https://t.me/ciaotoolarrow-up-right](https://t.me/ciaotool)

*   **Email**：[support@ciaotool.ioenvelope](mailto:support@ciaotool.io)
    
*   **官网**：[https://ciaotool.ioarrow-up-right](https://ciaotool.io/)
    
*   **X（Twitter）**：[https://x.com/CiaoToolarrow-up-right](https://x.com/CiaoTool)

# 创建并买入-BNB/USD1 教程 | 「EVM」使用教程 | CiaoTool

circle-check

**FourMeme创建并买入-BNB：**[https://bsc.ciaotool.io/fourmeme/bnb/create-and-buyarrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/fourmeme/bnb/create-and-buy)

circle-check

**FourMeme创建并买入-USD1:** [https://bsc.ciaotool.io/fourmeme/usd1/create-and-buyarrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/fourmeme/usd1/create-and-buy)

circle-exclamation

如果你更偏好视频形式的学习，欢迎观看本教程

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/fourmeme/create-and-buy#ru-he-jin-xing-chuang-jian-bing-mai-ru)

🧩 如何进行创建并买入？

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/fourmeme/create-and-buy#id-1.-lian-jie-qian-bao)

1.连接钱包

*   点击右上角【连接钱包】，选择钱包地址并确认授权。
    
*   页面右上角显示钱包地址即表示绑定成功。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2086467048-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%252Fuploads%252FLjor1kUby957a62JVWmp%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D7485a544-375c-4173-ab51-d135c084c412&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=cc603e81&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/fourmeme/create-and-buy#id-2.-tian-xie-dai-bi-ji-chu-xin-xi)

2\. **填写代币基础信息**

*   **私钥：**输入用于发币的控制地址私钥。注意安全，建议使用测试钱包或专用地址
    
*   **钱包地址 & 余额：**系统自动解析私钥生成钱包地址，并显示当前 BNB 余额
    
*   **代币名称：**Token 的完整名称（如：CiaoTool ）
    
*   **代币简称：**Token 符号（如：CIAO）
    
*   **描述：**简要介绍代币用途、故事或 Meme 背景（选填）
    
*   **上传图片：**上传 Token 图标，建议 1000×1000 像素，支持 jpg/png/webp/gif
    
*   **添加社交链接**：虽为可选项但强烈建议填写，**官网、X / Twitter、Telegram**
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2086467048-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%252Fuploads%252FluNFnOvjbrrdhACnWyhw%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D4529d892-c962-44f0-8f82-0eff935f96c3&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b829a5ab&sv=2)

circle-exclamation

小贴士：一个完整的视觉资产（图标+命名）可以帮助你更快获得 Birdeye 图表站收录，提高用户点击率与传播潜力。即便是 Meme 项目，也建议预设一个 TG 群组 + 备用 Twitter 页面，有助于 CMC/CG 审核与用户获取信息。

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/fourmeme/create-and-buy#id-3.-xuan-ze-xiang-mu-biao-qian)

3\. 选择项目标签

*   从以下标签中选择适合你项目的定位，系统不支持多选：
    

`Meme / AI / DeFi / Game / Infra / DeSci / Social / DePin / Charity / Others`

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FclJ7Ao8XsWGVFDIYfxA3%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b07bdd5f&sv=2)

circle-info

**示例用法：**你发的是狗狗币类 Meme，可选「Meme」；如果未来要做 NFT 或 Game 叙事，也可同步选「Game」。

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/fourmeme/create-and-buy#id-4.-pei-zhi-mai-ru-can-shu)

4\. 配置买入参数

*   这是此功能的核心亮点，允许你批量导入多个地址（最多20个地址），在代币创建的瞬间 **「自动完成买入」**，实现抢跑保护 + 初始建仓。
    
*   **配置方式**：
    
    1.  点击 **“导入私钥”**，支持批量粘贴多个私钥
        
    2.  系统自动读取每个私钥的 **BNB 余额**
        
    3.  为每个地址设置 **买入金额**（单地址无上限），刷新余额即可查看
        
    4.  可选择 **刷新余额** 或 **调整买入比例**
        
    5.  系统显示每个地址的 **状态与操作按钮**
        
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2086467048-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%252Fuploads%252Ftfx6sxhOuUrZGeNaGbsC%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D76f38fde-2a86-4a60-ae33-09d44fc841dd&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8241e28&sv=2)

triangle-exclamation

买入地址的BNB余额必须大于 0.0008！

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/fourmeme/create-and-buy#id-5.-dian-ji-chuang-jian-bing-mai-ru)

5\. 点击“创建并买入”

*   完成所有信息后，点击页面底部按钮
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F2086467048-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%252Fuploads%252FFidgJIcW77v5JvKEUWwt%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D814a38e9-9a2d-4966-a751-b01b3661040b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=8450e34a&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/fourmeme/create-and-buy#chang-jian-wen-ti-faq)

❓ 常见问题 FAQ

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/fourmeme/create-and-buy#id-1.-bnb-zuo-wei-lp-shi-wo-xu-yao-zhun-bei-duo-shao-yue)

1\. **BNB 作为 LP 时，我需要准备多少余额？**

*   check
    
    答：建议每个用于买入的钱包预留 **0.01–0.05BNB**，以支持买入和 gas fee，主钱包建议准备 > 0.5BNB 以防部署失败。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/fourmeme/create-and-buy#id-2.-chuang-jian-cheng-gong-hou-shi-fou-zi-dong-chu-xian-zai-pancakeswap)

**2\. 创建成功后是否自动出现在 PancakeSwap？**

*   check
    
    答：在 BNB 模式下，FourMeme 会在代币创建后开始播种流程，并将 100% 的流动性注入PancakeSwap 并销毁 LP 代币。
    
*   check
    
    一旦联合曲线达到 100%（约 18.18 BNB），代币即可直接在 PancakeSwap 搜索或通过合约地址进行交易。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/fourmeme/create-and-buy#id-3.-bnb-mo-shi-shi-fou-rong-yi-bei-ju-ji)

3\. **BNB 模式是否容易被狙击？**

*   check
    
    答：由于价格更易波动，建议搭配冷分仓等控盘机制提升安全性。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/fourmeme/create-and-buy#id-4.-wo-ru-he-zhi-dao-zi-ji-shi-fou-qiang-dao-zui-zao-mai-ru)

4\. 我如何知道自己是否抢到“最早买入”？

*   check
    
    答：CiaoTool 在执行“创建并买入”时，将优先按顺序执行你的地址交易，保障你获得“图表前排”持仓。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/fourmeme/create-and-buy#id-5.-shi-fou-zhi-chi-duo-ge-qian-bao-pi-liang-mai-ru)

5\. 是否支持多个钱包批量买入？

*   check
    
    答：支持。你最多可以添加 20 个钱包进行统一配置，系统会自动循环处理。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/fourmeme/create-and-buy#id-6.-wei-shen-me-wo-she-zhi-le-mai-ru-jinedan-xian-shi-yuebu-zu)

6\. **为什么我设置了买入金额但显示余额不足？**

*   check
    
    答：请确保对应地址 BNB 余额充足，同时刷新余额按钮在操作前点击一次更新数据。
    

**💬 如遇到问题？加入社群实时咨询**：[https://t.me/ciaotoolarrow-up-right](https://t.me/ciaotool)

*   **Email**：[support@ciaotool.ioenvelope](mailto:support@ciaotool.io)

*   **YouTube**：[https://www.youtube.com/@CiaoToolarrow-up-right](https://www.youtube.com/@CiaoTool)
    
*   **WhatsApp**：[https://whatsapp.com/channel/0029VbAuLrVAojYxRNw95W1Jarrow-up-right](https://whatsapp.com/channel/0029VbAuLrVAojYxRNw95W1J)

# Multi-Address Bundled Buy BNB/USD1/USDT Tutorial | 「EVM」Tutorial | CiaoTool

circle-check

**Multi-Address Bundled Buy (BNB)：**[https://bsc.ciaotool.io/flap/bnb/multi-address-buyarrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/flap/bnb/multi-address-buy)

circle-check

**Multi-Address Bundled Buy(USD1):** [https://bsc.ciaotool.io/flap/usd1/multi-address-buyarrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/flap/usd1/multi-address-buy)

circle-check

**Multi-Address Bundled Buy(USDT):** [https://bsc.ciaotool.io/flap/usdt/multi-address-buyarrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/flap/usdt/multi-address-buy)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/flap/multi-address-buy#how-to-use-multi-address-bundled-buy-bnb-usd1-usdt)

🧩 How to Use Multi-Address Bundled Buy BNB/USD1/USDT?

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/flap/multi-address-buy#id-1.-import-private-keys)

1\. Import Private Keys

*   Manually paste private keys; after pasting you’ll see the current wallet balances — you can refresh to update balances.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F467813208-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcL6r1KVJmw4jLFWVpQbl%252Fuploads%252FIs8KUggyMpFHWuKqEr3p%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D79d37c16-bd9f-4c64-9231-5d81d3fb489b&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=b9f94574&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/flap/multi-address-buy#id-2.-import-token-contract-address)

2\. Import Token Contract Address

*   In the token input field, paste the contract address of the target token.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F467813208-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcL6r1KVJmw4jLFWVpQbl%252Fuploads%252FjGnbpfNu6d8FYLnhVaxl%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df4cbf2a2-6842-47ad-b526-82780b32c884&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=58ef5475&sv=2)

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FcL6r1KVJmw4jLFWVpQbl%2Fblobs%2FhXCejhaGMV0qSyydNU8Z%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=cb218eff&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/flap/multi-address-buy#id-3.-import-buying-wallet-private-keys)

3\. Import Buying Wallet Private Keys

*   Choose the batch import option — you can either manually paste multiple private keys or upload a file (CSV/TXT) containing the private keys.
    
*   The system will automatically check each wallet’s BNB balance and approval status.
    
*   Note: Up to 20 wallet addresses can be imported in a single operation.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/flap/multi-address-buy#id-4.-set-buy-parameters)

4\. Set Buy Parameters

**Configuration options:**

1.  Set a “buy-in amount” for each address. There is no upper limit for a single address; just refresh the balance to check.
    
2.  You can choose to refresh balances or adjust the buy-in proportion.
    
3.  The system will display the status of each address plus action buttons.
    

triangle-exclamation

Note: Each buying address must have **more than 0.0008 BNB** in balance!

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F467813208-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcL6r1KVJmw4jLFWVpQbl%252Fuploads%252FZ3hOdu2K9DRkqr0rf4sB%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3Df86b91ed-6ae8-4e3b-9996-ac0bdf7af71f&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=9236db77&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/flap/multi-address-buy#id-5.-click-the-token-buy-button)

5\. Click the “T**oken Buy**” button.

*   The system will automatically generate transactions for each wallet and execute the bundled buy-in operations.
    
*   After execution, you can monitor each wallet’s buy-in status in real-time.
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2F467813208-files.gitbook.io%2F%7E%2Ffiles%2Fv0%2Fb%2Fgitbook-x-prod.appspot.com%2Fo%2Fspaces%252FcL6r1KVJmw4jLFWVpQbl%252Fuploads%252FtElPWajEsfKSNfrkZIWC%252Fimage.png%3Falt%3Dmedia%26token%3D54469c95-5470-47a2-b51c-bd314e043867&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=68a74f4d&sv=2)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/flap/multi-address-buy#frequently-asked-questions-faq)

❓ Frequently Asked Questions (FAQ)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/flap/multi-address-buy#id-1.-what-is-multi-address-bundled-buy)

1\. What is Multi-Address Bundled Buy?

*   check
    
    **Answer**：It means multiple wallets perform a purchase of the same token simultaneously, via batch transaction execution, improving success rate and speed.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/flap/multi-address-buy#id-2.-how-many-wallets-can-be-supported-in-one-operation)

2\. How many wallets can be supported in one operation?

*   check
    
    **Answer**：You can import up to **20** wallet addresses for synchronous buy-in in a single operation.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/flap/multi-address-buy#id-3.-why-must-the-buying-addresss-bnb-balance-be-more-than-0.0008)

**3\.** Why must the buying address’s BNB balance be more than 0.0008?

*   check
    
    **Answer**：Because each wallet needs at least 0.0008 BNB to ensure sufficient gas fees for transactions.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/flap/multi-address-buy#id-4.-what-if-the-token-address-input-is-incorrect)

4\. What if the token address input is incorrect?

*   check
    
    **Answer**：Please confirm that the token contract address is correct **before** executing.
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm-en/flap/multi-address-buy#id-5.-is-custom-buy-in-amount-supported)

5\. Is custom buy-in amount supported?

*   check
    
    **Answer**：Yes. You can set a separate buy-in amount for each wallet, or you can uniformly set the same amount for all.

# 创建流动性并捆绑买入「v3」教程 | 「EVM」使用教程 | CiaoTool

circle-check

**创建流动性并捆绑买入 v3：**[https://bsc.ciaotool.io/swap/v3/create-liquidity-and-buy-v3arrow-up-right](https://bsc.ciaotool.io/swap/v3/create-liquidity-and-buy-v3)

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/create-liquidity-and-buy-v3#ru-he-shi-yong-chuang-jian-liu-dong-xing-bing-kun-bang-mai-ru)

✅ 如何使用**创建流动性并捆绑买入？**

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/create-liquidity-and-buy-v3#id-1.-lian-jie-qian-bao)

1\. **连接钱包**

circle-info

创建前必须确保余额充足 钱包内至少有 0.03 BNB

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FIVf4IOZk63OZDweTKe3R%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=559b5673&sv=2)

*   输入用于创建/添加流动性的私钥。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FhhD5AaWP8Y7YT8jwiWOO%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=e47026b4&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/create-liquidity-and-buy-v3#id-2.-xuan-ze-jia-chi-de-liang-zhong-dai-bi)

2\. 选择加池的两种代币

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FhIKiWIV7nh7mGq6fSecB%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=132a7bb1&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/create-liquidity-and-buy-v3#id-3.-she-zhi-shou-xu-fei-ji-bie)

3.设置手续费级别

*   V3 的 LP 手续费不同于V2，不再是复利。
    
*   交易费用不同：V3有四种不同的交易费等级，最多可降低25倍交易费用；V2每一笔交易将支付0.25%手续费。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FKKMTiHm5UKZiOJREosCx%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=f7acebcc&sv=2)

circle-info

Swap v3创建流动性滑点设置默认为1%

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/create-liquidity-and-buy-v3#id-4.-she-zhi-chu-shi-jia-ge-yu-jia-ge-qu-jian)

**4.设置初始价格与价格区间**

1.区间大小決定收益高低 (LP 手续费收益、CAKE 收益皆适用)

*   越窄收益越高，无常损失越大
    
*   越宽收益越低，无常损失越小
    
*   全区间设置则类似于 V2 运作，收益将非常少
    

2.超出区间时

*   无收益
    
*   流动性仓位将变为单币
    
*   可以移除流动性并重新添加，或是等待价格重新回到区间内
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2Fw7mrJg3kJxmRGfUB1uXS%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=7cd390c8&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/create-liquidity-and-buy-v3#id-5.-tian-xie-jia-chi-shu-liang)

5.**填写加池数量**

*   输入代币的数量。
    

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FCX6ufpPmcO8mkdDQK41Z%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=a6cfd62&sv=2)

circle-info

提示：请自行计算合适的比例后再创建流动性。

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/create-liquidity-and-buy-v3#id-6.-dao-ru-mai-ru-qian-bao-si-yao)

6\. 导入买入钱包私钥

*   选择批量导入方式，可以手动粘贴多个私钥，也可以 上传包含私钥的表格文件（xlsx / xls）。
    
*   系统将自动识别每个钱包的 BNB 余额、From余额、To余额。
    

circle-exclamation

注意：单次最多支持导入 **20 个地址**。

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/create-liquidity-and-buy-v3#id-7.-she-zhi-mai-ru-can-shu)

7\. 设置买入参数

**配置方式：**

*   为每个地址设置「买入金额」 ，单个地址无上限买入金额，刷新余额查看即可
    
*   可选择刷新余额或调整买入比例
    
*   系统将展示每个地址的状态 + 操作按钮
    

circle-info

注意：买入地址的BNB余额必须大于 0.0008！

![](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/~gitbook/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fcontent.gitbook.com%2Fcontent%2FRbU9EUruu3lWQ1GJ5WVC%2Fblobs%2FylaxJvYLIARyXhf9k0Pp%2Fimage.png&width=768&dpr=3&quality=100&sign=d05af914&sv=2)

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/create-liquidity-and-buy-v3#id-8.-kai-shi-jiao-yi)

8\. 开始交易

*   检查无误后，点击“**开始交易”**按钮。
    
*   交易速度会受到链上拥堵情况影响，链上拥堵时可能交易速度较慢，还请您耐心等待。
    

### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/create-liquidity-and-buy-v3#chang-jian-wen-ti-faq)

❓常见问题 FAQ

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/create-liquidity-and-buy-v3#id-1.-wei-shen-me-chuang-jian-liu-dong-xing-bing-kun-bang-mai-ru-hui-shi-bai)

**1\.** 为什么创建流动性并捆绑买入会失败？

*   check
    
    答：请确认钱包内 BNB / WBNB 余额是否充足，以覆盖加池，捆绑买入所需资金及 Gas 费用。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/create-liquidity-and-buy-v3#id-2.-jia-chi-de-dai-bi-shu-liang-he-bi-li-you-yao-qiu-ma)

**2\.** 加池的代币数量和比例有要求吗？

*   check
    
    答：没有强制限制。你可以根据 代币经济模型、预期初始价格及市值目标 灵活调整加池数量与比例。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/create-liquidity-and-buy-v3#id-3.-yu-gu-jia-ge-hui-yi-zhi-gu-ding-ma)

**3\.** 预估价格会一直固定吗？

*   check
    
    答：不会。预估价格仅代表 上线初始价格，随着用户持续买卖，价格会实时变化，交易越活跃，价格越真实。
    

#### 

[hashtag](https://ciaotool.gitbook.io/ciaotool/evm/swap/create-liquidity-and-buy-v3#id-4.-shen-me-shi-duo-di-zhi-kun-bang-mai-ru-you-na-xie-xian-zhi)

**4\.** 什么是多地址捆绑买入？有哪些限制？

*   check
    
    答：多地址捆绑买入是指 多个钱包同时执行买入操作，提升成功率与效率。
